A Catalyst
Quest Info
Given by:
Master Varuuk
Location:
Bastion of the Order
Faction:
Order of Death's Vigil
Type:
side quest
Prerequisites:
Seals of Binding
Unlocks:
The Sacred Ashes
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Component
Catalyst is an
Act 3
side quest offered by
Master Varuuk
in the
Bastion of the Order
after completing the
Seals of Binding
quest.
The
Rite of Resurrection
planned by the Order requires a powerful energy source. Master Varuuk tells you this can be obtained by capturing the essence of a particular sorceress who is possessed by
Aetherials
.
Objectives
Collect
Aetherial Essence
(0/1)
Bring the Aetherial Essence to Master Varuuk at
Sorrow's Bastion
Guide
Master Varuuk will apply a Death's Vigil Enchantment - lasts for approximately 20 minutes and adds Cold damage to your weapon(s). The
sorceress
,
Noveria Stormfire
, can be found in
Stonerend Quarry
, situated east of the
Blood Grove
riftgate
past some Aether damaged ground. When Noveria is defeated she will drop the Aetherial Essence. Return it to Master Varuuk to complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
11000
36000
70000
Death's Vigil
Reputation
+250
Item
Random Partial Component
Master Varuuk will tell you to speak with the
Keeper of Tomes
, located in another room of the Bastion of the Order, who will offer the
The Sacred Ashes
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
The ritual to bring back a being as powerful as Malkadarr will require a potent source of arcane energies. Aetherials are the Aether itself, manifested within our realm. In a fiery conflagration at the Stonerend Quarry to the northeast of Blood Grove, near
Fort Haron
, there is a powerful Aetherial sorceress known as Noveria Stormfire. Using necromantic power bestowed upon you by the Order of Death's Vigil, capture her essence and bring it back to Master Varuuk at Sorrow's Bastion.
Objectives:
Collect Aetherial Essence
Bring the Aetherial Essence to Master Varuuk at Sorrow's Bastion
Dialogue
(Immediately upon completing the prerequisite quest)
Master Varuuk
Next, we will require a source of arcane power. I have just the thing in mind.
[Question] What's next?
Master Varuuk
The Rite of Resurrection requires powerful incantations, and an equally powerful energy source.
Without something to draw upon, the ritual would drain the participants dry and leave them as nothing but withered husks.
[Question] How can we prevent that?
Master Varuuk
Aetherials are a manifestation of the Aether itself, a source of pure arcane energy. The more powerful the Aetherial, the hotter its spirit will burn within the ritual.
To the north, near Fort Haron, there is a mine called Stonerend Quarry that's become blasted with Aetherfire, a front for the Aetherials in this region. Travel there and track down an Aetherial by the name Noveria Stormfire. She was once a great sorceress, now no more than a pawn of the Aetherials.
[Question] Continue
Master Varuuk
I will bestow a boon of the Order upon you to help counter her arcane prowess and to contain her essence. Destroy Noveria in the Order's name!
[Accepts quest] I will gather the essence.
[Refuses quest] I am not going into that hell-hole.
[Ends conversation] I will return later.
[Ends conversation] There are other matters I must attend to.
(While the quest is active)
Master Varuuk
Have you dealt with Noveria?
[Question] Where should I be looking?
(Available before defeating Noveria Stormfire)
Master Varuuk
Travel north, near Fort Haron. Look for the Stonerend Quarry; it's an area blasted with Aetherfire. Track down an Aetherial by the name Noveria Stormfire. She was once a great sorceress, now no more than a pawn of the Aetherials.
Destroy Noveria and gather her essence.
[Ends conversation] I will do so.
[Ends conversation] Not yet.
(While the quest is active)
Master Varuuk
Have you dealt with Noveria?
[Question] I have gathered her essence.
(Available after defeating Noveria Stormfire; will complete the quest)
Master Varuuk
Excellent work. I was worried that she may have been too much for you, but you have proven to be quite resourceful.
There is but one final piece we still require to bring back Malkadarr, but that is not for me to discuss. Speak with the Keeper when you are able. She will have the details.
[Question] The Keeper?
Master Varuuk
The Keeper of Tomes, guardian of the Order's knowledge. She has become the Order's de-facto leader after Uroboruuk's disappearance.
[Question] Uroboruuk is gone?
Master Varuuk
Yes, sadly our master has left us several years ago. To what end, we do not know.
He left us no information as to his departure, nor has he tried to contact anyone within the Order.
[Question] Has anyone gone after him?
Master Varuuk
Yes, quite a few. Some never returned, dead or still searching.
Before the Grim Dawn, our accomplished acolytes would set out into the world for a year in order to search for our master. It was a rite of passage of sorts.
[Ends conversation] Perhaps he will return some day.
[Ends conversation] I see.
[Ends conversation] I will speak to her.
[Ends conversation] I will.

A Cultist in the Midst
Quest Info
Given by:
-
Location:
Burrwitch Village
Faction:
Devil's Crossing
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
None
Unlocks:
A Strange Key
Rewards:
This is an
Act 1
side quest that begins when you find the
Cultist Orders
inside a building in
Burrwitch Village
.
The note provides evidence that
Direni
is an agent for the Cult of Ch'thon and was responsible for sabotaging the water pump.
Objectives
Confront Direni at Devil's Crossing.
Guide
Return to the prison and talk to Direni. You can choose to either kill him or let him live. If you decide to kill him, you will have to fight him. Speak to
Captain John Bourbon
afterwards.
If you kill Direni you will not obtain the Strange Key from him. However, it can drop from the cultists located in the
Cultist's Lair
or outside the Depraved Sanctuary, regardless of whether you let Direni live or die, and can be farmed for in these areas.
If you let Direni live, or do not trigger this quest at all, you will encounter Direni again in
Act 2
inside
Cronley's Hideout
, this time siding with Cronley's Gang, and you will have the opportunity to fight him again.
Rewards
If you kill Direni:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
500
14000
32000
Iron
1000
4000
10000
Reputation
+500 (Devil's Crossing)
Item
Blood of Ch'thon
(1)
If you let Direni live:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
300
12000
27000
Item
A Strange Key
(quest item)
Item
Direni's Directions
(note)
Upon receipt of the key from Direni, the
A Strange Key
side quest will be activated, and the quest item and note can be used to find and unlock the
Depraved Sanctuary
.
Cultist Orders Location
Quest Log
Quest log
You discovered a curious note within the ruins of Burrwitch.
Inside, you found damning evidence that Direni at Devil's Crossing has secretly been in league with the Cult of Ch'thon, and is responsible for some of the recent troubles that have befallen the refuge.
You should confront him before he has a chance to further sabotage the survivors' only sanctuary.
Objectives:
Confront Direni at Devil's Crossing.
Upon seeing the evidence, Direni has become violent and threatens the safety of the denizens of Devil's Crossing.
You must eliminate him before anyone gets hurt.
Objectives:
Kill Direni
Direni is dead and John Bourbon of Devil's Crossing will surely want to hear an explanation.
Bring the cultist note to him.
Objectives:
Bring Note to Bourbon

Act 3
side
quest
, only obtainable if you let

live in the Act 2 quest
Vengeance

Homestead

Josephine

Objectives
Speak to Isaiah in Homestead
Guide
Speaking to Isaiah will unlock his services as a
Salvage Dealer
. The prices he offers depend on whether you extorted him or not in the Act 2 quest; if you didn't, he buys and sells at much better prices.

A Familiar Witch
Quest Info
Given by:
Rallia
Location:
Coven's Refuge
Faction:
Coven of Ugdenbog
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Burn the Taken
Unlocks:
n/a
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is a small
Act 5
side
quest
, granted by
Rallia
in
Coven's Refuge
if you let her live in the
Act 3
side quest
Burn the Taken
.
Objectives
Speak to Rallia
Guide
Rallia can be found in the southeast of the Coven's Refuge. Speaking to her will both begin and complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2000
5000
10000
Coven of Ugdenbog
Reputation
+250
Quest Log
Quest log
You found Rallia at the Coven's Refuge.
She was ever grateful for your rescue back in the Blood Grove and put in a few kind words in your favor amongst the coven.

Speak to rallia

======================================================================
PAGE: A Family Crisis
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/A_Family_Crisis
======================================================================

A Family Crisis
Quest Info
Given by:
Stephen Skinner
Location:
Kymon's Retreat
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
None
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Item
This is a small
Act 2
side quest that begins when you talk to
Stephen Skinner
after encountering him at his house in the
Arkovian Foothills
.
The quest will only activate if you talk to him and offer hope and safety in
Devil's Crossing
.
If you fail to convince him, or let him burn the house down, you will receive no quest or reward. Stephen Skinner will become attackable and will drop the
Skinner's Torch
item.
Objectives
Speak to Stephen Skinner in Devil's Crossing
Guide
By following the second line of each dialogue option, Stephen Skinner will accept your offer of safety and he and his family will be teleported to Devil's Crossing. They can then be found in a room on the upper level of the prison. Speak to him and he will offer his thanks for showing him that there is still hope in the world.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
1000
11000

As the relic was clearly not within easy reach on the surface, you will have to check the cellar behind Scorv for what you need; but it is locked and Scorv likely has the key.
Slay Scorv Egdenor in Barrowhold and take his cellar key in order to access the cellar. Once inside, find the Ugdenbog Fetish and return it to Garradia at the Coven's Refuge.

4500
19000

Isaac's Spaulders
rare item in addition to other random loot. Isaac himself turns into a pile of bones which can be scavenged.

If you find him afterwards, when he offers to tell you where his stash is you can tell him you have already found it, to which Isaac laments that he should have hidden it better.
Cultis's Lair and Isaac's Stash locations
Quest Log
Quest log
You found a poor soul beyond rescue out in Wightmire. Isaac, who was in the process of being sacrificed by some cultists, was too far gone when you reached him. With his last breath, he informed you of a valuable stash he hid away out in the swamp. If you follow the river outside the cabin where you found Isaac down to the river delta, you will find his stash hidden along the shore. He said to look for a loose tree stump.
Objectives:
Find Isaac's hidden stash in Wightmire

A Strange Key
Quest Info
Given by:
N/A
Location:
-
Faction:
N/A
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
A Cultist in the Midst
Unlocks:
Depraved Sanctuary
Rewards:
XP
This is a small
Act 1
side quest that begins after finding the
A Strange Key
quest item.
The Key can be obtained in two ways.
Direni
will give it to you if you let him live in the
A Cultist in the Midst
quest, otherwise it has a chance to drop from the Cultists in the
Cultist's Lair
(and the surrounding area in the
Foggy Bank
), the
Burrwitch Outskirts
, and the
East Marsh
.
Objectives
Use the Strange Key to enter the Depraved Sanctuary
Guide
The Sanctuary is located in an area some way to the east of the Burrwitch Outskirts Riftgate;  find and destroy a section of breakable wall by the road and continue east to access the area. Unlocking the Iron Door entrance completes the quest.
Reward
How to get to Depraved Sanctuary
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
300
6500
22000
Access to the
Depraved Sanctuary
is also now allowed.
Quest Log
Quest log
You are in possession of a strange key belonging to the Cult of Ch'thon. It will likely grant access to one of their hideouts in the area.
Objectives:
Use the Strange Key to enter the Depraved Sanctuary

and/or

4000
10000

Like an itch in the back of your mind, brief visions of a stranger beckon your return to town.
It seems no matter where you go, Devil's Crossing, Homestead, Fort Ikon or even Malmouth, the same vision haunts your waking thoughts.
Perhaps you should seek out this stranger and uncover why his visage infects your mind.

======================================================================
PAGE: A Stranger in Need
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/A_Stranger_in_Need
======================================================================

A Stranger in Need
Quest Info
Given by:
Myla Finegan
Location:
Morton's Claim
Faction:
none
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
none
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP
A Stranger in Need is an
Act 3
side quest offered by
Myla Finegan
in
Morton's Claim
.
Stranded in the cultist-infested wilderness, she asks you to help clear the collapsed entrance to her cave hideout.
Objectives
Gather Dynamite (0/1)
Deliver the Dynamite to Myla Finegan in the Blood Grove
Speak to Myla Finegan in her cave in the Blood Grove
Slay Myla within the Bone Pit
Guide
Myla can be found in
Morton's Claim
, a small sub-area in the east of
The Blood Grove
. Speak to her and she will ask for some
Dynamite
. If you decide to help her, return with 1 Dynamite and give it to her. She will clear the entrance to her cave and invite you inside for a reward.
Enter her cave -
The Bone Pit
- and speak with her again. She will reveal that her request for aid was a ruse to lure you to her lair so she could drain your life. Several dialog options will then lead to her transforming into the
Wraith of Sorrows
and attacking you. Defeat the wraith to conclude the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
12000
38000
75000
Quest Log
Quest log
You encounted a lone traveler, Myla Finegan, outside of a collapsed cave in the Blood Grove. As this was her only safe haven out in the wild, she refused to go back to Homestead with you, she implored you to help her acquire some Dynamite to clear out the entrance for her so she can keep using the cave as a hideout.
Objectives:
Gather Dynamite (0/1)
Deliver the Dynamite to Myla Finegan in the Blood Grove
You provided Myla with some dynamite, which she used to clear the way into her cave. Follow her inside for your reward.
Objectives:
Speak to Myla Finegan in her cave in the Blood Grove.
Myla has betrayed you. She turned out to be a vile spirit that lures travelers into her cavern to feast on their vitality. Banish her at the Bone Pit in the Blood Grove.
Objectives:
Slay Myla within the Bone Pit

======================================================================
PAGE: A Timely Arrival
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/A_Timely_Arrival
======================================================================

A Timely Arrival
Quest Info
Given by:
Ulgrim
Location:
Deadman's Gulch
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Main quest
Prerequisites:
-
Unlocks:
The Black Legion's Finest
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 3
quest, granted by
Ulgrim
after finding him in
Deadman's Gulch
.
Background
Ulgrim is stuck out in Deadman's Gulch with several refugees, many of them injured. He has asked you to fight your way through the Mountain Deeps, a treacherous cavern system traveled by few, in order to reach the other side of the gulch and eventually Homestead itself. Once you've made your way out of the Mountain Deeps, you should follow the Prospector's Trail northwest until you reach the farmlands. There you will find Homestead, hopefully still under the control of the Black Legion.
Objectives
Travel to Homestead through the Mountain Deeps
Secure the Riftgate outside of Homestead
Return to Ulgrim and the refugees in Deadman's Gulch
Speak to Ulgrim in Homestead
Guide
The entrance to the Mountain Deeps can be found just to the west of Ulgim's location. The exit will bring you onto the Prospector's Trail and it's Rift Gate. From there the road can be followed to Homestead or you can cut northwest across the fields.
When you reach Homestead you will have to clear the riftgate area as you did in Burrwitch. The riftgate will then activate and you can return to Ulgrim. After talking to him you will automatically open a rift gate to teleport the group to safety. You can then return to Homestead see Ulgrim (located on the upper level) for the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
8000
31000
64000
Black Legion
Reputation
+500
Ulgrim will then offer
The Black Legion's Finest
quest.

======================================================================
PAGE: A Witch's Bargain
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/A_Witch's_Bargain
======================================================================

A Witch's Bargain
Quest Info
Given by:
Garradia
Location:
Coven's Refuge
Faction:
Coven of Ugdenbog
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Desperate Measures
Unlocks:
A Jewel in the Mud
Into the Jaws of Madness
The Coven's Walls
Rewards:
A Witch's Bargain
is an
Act 5
main
quest
, offered by
Garradia
after completing the
Desperate Measures
quest.
Garradia agrees to help you in your mission to reach Malmouth if you first help her retrieve the Ugdenbog Fetish, an object presently held by
Scorv Egdenor
in
Barrowholm
.
Note that this quest allows you to choose between becoming friendly or hostile with
the Barrowholm faction
.
Objectives
Find Barrowholm
Speak to Scorv Egdenor in Barrowholm
Acquire the Ugdenbog Fetish from Scorv Egdenor
Bring the Ugdenbog Fetish to Garradia at the Coven's Refuge
Guide
Barrowholm
can be found in the north of Ugdenbog, and
Scorv Egdenor
inside his house in the village. On speaking with him you will have the option of being friendly or hostile. The
A Jewel in the Mud
quest will then activate, which will play out differently depending on your choice.
If you befriend Scorv, he will ask you to run two short quests for his people before he gives the
Ugdenbog Fetish
quest item to you.
If you attack Scorv, he will turn into a Wraith. On death he will drop the
Barrowholm Cellar Key
quest item, which unlocks the
Forlorn Cellar
. This area leads to the
Den of the Wendigo
, where the Ugdenbog Fetish will drop from
Namadea, the Reaper
.
Return the quest item to Garradia to compete the quest.
Rewards
Component Reward Table
Black Tallow
Ectoplasm
Haunted Steel
Rotten Heart
Serrated Spike
Severed Claw
Vengeful Wraith
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
29000
62500
112000
Item
Random partial Component (2)
Item
Ulgrim's Keepsake
Coven of Ugdenbog
Reputation
+500
Garradia will then offer the
Into the Jaws of Madness
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Garradia of the Coven of Ugdenbog has accepted your offering and agreed to help you in finding a way through the Aetherfire. In a way, finding Ulgrim may be just the key to reaching Malmouth...through the Chthonic void.
But before she helps you, there is one more thing you must do for her: retrieve the Ugdenbog Fetish from the denizens of a nearby village called Barrowholm. Head out east from the Coven's Refuge and make your way through the bog, headed north, until you've see buildings.
Objectives:
Find Barrowholm
You have found the village that Garradia has instructed you to seek out.
The man named Scorv Egdenor seems to be in charge. Speak to him in Barrowholm about the Ugdenbog Fetish.
Objectives:
Speak to Scorv Egdenor in Barrowholm
You spoke with Scorv Egdenor in Barrowholm. Now you must acquire the Ugdenbog Fetish and return it to Garradia's at the Coven's Refuge.
Objectives:
Acquire the Ugdenbog Fetish from Scorv Egdenor
Bring the Ugdenbog Fetish to Garradia at the Coven's Refuge

PAGE: Aether Crystal (Item)
CATEGORIES: Quest Items

"A crystalline shard still lingering with Aetherial power. Can be used in the creation of arcane items."
Aether Crystals are a
Crafting
item, and can be obtained by destroying
Aether Crystals
; they will only drop if the player is no more than 5 levels above it.
They are also used in the quest
Kasparov's Experiment
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Aetherial Essence
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Aetherial_Essence
======================================================================

"The lingering spirit of an Aetherial, trapped by necrotic energies."
Aetherial Essence is a quest item looted from
Noveria Stormfire
during the
A Catalyst
quest.

======================================================================
PAGE: Allies Among the Ashes
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Allies_Among_the_Ashes
======================================================================

Allies Among the Ashes
Quest Info
Given by:
Ulgrim
Location:
Homestead
Faction:
Kymon's Chosen
Order of Death's Vigil
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
The Aetherial Farm
Unlocks:
The Prophet's Call
or
Seeking the Order
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is a small
Act 3
quest
, offered by
Ulgrim
after completing
The Aetherial Farm
.
Accepting this quest opens the eastern gate at Homestead and allows access to the
Fallow Fields
,
The Blood Grove
and other later Act 3 areas.
Background
Ulgrim says he knows of two other survivor groups operating in the area, and although they are mutual enemies, working with one or the other could prove beneficial. He has thus invited representatives from both factions to Homestead.
Objectives
Choose between
Kymon's Chosen
and the
Order of Death's Vigil
Guide
Speak with
Haruuv
of the Order of Death's Vigil and
Brother Molltair
of Kymon's Chosen to decide who you want to ally with.
The main reason for choosing one faction over the other is for the faction-specific equipment each offers.
Kymon's Chosen
offers support for Physical, Fire, and Lightning damage builds, while
Death's Vigil
equipment gives  bonuses to Cold, Vitality and Pet damage.
Each Faction will also offer its own separate quest line.
After reaching Elite or Ultimate difficulties, the player may choose to side with a different faction. This will reset the reputation for both factions on all difficulties, which means the player can only be allied to one faction at a time, regardless of the difficulty that the player starts the game on.
Note that it is not possible to side with
Kymon's Chosen
if the player has selected the
Necromancer
Mastery.
Rewards
If you side with the
Order of Death's Vigil
:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
5000
17000
33000
Reputation
-1500 Kymon's Chosen
+1500 Order of Death's Vigil
If you side with
Kymon's Chosen
:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
5000
17000
33000
Reputation
+1500 Kymon's Chosen
-1500 Order of Death's Vigil
Note that you will achieve
Despised
status with the faction you do not choose and they will become hostile toward you.
Quest Log
Quest log
Ulgrim firmly believes, even though the leadership in the Black Legion disagrees, that the local factions could be of great use in the battles ahead. He has asked representatives from the Order of Death's Vigil and Kymon's Chosen to come to Homestead and speak with you. These two factions are at odds with each other, and making them work together is virtually impossible. Ulgrim has tasked you with speaking to both emissaries in order to determine who will be of superior strategic value.
Objectives:
Choose between Kymon's Chosen and the Order of Death's Vigil

You found Ulgrim alive, though worse for wear. While he is in no state to fight chthonians, your have restored the warrior to his senses and offered him a glimmer of hope.

An Old Threat
Quest Info
Given by:
Mornay
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
Devil's Crossing
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Murderers and Worse
Unlocks:
We Need Food
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep
This is an
Act 2
quest, and offered by
Mornay
after completion of
Murderers and Worse
.
Objectives
Kill Darius Cronley (0/1)
Report to Mornay in Devil's Crossing
Guide
Darius Cronley
can be found in
Cronley's Hideout
. Battle your way through his gang members to reach him in his room at the end of the area. You can speak to him briefly before you fight and kill him. Return to Mornay for the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
10000
34000
85000
Iron
2500
9000
20000
Devil's Crossing
Reputation
+1000
Mornay will then offer you the next quest,
We Need Food
.
Quest Log
Quest log
The bandits roaming Old Arkovia are under the command of one Darius Cronley, a former inmate at the Devil's Crossing prison, before the chaos caused by the Grim Dawn provided him with an opportunity to escape. He now plans to retake the prison for himself and his convicts turned bandits, with little regard for its inhabitants.
Darius and his group must be eradicated if Devil's Crossing is to survive. You must venture out to Old Arkovia and shatter Darius' operation. The outlaws built themselves a makeshift stronghold on top of the Four Hills in Old Arkovia.
Darius is rarely seen outside the mines underneath Four Hills. Leave them crippled and broken, just as they intended for the people of Devil's Crossing.
To really cripple their operations, you should also deal with Darius' lieutenants, whom you will recognize by their odd nicknames. They will likely be atop the Four Hills.
Objectives:
Kill Darius Cronley (0/1)
The bandits are scattered and leaderless. They should no longer pose a threat for the defenders of Devil's Crossing. Report back to Mornay in Devil's Crossing.
Objectives:
Report to Mornay in Devil's Crossing

======================================================================
PAGE: And Not a Drop to Drink
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/And_Not_a_Drop_to_Drink
======================================================================

And Not a Drop to Drink
Quest Info
Given by:
Barnabas
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
None
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Helping Out
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Inventory Bag
And Not a Drop to Drink
is an
Act 1
quest offered by
Barnabas
in
Devil's Crossing
, and forms part of the
Helping Out
main quest.
Background
The defeat of
Kyzogg the Reanimator
has given
John Bourbon
enough time to plan the next major step for
his people
and
the Taken
, but while he does so, the protagonist
needs to help out
the survivors inhabiting the old prison.
One of the survivors the Taken needs to help is the settlement's handyman,
Barnabas
. He reports that the wind pump has broken down and Devil's Crossing is running low on water. Even though there's a river nearby, the water in it is too contaminated by all the corpses floating in it, so the only option is repairing the pump. To accomplish this, Barnabas needs some scrap.
Objectives
Collect Scrap for Barnabas (0/5)
Bring the Scrap to Barnabas in Devil's Crossing (0/5)
Slay Viloth the Corruptor (0/1)
Return to Barnabas
Guide
Scrap
can be found in barrels, crates and other breakable objects around
Lower Crossing
and
The Old Dump
.
Return to Barnabas with 5 pieces of scrap and he will reward you with 350 Experience and 300 Iron.
Barnabas will then say that although the pump is repaired, the water appears to be poisoned, and he suspects there is a nest of
Slith
in the cave that supplies the water. He asks you to find and kill the matriarch of this Slith pack so that the water will become drinkable again.
Enter the trapdoor in the building behind Barnabas and travel through the
Prison Dungeons
to the
Devil's Aquifer
and slay
Viloth, the Corruptor
. After that, return to Barnabas.
Rewards
Stage 1:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
350
21000
51000
Iron
300
1800
7000
Stage 2:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
500
23000
58000
Reputation
+100 (Devil's Crossing)
Item
Inventory Bag
-
-
Outcome
After the pump is repaired, and its water source purged of its poisonous inhabitants, Devil's Crossing gets a functional source of drinking water. That's one key necessity for survival which will not be a problem in the foreseeable future. And Captain Bourbon is one step closer to deciding where to strike next.
Quest Log
Quest log
Barnabas in Devil's Crossing wishes to repair the prison's water pump, but he needs Scrap.
He could melt down the few weapons the survivors have, but dying unarmed to the Dead is not any better than dying of thirst.
Find Scrap amongst the ruins of Lower Crossing and old houses in Wightmire, and bring it to Barnabas.
Objectives:
Collect Scrap for Barnabas (0/5)
Bring the Scrap to Barnabas in Devil's Crossing (0/5)
Barnabas believes that Slith have inhabited the cave Devil's Crossing pumps for water. Slith are foul beasts that secrete poisons lethal to humans.
Find and kill the matriarch of this Slith pack so that the water will become drinkable again.
Objectives:
Slay Viloth the Corruptor (0/1)
Viloth, the Slith matriarch has been slain by your hand.
Return to Barnabas in Devil's Crossing and inform him that the water will soon be safe to drink again.
Objectives:
Return to Barnabas
Gallery
Unhealthy-looking green water coming out of the pump

CATEGORIES: Quests

======================================================================

Arming the Resistance
Quest Info
Given by:
Captain Wilfor
Location:
Steelcap District
Faction:
Malmouth Resistance
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Stoking the Flames
Unlocks:
Liberate the Liberators
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 6
side
quest
, offered by
Captain Wilfor
in the
Steelcap District
Resistance Hideout as part of the
Stoking the Flames
quest.  Completing the quest will add an improved crafting area for the Steelcap District's
Quartermaster
and
Forgemaster
, in the base's north corner.
The Steelcap District and its manufacturing capabilities were once the pride of Malmouth, All is destroyed now, but some old supplies still remain. Captain Wilfor asks you to keep an eye out for any old weapon caches or arcane supplies for use by the Resistance.
Objectives
Find the Weapon Supplies
Find the Arcane Supplies
Speak with Captain Wilfor at the Resistance Hideout
Guide
The Arcane Supplies can be found west of the Hideout in the Steelcap District, the Weapon Supplies in Malmouth Harbor.
Weapon Supplies Location
Arcane Supplies  Location
Rewards
Component Reward Table
Ballistic Plating
Mark of Illusions
Oleron's Blood
Purified Salt
Reinforced Shell
Resilient Plating
Wardstone
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
17000
32000
70000
Malmouth Resistance
Reputation
+250
Item
Random Partial Component (2)
Captain Wilfor will then offer the
Liberate the Liberators
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
In order to fight back, the Aetherial needs to arm its resistance fighters. Without easy access to the forges and arcane circles, the resistance cannot simply forge new weapons. They have to rely on scavenging. Captain Wilfor's scavengers have become aware of two such stashes out among the ruins of the rowhouses in the Steelcap District. Recover these for the resistance.
Objectives:
Find the Weapon Supplies
Find the Arcane Supplies
You have recovered the supplies for the resistance and should report back to Captain Wilfor at the Resistance Hideout.
Objectives:
Speak with Captain Wilfor at the Resistance Hideout

======================================================================
PAGE: Betrayal at Fort Ikon
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Betrayal_at_Fort_Ikon
======================================================================

Betrayal at Fort Ikon
Quest Info
Given by:
Inquisitor Creed
Location:
Fort Ikon
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
A Forgotten Evil
Unlocks:
The Necropolis
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 4
main
quest
, offered by
Inquisitor Creed
after completing the
A Forgotten Evil
quest.
Fort Ikon's
Commander Lucius
has betrayed the Legion to the Aetherial forces and opened the gates to let them over-run the fort. The Fort gates were blown up to stop them and Lucius fled to the Armory when Legion reinforcements arrived. Creed asks you to help deal with him and clear the gate so that the Black Legion can advance on the Necropolis.
Objectives
Slay Commander Lucius
Recover the Heavy Explosives
Clear the Front Gates of Fort Ikon
Speak to Inquisitor Creed at Fort Ikon
Guide
Commander Lucius can be found without trouble in the
Fort Ikon Armory
. He will drop the
Legion Heavy Explosives
when defeated. Use the heavy explosives at the nearby
Detonation Site
to clear the gates.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
16000
40000
79000
Black Legion
Reputation
+500
Inquisitor Creed will then offer the
Necropolis
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
The Fort is overrun with Aetherials after the fort commander had betrayed humanity to the enemy. The Legion was able to contain the breach by collapsing the front gates, but now the way to the Necropolis is barred by several tons of stone.
It will take some heavy explosives to clear it out, and the only munitions capable of doing so are within the fort armory, where the bloated mutant form of Commander Lucius has fled following the arrival of Legion reinforcements. Put down this Aetherial-Possessed traitor and recover the Heavy Explosives.
Objectives:
Slay Commander Lucius
With the traitorous commander dealt with, you must now clear the front gates so that the Black Legion can advance on the Necropolis in force. The heavy explosives left behind by Commander Lucius should suffice.
Objectives:
Recover the Heavy Explosives
Clear the Front Gates of Fort Ikon
You have opened the way to the Necropolis. Speak to Inquisitor Creed about the next step.
Objectives:
Speak to Inquisitor Creed at Fort Ikon

Black Heart of the Void
Quest Info
Given by:
Anasteria
Location:
Fort Ikon Prison
Faction:
The Outcast
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Secrets of the Lost
Respected Faction Status
Unlocks:
The Outcast's Revenge
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
Black Heart of the Void is an
Act 4
Faction side quest offered by
Anasteria
in the
Fort Ikon Prison
, after completing the
Secrets of the Lost
quest and gaining
Respected
Faction Status.
The crafting of a
Skeleton Key
is required to complete this quest.
Objectives
Acquire the Pulsating Obsidian Shard (0/1)
Bring the Shard to Anasteria
Guide
Galar'Bargok (a Chthonic Unraveler) can be found on level 3 of the
Bastion of Chaos
(
Anarchy
), and will drop the
Pulsating Obsidian Shard
when slain. Start at the Necropolis Interior Rift and head north to find the Bastion of Chaos rift.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
18000
47000
85000
Reputation
+1500 (The Outcast)
-250 (Black Legion)
Item
Empowered
Relic Blueprint
Transcendent
Relic Blueprint
Mythic
Relic Blueprint
Anasteria will then offer her final quest, the
The Outcast's Revenge
(after reaching
Honored
status).
Quest Log
Quest log
Anasteria is interested in the powers of the void, particularly where they draw their strength. To achieve this, she requires a Pulsating Obsidian Shard from a powerful fiend. Enter the Bastion of Chaos through a rift in the Necropolis and break the chthonian seal. Once inside, slay the creature known as Galar'Bargok, collect its Obsidian Shard and deliver it to Anasteria at the Fort Ikon Prison.
Objectives:
Acquire the Pulsating Obsidian Shard (0/1)
Bring the Shard to Anasteria

Blood Harvest
Quest Info
Given by:
Captain Somer
Location:
Homestead
Faction:
Homestead
The Black Legion
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
The Aetherial Farm
Unlocks:
Reaping What You Sow
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
Blood Harvest is an
Act 3
quest offered by
Captain Somer
in
Homestead
after completion of the
The Aetherial Farm
quest.
Objectives
Find the captured farmers in the Blood Grove
Speak to Lisandra in the cage
Return to Captain Somer in Homestead
Guide
The captured farmers can be found in a large cage in the centre of the
Blood Grove
. Speak to
Lisandra Avery
and you will automatically teleport the rescued people to safety in Homestead. Return to Captain Somer for the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
12000
39000
76000
Reputation
+250 (Homestead)
+250 (Black Legion)
Captain Somer will then offer the
Reaping What You Sow
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Captain Somer's scouts have reported back from the cultist-controlled lands to the north and the situation is worse than she even imagined. The cultists are capturing farmers and using them for their blood rituals. The Black Legion cannot risk the Cult of Ch'thon bolstering their forces with Chthonic beings. You must venture out beyond Sorrow's Bastion, to the north of Homestead, and search the cultist camps. Rescue any survivors before the cultists can use them as sacrifices.
Find the captured farmers in the Blood Grove
You found a group of captives in one of the cultist camps in the Blood Grove. Speak to Lisandra and get them to safety.
Speak to Lisandra in the cage
You have rescued the farmers captured by the Cult of Ch'thon. Those that survived the blood harvest were shaken, but alive. Report back to Captain Somer in Homestead of your success.
Return to Captain Somer in Homestead

Respected Faction Status

Braving the Void is a side quest offered by
Father Kymon
in
Kymon's Sanctuary
, after completing
The Sacred Ashes
.
Background
Father Kymon has asked you to prove your worth to him by entering the chthonic void and slaying a fiend named
Bane'Gargoth
.
Objectives
Slay Bane'Gargoth (0/1)
Return to Father Kymon
Guide
The
Obsidian Throne
is accessed through a Chthonic Rift located in the
Plains of Strife
.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
15000
43000
79000
Kymon's Chosen
Reputation
+1000
Item
Random Epic Ranged Weapon
Quest Log
Quest log
There are many layers to the forsaken void, filled with ashes and misery, but one such place houses a fiend known as Bane'Gargoth. From within it's Obsidian Throne, this void spawn sends forth his armies to spread havoc and suffering upon Cairn. Prove your worth to Father Kymon. Enter the void through a rift at the Plains of Strife to the north of Fort Ikon. Brave the Forsaken Wastes and enter the Obsidian Throne. Destroy Bane'Gargoth.
Objectives:
Slay Bane'Gargoth (0/1)
You have slain Bane'Gargoth and passed Father Kymon's test. Speak to him back at Sorrow's Bastion of your success.
Objectives:
Return to Father Kymon

Burn the Taken is an Act 3 side quest offered by
Nathaniel Thorn
in the
Blood Grove
.
Nathaniel and his friends believe
Rallia
, a young witch, has been possessed by an Aetherial and are about to burn her at the stake.
Guide
There are several dialogue options, which can result in two possible outcomes: siding with Rallia and killing Nathaniel and his friends, or siding with Nathaniel and letting Rallia be burnt alive.
Rewards
If you save Rallia:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
5000
17000
33000
Item
Witch's Effigy
Quest
A Familiar Witch
If you let her burn:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
5000
17000
33000
Item
Witch's Spellblade
Quest Log
Quest log
You have encountered a group of survivors who were about to burn a young woman they suspect of being a Taken. You asked to speak with her before they do anything rash.
Objectives:
Speak to Rallia
Rallia has convinced you that she is not a Taken, but you must now convince Nathaniel to let her go.
Objectives:
Convince Nathaniel to let Rallia go
You are convinced that the men trying to burn Rallia alive are paranoid, but they refuse to listen to reason. They have become violent when you suggested letting her go. There is only one way out of this: Nathaniel and his lackeys have to die.
Objectives:
Kill Bolvia
Kill Nathaniel
Kill Vaam
You have freed Rallia from her captors, for which she is eternally grateful. Speak to her for a reward.
Objectives:
Speak to Rallia
You have burnt the Taken Rallia, as she deserved. Speak to Nathaniel about the ordeal.
Objectives:
Speak to Nathaniel

======================================================================

Byscilla's Plan
Quest Info
Given by:
Byscilla, Matron of Rifts
Location:
Vanguard of the Three
Faction:
Cult of Bysmiel
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
In Service of Bysmiel
Unlocks:
Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Item
This is an
Act 7
main
quest
, offered by
Byscilla, Matron of Rifts
after completing the
In Service of Bysmiel
quest.
Byscilla has used the items brought to her to craft  a Gargan Key. It is to be used to summon an ancient guardian that will aid in the battle against the servants of Korvaak.
Objectives
Obtain the Gargan Key
Eliminate the guardians at the Temple of Ateph
Activate the Altar of Ateph
Return to Byscilla at the Vanguard of the Three
Guide
The entrance to the
Temple of Ateph
is found north-east of the
Vanguard of the Three
. The Altar of Ateph is on the second level. Defeat the three Temple Guardian Bosses before activating the Altar - a
Spawn of Ateph
gargoyle will appear. Return to Byscilla to complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
6000
21000
52000
Cult of Bysmiel
Reputation
+250
Item
Eldritch Essence
Byscilla will then offer the
Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
quest.
The
Spawn of Ateph
can be found later in the
Remnants of Korvan City
, fighting alongside members of the Cult of Bysmiel.
Quest Log
Quest log
The materials you collected for Alain were used to create a powerful relic called the Gargan Key. Byscilla plans to use this relic to summon an ancient guardian that will serve as a weapon in the battle against the servants of Korvaak.
This summoning ritual must be performed at a place of great power, where the veil between realities is thin and ripe for rituals.
Travel North to the Ruins of Abyd and find the Temple of Ateph. Eliminate the temple guardians and then use the Gargan Key to perform the summoning ritual at the temple altar.
Objectives:
Obtain the Gargan Key
Eliminate the guardians at the Temple of Ateph
Activate the Altar of Ateph
The ritual was a success. The guardian is bound to Byscilla's will.
Report back to her at the Vanguard of the Three.
Objectives:
Return to Byscilla at the Vanguard of the Three

======================================================================
PAGE: Can't Leave Them
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Can't_Leave_Them
======================================================================

Can't Leave Them
Quest Info
Given by:
Rivia Hol
Location:
Steelcap District
Faction:
Malmouth Resistance
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Unlocks:
n/a
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Item
This is a small
Act 6
side
quest
, offered by
Rivia Hol
in the
Steelcap District
after completing the
Tip of the Spear
quest.
Rivia's mother and daughters were taken by the Aetherials when the Candle District was attacked. Captured women, both living and dead, were taken to Crown Hill, which means they are probably in the Fleshworks.
Rivia doesn't know if they are still alive or not, and asks you to find them.
Objectives
Rescue the Women in the Fleshworks
Speak to Rivia at the Resistance Hideout
Guide
Take the Malmouth Crown Hill Rift. Keep going North-East until you come across the Fleshbound Entrance. Navigate North until
Fleshworks
door is found. The women can be found, beyond saving, in the Birthing Chambers of the
Fleshworks
, towards the west side, in a gated boss area containing
Fleshweaver Krieg
. Entering the area will update the quest and the player can speak to Rivia for the reward.
Rewards
Component Reward Table
Ballistic Plating
Mark of Illusions
Oleron's Blood
Purified Salt
Reinforced Shell
Resilient Plating
Wardstone
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
10000
23000
52000
Malmouth Resistance
Reputation
+500
Item
Random Partial Component (2)
Quest Log
Quest log
Rivia at the Resistance Hideout is concerned for the people of Malmouth that never made it to the sewers in time, particularly the women. The Aetherials seem to have taken a strange interest in women in particular. She believes some of them may still survive within the Aetherial Fleshworks. She understands that what she asks of you is incredibly dangerous, but she wants to save those women and thinks you are the only one who could.
Objectives:
Rescue the Women in the Fleshworks
You discovered the fate of the women captured by the Aetherials. Report back to Rivia of their grisly fates.
Objectives:
Speak to Rivia at the Resistance Hideout

======================================================================
PAGE: Cast Off the Flesh
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Cast_Off_the_Flesh
======================================================================

Cast off the Flesh
Quest Info
Given by:
Scorv Egdenor
Location:
Barrowholm
Faction:
Barrowholm
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Feast
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Item, Optional Ravager Boss Fight
This is an
Act 5
side
quest
, offered by
Scorv Egdenor
in
Barrowholm
, after completing the
The Feast
side quest and reaching
Honored
Faction status. The Barrowholm quest line concludes here.
It is the hour of the Ravager's return, and the honor of choosing the one who shall become his flesh and blood falls to you.
Objectives
Select the Chosen who will join with
Ravager
Guide
Talk to any or all of the three chosen,
Tyvald Hallows
,
Jordyth Evelline
and his sister Aurin. All three will give reasons for why they should be selected.
Speak to Scorv Egdenor again to inform him of your choice. The NPC you selected will then be consumed by the Ravager, who will appear as an NPC.
Ravager
will offer several dialogue options, and any time thereafter, the player may also (unwisely) choose to fight him, in which case he will take one of three forms, depending on who was sacrificed during the quest. If he is killed, he will respawn on the next game session.
Ravager of Flesh
- Tyvald
Ravager of Minds
- Aurin
Ravager of Souls
- Jordyth
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
34000
56000
101000
Item
Random Epic Armor
Random legendary Armor
Barrowholm
Reputation
+2000
Quest Log
Quest log
The time has come to bring forth Ravager into the physical realm. The Great Wendigo Spirit demands a blood sacrifice and three members of the cult have offered themselves willingly. As reward for your faithful service, Scorv reluctantly asked you, at the behest of the Wendigo, to speak to all three and decide who will serve Ravager as a sacrifice. Be mindful of who you choose as their personalities and quirks may impart themselves upon the physical form of Ravager.
Objectives:
Select the Chosen who will join with Ravager

"Sigils used by the Cult of Ch'thon to bind powerful creatures to the physical realm."

Bloodsworn

It is required during the

and

quests, as well as several
Bounties
.
It is also used in crafting.

======================================================================
PAGE: Cleanse the Corruption
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Cleanse_the_Corruption
======================================================================

Cleanse the Corruption
Quest Info
Given by:
Mogdrogen
Location:
Ugdenbog
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
n/a
Unlocks:
n/a
Rewards:
XP, Item
Cleanse the Corruption
is an
Act 5
side
quest
, available on encountering
Mogdrogen
outside the entrance to the
Ancient Grove
in
Ugdenbog
.
The
Ancient Grove
has become corrupted by the
Aetherial
and
Chthonic
forces, and the taint now threatens to spill forth into the surrounding environment and wreak unimaginable destruction.
Mogdrogen
asks you to enter the
Heart of the Forest
and destroy the Grove's corrupted guardian.
Objectives
Cleanse the Ancient Grove
Speak to Mogdrogen in Ugdenbog
Guide
The target of the quest is
Gargabol, Heart of the Wild
, the Boss creature at the end of the
Ancient Grove
.
Mogdrogen
will give the player a
Skeleton Key
as a quest progress reward to enter the Roguelike section. After defeating
Garbagol
, return to
Mogdrogen
in
Ugdenbog
to receive the final reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
45000
80000
150000
Item
Random Epic Weapon
Random Legendary Weapon
Quest Log
Quest log
Mogdrogen's Avatar has shown himself before you in Ugdenbog. As the god of beasts is occupied elsewhere, he has asked you to assist him in cleansing the Ancient Grove of Ugdenbog of the vile corruption growing within it.
Only when the Heart of the Forest has been purged will the grove be allowed to cleanse itself of the Aetherial and Ch'thonic taint.
This task will require a Skeleton Key.
Objectives:
Cleanse the Ancient Grove
You have cleansed the corruption within the heart of the Ancient Grove.
Return to Mogdrogen in Ugdenbog and report on your success.
Objectives:
Speak to Mogdrogen in Ugdenbog

======================================================================
PAGE: Clearing the Way
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Clearing_the_Way
======================================================================

Clearing the Way
Quest Info
Given by:
Bernard
Location:
Arkovian Foothills
Faction:
Rovers
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
none
Unlocks:
nothing
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep, Inventory Bag
This is an
Act 2
quest offered by
Bernard
at the Rover Camp in the
Arkovian Foothills
.
Background
The bandits in the area have set up a barricade along the road to trap travelers, and the rovers are unable to continue on their way. Bernard will offer you some coin if you can recover some dynamite from the nearby mine and destroy the barricade.
Objectives
Collect Dynamite (0/1)
Destroy the Bandit Barricade blocking the road
Report back to Bernard at the Rover Camp in the Arkovian Foothills.
Guide
The
Dynamite
can be found in the nearby
Staunton Mine
; The entrance is just over the bridge on the western edge of the Rover camp. The quest item will be in plain sight in one of the areas inside the mine.
Exit Staunton Mine and head north to the barricade. Place the Dynamite in the Detonation Site near the base of the Barricade to destroy it, then return to Bernard for the reward.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
3000
24000
55000
Iron
5000
2500
8000
Rovers
Reputation
+250
Item
Inventory Bag
Quest Log
Quest log
You encountered a Rover camp along the road in the Arkovian Foothills, east of the Staunton Mine. Their leader, Bernard, has asked you to recover some dynamite from the nearby Staunton Mine so that you can clear the nearby road of a blockade the bandits had created in order to stop travelers. When you have enough dynamite, you should head to the barricade and destroy it.
Objectives:
Collect Dynamite (0/1)
Destroy the Bandit Barricade blocking the road
You destroyed the barricade blocking the road in the Arkovian Foothills. Bernard from the nearby Rover camp will be happy to hear the news. Report back to him.
Objectives:
Return to Bernard at the Rover Camp in the Arkovian Foothills

The Shattered Realm offers infinite promise, but many dangers await. You will not simply accept partial victory, this broken reality, and all of its power, is yours for the taking.

======================================================================
PAGE: Crate's Secret Quest
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Crate's_Secret_Quest
======================================================================

Crate's Secret Quest
Quest Info
Given by:
n/a
Location:
n/a
Faction:
n/a
Type:
n/a
Prerequisites:
n/a
Unlocks:
Edge of Reality
Rewards:
n/a
Crate's Secret Quest
is an Easter Egg in the
Forgotten Gods
Expansion. Like
Daila's Secret Quest
in the base game and
Lokarr's Secret Quest
in the
Ashes of Malmouth
, it can only be accessed on Ultimate
Difficulty
, with no quest text and only cryptic clues given for each step. This quest eventually leads the player to a series of hidden levels and the secret super boss
Crate of Entertainment
.
Guide
Complete access to all of the locations in Crate's Secret Quest requires:
6 seals to be destroyed
locating the portal to the
Sanctum of the Chosen
the player to have
Chillheart
in their inventory
The Seals
The 6 seals appear as
Unassuming Crates
, located across various parts of Cairn. The seals must be destroyed in the following order.
The quest begins upon entering the
Forgotten Cellar
. The entrance to it is in the
Conclave of the Three
, hidden behind the
Cult of Dreeg
faction vendor. Inside the cellar is an Unassuming Crate. Destroying the crate will cause the
Spirit of Crate
NPC to appear. The Spirit will say that the Unassuming Crate was the first of six seals to be broken, but refuses to reveal the location of the others or their purpose, leaving the player to search for them on their own.
The second Unassuming Crate is located in the northern portion of the
Hidden Refuge
, a secret area adjacent the
Temple City of Osyr
.
The third Unassuming Crate is found in
Sunbane Oasis
, concealed under some trees in a secret area, which itself is accessed by a secret path under the broken bridge.
The fourth Unassuming Crate is in the
Ruins of Abyd
, in another secret area behind a breakable wall, just north of the
Vanguard of the Three
.
The fifth Unassuming Crate is found in the
Valley of the Chosen
, behind a breakable wall to the east of the entrance to the
Tomb of Nephos
.
The sixth and final Unassuming Crate is found in a secret area on the second floor of the
Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
West Side (2 breakable walls).
Chillheart
Chillheart
is a Unique Dagger and counterpart to
Stormheart
and
Blazeheart
. The sword will appear in the
Vanguard of the Three
after the player has stood in the green ritual circle near the
Vanguard Ritualists
for 15 seconds.
Bonebleach Basin
Once all 6 Unassuming Crate seals are broken, the player can travel to the
Cairan Docks
, to an area where the
Crate Entertainment
logo can be found on the ground. Walking over the logo will destroy a section of the nearby wall, allowing the player to enter
Bonebleach Basin
. The persistent sandstorm in the basin will cause damage over time to the player, which can be avoided by taking shelter behind large rock formations or leeching life from the
Bonebleach Dromedary
creatures that inhabit the area.
At the northern end of Bonebleach Basin, on the right, is a
Desert Altar
. The altar can only be activated if the player has the
Chillheart
sword in their possession. Activating the Altar opens a portal to the
Sanctum of the Chosen
.
Inside the Sanctum of the Chosen are five different-colored levers that correspond to the colors used for different item tiers. Activating the levers in increasing item rarity order (white, yellow, green, blue, purple) opens a door to the
Edge of Reality
.
Edge of Reality
The Edge of Reality has three sections.
The first section is a desert area populated by
Oversized Maggots
. These Oversized Maggots are initially passive and will not react to the player moving near them. Once they are attacked, however, they will become aggressive and retaliate using melee attacks that can one-shot most characters. Hidden among the Oversized Maggots is a single
Perfectly Usual Oversized Maggot
, which is grayer in color. Killing this maggot will open an Eldritch Rift in the tower at the far end of the section which leads to the next section.
The second section is a temple ruined by volcanic activity. Most of the ground is magma rock that will damage the player over time. In addition, from the section onwards, the player is unable to leave using their personal rift. Another Eldritch Rift can be located near the end of the section, which takes the player to the third section.
The third and final section is an Eldritch remake of
Devil's Crossing
.
Crate of Entertainment
is found in the central area of the prison compound, flanked by two locked Crate Collections chests. Defeating Crate of Entertainment will unlock both chests and open an Eldritch Rift at his starting location that sends the player back to the
Vanguard of the Three
. Upon his defeat, Crate of Entertainment will also always drop a
Mildly Amusing Box
and may drop an additional
Wilhelm's Wondrous Wargem
at a 25% chance.

======================================================================
PAGE: Cronley's Secret
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Cronley's_Secret
======================================================================

Cronley's Secret
Quest Info
Given by:
no-one
Location:
Cronley's Hideout
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
An Old Threat
Unlocks:
Nothing
Rewards:
XP,
Aether Cluster
Cronley's Secret is a small
Act 2
quest available after you have killed
Darius Cronley
in his hideout.
After killing him, a secret room can be found behind the bed in his boss-room. The room contains a laboratory and an Aether Cluster which can be interacted with.
Guide
The quest dialogue presents three possible actions:
Destroy the Laboratory and the Crystal.
Destroy the Laboratory and keep some of the Crystal for yourself.
Leave the Crystal alone.
There is little difference in choosing one option over another.
Rewards
Destroy the Crystal:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2500
8000
17500
Keep some of the Crystal:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2500
8000
17500
Item
Aether Cluster

======================================================================
PAGE: Culling the Swarm
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Culling_the_Swarm
======================================================================

Culling the Swarm
Quest Info
Given by:
Douglass Sullivan Oldbarrow
Location:
Homestead
Faction:
Homestead
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Infested Fields
Unlocks:
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep, Inventory Bag
This is an
Act 3
main
quest
, offered by Douglass after completing
Infested Fields
.
Background
Douglass explains that the Dermapteran hives are cyclical in nature, and every seven years they birth a new queen who quickly proliferates their numbers. Prior to the Grim Dawn the farmers of Homestead would band together to destroy the Dermapteran queen to stop the reproductive cycle, but of late they have been allowed to thrive.
The Queen must be destroyed or the insects will soon run out of food and attack Homestead.
Objectives
Collect a Pheromone Gland from Grand Vizier Lozakal
Collect a Pheromone Gland from Grand Vizier Inixil
Access the Queen's Lair
Slay Swarm Queen Ravna
Return to Douglass in Homestead
Guide
Locate and enter the
Royal Hive
; the Cave Entrance spawns randomly in the upper northern part of the Rotting Croplands and you may need to explore several fields.
You will then need to kill two Boss creatures,
Grand Vizier Lozakal
and
Grand Vizier Inixil
, both located randomly within the Royal Hive, and collect their pheromone glands. These two quest items are required to unseal the Entrance to the
Hive Queen's Lair
. Once inside the lair it is best to skirt the left and right sides to clear out the Dermapteran packs before taking on
Swarm Queen Ravna
. After killing her report back to Douglass.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
11000
38000
73000
Iron
2000
10000
20000
Homestead
Reputation
+1000
Item
Inventory Bag
Quest Log
Quest log
Douglass was impressed with how you handled the Dermapterans out in the Rotting Croplands. He is confident in your abilities and believes you can put a stop to the Dermapterans for good. Dermapteran hives are cyclical. Every seven years or so, they birth a new queen, which promptly proliferates their numbers. In the past, the farmers would rally and exterminate the queen while she was still young. But after the Grim Dawn, the Dermapterans were allowed to thrive, and now their queen is a massive creature that spawns new Dermapterans by the dozen every day.
She has to be destroyed, otherwise the Dermapterans will eventually run out of food and attack Homestead in force. The queen is guarded by two of her Grand Viziers. You will not be able to even enter her chamber without their pheromone glands. Seek out the Royal Hive somewhere out in the Rotting Croplands, to the west of Homestead and open the queen's chamber.
Objectives:
Collect a Pheromone Gland from Grand Vizier Lozakal
Collect a Pheromone Gland from Grand Vizier Inixil
Access the Queen's Lair
You have opened the way into the Dermapteran Queen's lair. It is now time to destroy her and halt the Dermapteran reproductive cycle, giving the farmers of Homestead a much needed reprieve.
Objectives:
Slay Swarm Queen Ravna
You have slain the Dermapteran Queen. Return to Douglass in Homestead with the good news.
Objectives:
Return to Douglass in Homestead

======================================================================
PAGE: Cult Activity
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Cult_Activity
======================================================================

Cult Activity
Quest Info
Given by:
Captain Reave
Location:
Fort Ikon
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Aetherial Witch
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP,Iron,  Reputation
This is an
Act 4
side quest offered by
Captain Reave
after completing the
The Aetherial Witch
side quest and killing
Anasteria
.
Captain Reave asks you to deal with a group of Chthonic cultist reported to be occupying the ancient Tomb of Korvaak.
Objectives
Slay Cultist Priests at the Tomb of Korvaak (0/5)
Return to Captain Reave
Guide
The
Tomb of Korvaak
is located a short way south-east of the
Asterkarn Valley
Rift. Enter and kill the five Cultist Priests.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
7500
18000
44000
Iron
1750
8750
17500
Black Legion
Reputation
+250
Quest Log
Quest log
Captain Reave of the Black Legion is uncomfortable with the cult activity going on around an old tomb in the Asterkarn Mountains. Anything that attracts that much cult activity cannot be good for the Legion. He has tasked you with disrupting whatever the cult is up to. Travel to this Tomb of Korvaak in the Asterkarn Mountains and slay any Bloodsworn Priests and Bloodsworn Doomsayers you encounter. The tomb is somewhere in the wilderness, away from the road.
Objectives:
Slay Cultist Priests at the Tomb of Korvaak
You have interrupted the cult's activities in the Tomb of Korvaak and should report back to Captain Reave at Fort Ikon.
Objectives:
Return to Captain Reave

======================================================================
PAGE: Cultist Orders
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Cultist_Orders
======================================================================

The Cultist Orders is a quest note found on a Dusty Lectern inside a house in
Burrwitch Village
. Finding this item activates the
A Cultist in the Midst
quest.
The text of the note is as follows:
"Brothers of the Blood,
The Aetherial presence in Burrwitch grows stronger with each passing day. We are shifting our operations beyond the city limits where we may proceed with our plans undisturbed. Our focus now turns upon Devil's Crossing, where our newest agent, Direni, has successfully sabotaged their water pump. Soon that irksome group will be forced to flee their sanctuary, and then they shall be at our mercy.
Ready yourselves, brothers. Soon we shall drink of their blood!
Salazar, Blade of Ch'thon"

======================================================================
PAGE: Daila's Diary
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Daila's_Diary
======================================================================

"Property of Daila Thornsbury."
Daila's Diary is an Act 3 quest item located on a Lectern in a house in
Thornsbury Farm
. Finding it activates the
Missing Diary
quest.

======================================================================
PAGE: Daila's Secret Quest
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Daila's_Secret_Quest
======================================================================

Daila's Secret Quest
Quest Info
Given by:
n/a
Location:
n/a
Faction:
n/a
Type:
n/a
Prerequisites:
Stormheart
Unlocks:
Edge of Reality
Rewards:
n/a
Daila's Secret Quest
is available on Ultimate  difficulty only. Although not technically a quest, as no quest log objectives or rewards are given to the player, it expands upon the lore relating to
Daila Thornsbury
and her brother Dravis, and  unlocks the secret
Edge of Reality
level.
Guide
To complete the quest, the player must find several items. Each can only be found after acquiring the one before, and the item from each step must remain in your inventory.
1). The Legendary Dagger
Stormheart
, located within a breakable urn inside the
Tomb of Korvaak
.
WARNING: Dont sell the stormheart, or you wont progress in the quest.
2).
Dravis' Letter to Daila - First Entry
. Following the hint given in the
Excerpt from Daila's Diary
note, the player must find the
Weeping Oak
, a large tree full of hanged corpses located in
The Blood Grove
.  At the base of the tree is a small plume of blue smoke; moving close enough will add the quest item to the inventory, and the following text will appear on-screen:
You feel a chilling breeze, but there is no wind...
The note text provides a clue to the location of the Second Entry.
3).
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Second Entry
is found in
Anguish
, the fifth level of the
Steps of Torment
, in a secret room in the south corner. A pile of skulls with a plume of blue smoke can be seen inside; moving close enough will add the quest item to the inventory, and the following text will appear on-screen:
A sense of dread overwhelms you...
The note text provides a clue to the location of the Third Entry.
4).
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Third Entry
is found in
The Forsaken Wastes
, inside a ruined house to the north of the area. A small plume of blue smoke can be seen inside; moving close enough will add the quest item to the inventory, and the following text will appear on-screen:
This place feels strange...
The note text provides a clue to finding the Final Entry.
With all four of the above items in the player's inventory, a
Bound Spirit
will spawn in the hidden area of the
Gates of Necropolis
located to the northeast from the
riftgate
, beyond some
Aether Crystals
and a wagon.
Giving the Bound Spirit a
Salt Bag
amulet
will cause a Chthonic Rift to open, leading to the
Sanctum of the Immortal
. There the player will find
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Final Entry
, and can activate a
Loose Torch
which opens a Chthonic Rift to the
Edge of Reality
.
Gallery
Stormheart Location
First Entry Location
Second Entry Location
Third Entry Location
Bound Spirit Location

======================================================================
PAGE: Dangerous Curiosity
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Dangerous_Curiosity
======================================================================

Dangerous Curiosity
Quest Info
Given by:
Kasparov
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
Devil's Crossing
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Inventor's Apprentice
Unlocks:
Dismantling
Rewards:
XP, Rep
This is a small side quest offered by
Kasparov
after completing
The Inventor's Apprentice
, repairing the bridge connecting
Devil's Crossing
to the
Arkovian Foothills
and gaining
Respected
faction status with
Devil's Crossing
. The quest is offered after repairing the bridge to the
Arkovian Foothills
in Elite and Ultimate Difficulties - the Act 1 quest line need not be completed to do so.
Completing this quest unlocks the
Inventor's
Dismantling ability.
Objectives
Collect Dynamite (0/3)
Bring the Dynamite to Kasparov in Devil's Crossing
Guide
The
Dynamite
can be found in mines and around Bandit camps.
Staunton Mine
and
Hanneffy Mine
each have at least one dynamite, and it can also be found around the
Four Hills
camps.
"Moneybags" Martin
in
Cronley's Hideout
also drops dynamite.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2000
13000
35000
Quest Log
Quest log
Kasparov has a hypothesis that items of great magical power can be broken down into their base components if enough energy is supplied into the system. To prove him right, you are to collect Dynamite from the mines scattered around the Arkovian Foothills and Old Arkovia. Then the experiment shall begin.
Objectives:
Collect Dynamite (0/3)
Bring the Dynamite to Kasparov in Devil's Crossing

Deeper in Debt
Quest Info
Given by:
Riggs
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
N/A
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Now You Owe Me
The Forgotten God
Unlocks:
Paying Debts
Rewards:
XP, Item
Deeper in Debt a small
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Riggs
after completing
Now You Owe Me
and
The Forgotten God
, as well as being level 50 or over.
Riggs has something new for you if you are prepared to be further in his debt.
Objectives
Make another deal with Riggs
Guide
The quest can be refused or accepted and completed in the dialogue options.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
100
5500
14000
Item
Random Epic Item
Random Legendary Item
Quest Log
Quest log
You spoke with Riggs again.
Once more, he gave you another of his wares, asking only that you be in his debt.
No doubt he will come to collect on this debt eventually.
Objectives:
Make another deal with Riggs

======================================================================
PAGE: Descent into Torment
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Descent_into_Torment
======================================================================

Descent into Torment
Quest Info
Given by:
Kalderos
Location:
Broken Hills
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Old Scars
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
Xp, Skeleton Key, Blueprint
This is an
Act 2
side quest offered by
Kalderos
outside the entrance of the
Steps of Torment
in the
Broken Hills
.
Objectives
Slay Grand Priest Zarthuzellan (0/1)
Speak to Kalderos in the Steps of Torment
Guide
Grand Priest Zarthuzellan
is located in his room toward the north-east end of
Misery
, the third level of the Steps of Torment. The portcullis at the bridge to his room will lock behind you until he is defeated.
Kalderos will be waiting in the room by the Gates of Anguish. Speak to him to receive your reward.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
7500
29000
76000
Item
Skeleton Key
Item
Blueprint: Skeleton Key
The Skeleton Key will allow you to unlock the Gates of Anguish, which lead to the fourth and fifth levels of the Steps of Torment (
Suffering
and
Anguish
). On unlocking the door the key will be used up and another must be crafted with the blueprint to enter again.
Quest Log
Quest log
Kalderos has instructed you to descend into the Steps of Torment, the ruined remnants of Arkovia's dark history. Once inside, you must seek out the Grand Priest Zarthuzellan, who resides on the third floor. When you have destroyed the corrupted priest, the way will be clear to the doors sealing off the deepest pits of the Steps of Torment. The Steps of Torment are located deep within the Broken Hills.
Objectives:
Slay Grand Priest Zarthuzellan
You have destroyed the undead remains of Grand Priest Zarthuzellan and earned the right to your reward. Speak with the spirit of Kalderos, who is awaiting you within Zarthuzellan's chamber in the Steps of Torment, on the third floor.
Objectives:
Speak to Kalderos in the Steps of Torment
Gallery
The Steps of Torment (Level #1)
The Steps of Torment Level #2
The Steps of Torment Level #3
The Steps of Torment Level #3

"The corrupted ashes of Archon Barthollem, devout follower of a forgotten god."
The Desecrated Ashes of Empyrion is a quest item used in
The Sacred Ashes (Death's Vigil)
. It drops from
Archon Barthollem
in the second level of the
Tomb of Archon Barthollem
.

Desperate Measures
Quest Info
Given by:
Inquisitor Creed
Location:
Fort Ikon
Faction:
Coven of Ugdenbog
Type:
Main
Prerequisites:
The Bane of Cairn
Unlocks:
A Witch's Bargain
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Item
This is an
Act 5
main
quest
. It is offered by
Inquisitor Creed
after completing
Act 4
and beginning the
Ashes of Malmouth
Expansion content.
Objectives
Acquire Creed's Pendant from Inquisitor Creed
Destroy the Aetherial Barrier leading north out of the Burrwitch Estates
Slay Carraxus Foul and take its heart.
Acquire Ulgrim's Keepsake from Inquisitor Creed
Bring the Heart and Ulgrim's Keepsake to Garradia in the Coven of Ugdenbog.
Guide
Creed will give two quest items on acceptance of the quest:
Creed's Pendant
and
Ulgrim's Keepsake
. The first is used to destroy the blockage in the
Burrwitch Estates
,  which opens the road to
Gloomwald
.
the
Den of Carraxus
is located at the northeast corner of Gloomwald, behind a building. Take the Gloomwald Crossing riftgate, then head east a bit and look for the cave. Defeat
Carraxus Foul
and collect his Heart. Continue to the
Coven's Refuge
and give the heart and Ulgrim's Keepsake to
Garradia
.
Rewards
Garradia will grant the reward then offer the next quest,
A Witch's Bargain
.
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
25000
55000
102000
Item
Tonic of Clarity
Reputation
+500 (Coven of Ugdenbog)
Quest Log
Quest log
Inquisitor Creed was unable to determine Ulgrim's location, but he's not ready to give up on his friend just yet. A desperate plea from Devil's Crossing demands his immediate attention and the rising Aetherial threat from the taken city of Malmouth presents a new challenge for the Black Legion.
However, Creed believes both goals can be equally served by reaching out to the coven of witches hiding out on the edges of Ugdenbog, the only route by land to Malmouth.
Creed has presented you with his pendant, one of his hidden tricks. With it, you should be able to penetrate the Aetherial flames barring the way north out of the Burrwitch Estates and into Gloomwald, where the coven was known to be hiding.
Objectives:
Acquire Creed's Pendant from Inquisitor Creed
Destroy the Aetherial Barrier leading north out of the Burrwitch Estates
With the barrier destroyed, you can now enter Gloomwald and seek out the Coven of Ugdenbog. But the witches are not likely to simply welcome you with open arms, much less help you in your predicament. In order to appease them, Inquisitor Creed recommended hunting down Carraxus Foul, the scourge of Ugdenbog, and bringing its heart to Garradia, one of the witches in the coven.
Carraxus Foul has been a menace in those parts for years, and its heart is sure to serve some questionable purpose in a witch's ritual. But desperate times demand that such acts be overlooked. Follow the road through Gloomwald and look for a cave near the waterfront. Carraxus Foul had likely turned it into a den.
Once you have the heart, bring it to the Coven's Refuge, somewhere on the border between Gloomwald and Ugdenbog. Present it to the witches along with Ulgrim's Keepsake.
Objectives:
Slay Carraxus Foul and take its heart.
Acquire Ulgrim's Keepsake from Inquisitor Creed
Bring the Heart and Ulgrim's Keepsake to Garradia in the Coven of Ugdenbog.

Devil's Crossing Needs You
Quest Info
Given by:
n/a
Location:
n/a
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Main
Prerequisites:
The Bane of Cairn
Unlocks:
Desperate Measures
Rewards:
XP
Devil's Crossing Needs You
is an
Act 5
main
quest
, available to characters that have finished the base game, without completing the
Act 1
quest line, prior to installing the
Ashes of Malmouth
Expansion. It is granted automatically on commencing the Expansion to direct the player to finish the Act 1 main quest line.
Objectives
Assist Devil's Crossing
Speak to Inquisitor Creed at Fort Ikon
Guide
The player must return to
Devil's Crossing
to complete the main quest line and Kill
Warden Krieg
before unlocking the Expansion content.
Speaking with
Inquisitor Creed
will provide several dialogue options which will initiate the Expansion cut-scene. Creed will then offer the
Desperate Measures
quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
5000
12000
18000
Quest Log
Quest log
Inquisitor Creed is seeking ways to rescue Ulgrim from the jaws of the void. In the meantime, there are unsettled matters in Devil's Crossing that require your attention.
Assist Captain Bourbon in any way you can.
Objectives:
Assist Devil's Crossing
You have assisted Devil's Crossing and dealt with the cruel Warden Krieg.
Return to Inquisitor Creed in Fort Ikon to discuss Ulgrim's situation.
Objectives:
Speak to Inquisitor Creed at Fort Ikon
