======================================================================
PAGE: Disarming the Enemy
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Disarming_the_Enemy
======================================================================

Disarming the Enemy
Quest Info
Given by:
Quade
Location:
Old Arkovia
Faction:
Rovers
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Warrior Among Rovers
Unlocks:
A Life for an Eye
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep
This
Act 2
quest is offered by
Quade
after completing
The Warrior Among Rovers
quest.
Objectives
Destroy bandit Forges around Four Hills (0/3)
Return to Quade at the Rover Camp in Old Arkovia
Guide
There are several entrances into the outlaw strongholds., two just north of the rover camp and one to the north west just past New Harbor. The forges are all inside outlaw camps atop each of the Four Hills, which are all connected by bridges. Simply follow the bridges from camp to camp to find the forges. There are actually 5 to find but you only need to destroy 3 to finish this quest.
This quest can also be completed retroactively if at least 3 Forges are destroyed during a single game session, prior to accepting the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
3500
26000
56000
Iron
500
3000
8700
Rovers
Reputation
+500
Quade will then offer you another quest,
A Life for an Eye
.
Quest Log
Quest log
Quade of the Rovers in Old Arkovia is tired of the lives lost to the pacifist views of his people. He, along with a group of like-minded rovers, parted ways with his elders in order to fight back against the outlaw threat. He offered you some iron bits in exchange for your assistance. The first step, he explained, is to destroy the weapons forges the bandits had set up in their strongholds atop the Four Hills.
Objectives:
Destroy bandit Forges around Four Hills
You have destroyed the forges in the outlaw camps, effectively crippling their ability to create new weapons. Return to Quade at the Rover camp in Old Arkovia with the news.
Objectives:
Return to Quade at the Rover Camp in Old Arkovia

======================================================================
PAGE: Dravis' Letter
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Dravis'_Letter
======================================================================

Dravis' Letter
is a quest item found on a Lectern in the
Burning Cellar
within
Malmouth Outskirts
. The item is required for the
A Sister's Love
quest.
Dear Sister,
again I find myself at a loss of words.
Why is it that you defy your very blood?
Why do you forsake your brother when I am so close to the truth?
But no matter, I shall tear it out of our father's dying breath with or without you.
If you are reading this, then you are again too late,
for I have ventured where the dead dare not,
where the blood of the living is joined with the master.
The time to join me has passed, Daila.
Turn back, for where I go, you cannot follow...
Dravis

======================================================================
PAGE: Dravis' Letter to Daila - First Entry
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Dravis'_Letter_to_Daila_-_First_Entry
======================================================================

Dravis' Letter to Daila - First Entry is a quest item that can be found in the
Blood Grove
as part of
Daila's Secret Quest
on Ultimate Difficulty only.
To acquire the letter, the player must first have equipped, or in their inventory, the Legendary Dagger
Stormheart
. The letter can then be found in the
Blood Grove
under the
Weeping Oak,
a large tree full of hanged corpses.  At the base of the tree is a small plume of blue smoke; moving close enough will add the quest item to the inventory, and the following text will appear on-screen:
You feel a chilling breeze, but there is no wind...
The note text provides a clue to the location of the
Second Entry
.
Dearest sister,
I am confident that this letter will find its way to you. You cannot resist returning to this place; I know that the memories of that night still conjure nightmares in your sleep. The face you saw, that is the price one pays for learning the truth. Truth which you deny!
Do you remember how we used to play around the old ruins as children? Father always told us not to, that we would be swept away by the harpies that fill the sky in the twilight hours. But what if he was not just trying to protect us? Perhaps there were ulterior motives to keeping us away from the old places of the world? What if, should we venture inside, we would learn more about his past than he wished for us to know?
I have done what you could not, Daila. I have defied our father and entered the depths of Anguish. It is there that my eyes were truly opened. If you are wise, you will do as I have...
Dravis
Weeping Oak Location
See also:
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Second Entry
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Third Entry
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Final Entry

======================================================================
PAGE: Dravis' Letter to Daila - Second Entry
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Dravis'_Letter_to_Daila_-_Second_Entry
======================================================================

Dravis' Letter to Daila - Second Entry is a quest item that can be found in
Anguish
(Level 5 of the
The Steps of Torment
) on Ultimate Difficulty only.
To acquire the letter, the player must first have equipped, or in their inventory, the Legendary Dagger
Stormheart
, and the
First Entry
.
The letter can then be found in a secret room in the bottom corner of
Anguish
. A pile of skulls with a plume of blue smoke can be seen inside; moving close enough will add the quest item to the inventory, and the following text will appear on-screen:
A sense of dread overwhelms you...
The note text provides a clue to the location of the
Third Entry
.
by now you must have seen the haunting echoes from Arkovia's past. Have you never wondered how all this came to be? How Arkovia really fell? Father called it greed, but greed alone cannot condemn a man to such torment. Nay, powerful sorcery was at play here.
I could feel it in very walls. The stones screamed with unfettered rage, rage towards...me. Do the dead despise the living so? Do they yearn after what was stolen from them? To exist in such a state of endless limbo would drive any soul mad, but I do not believe that madness is what inspired this response. There was something familiar within these stones.
I have to learn more. So I intend to visit the one place I know our father had been: our childhood home. Of course, this presents me with a bit of a challenge, as you well know why, for our home was consumed by the Chthonian rifts not long ago. But such trivialities will not stop me from discovering the answers I seek...
Dravis
Letter Location
See also:
Dravis' Letter to Daila - First Entry
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Third Entry
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Final Entry

======================================================================
PAGE: Dravis' Letter to Daila - Third Entry
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Dravis'_Letter_to_Daila_-_Third_Entry
======================================================================

Dravis' Letter to Daila - Third Entry is a quest item that can be found in
The Forsaken Wastes
on Ultimate Difficulty only.
To acquire the letter, the player must first have equipped, or in their inventory, the Legendary Dagger
Stormheart
, as well as the
First
and
Second Entry
.
The letter can then be found in
The Forsaken Wastes
, inside a ruined house to the north of the area. A small plume of blue smoke can be seen inside; moving close enough will add the quest item to the inventory, and the following text will appear on-screen:
This place feels strange...
The note text provides a clue to finding the
Final Entry
.
The pieces are finally falling into place. The answers were under our very noses all along. The rift violently consumed our home, but in doing so it revealed what was hidden from us underneath the floorboards. Our father kept a journal, a seemingly innocuous object, yet the pages were sealed from me with a protective rune.
Carelessly, or perhaps arrogantly, I dispelled the seal. The resulting flames consumed the book and marked my face with embers that refuse to extinguish. It is agonizing, but I will endure. Despite our father's efforts, I was able to rescue some pages from the inferno. He told us that our mother died in childbirth, that much is true, but what you do not know is that we were not the first. There were other women, and other children, but the dates...they did not make any sense. It was not until I turned to the final page that the answer became clear.
I must make haste to the City of the Dead. Therein lies our final clue...
Dravis
Letter Location
See also:
Dravis' Letter to Daila - First Entry
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Second Entry
Dravis' Letter to Daila - Final Entry

, offered by

after completing the the

is found in the
Sanctuary of Horran
, west of the
Sunbane Oasis
rift.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
4000
18000
45000
Cult of Dreeg
Reputation
+250
Item
Tonic of Clarity
Quest Log
Quest log
The vision of Dreeg can be as much a curse as it is a gift. With the followers of the Forgotten God ravaging the land some loyal worshipers of Dreeg have succumb to their gift, driven mad by visions of a hopeless fate.
Some turn against their faith, gathering the weak at their side, claiming they alone see the way forward.
This dissension will not be tolerated. Go to the Sanctuary of Horran in the Sunbane Oasis, find the one they call Navan the Usurper and put an end to her madness.
Objectives:
Slay Navan the Usurper
Navan the Usurper lies dead. Her madness will no longer poison the minds of weak.
Return to Kira at Conclave of the Three and report on your success.
Objectives:
Return to Kira at the Conclave of the Three

======================================================================
PAGE: Dynamite
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Dynamite
======================================================================

“A crude explosive once fielded by demolitionists to counter the devastating powers of magic users.”
Dynamite is an item primarily used at
Detonation Sites
to open up various areas in the game world. It is also used to open
Treasure Trove
chests and to
Dismantle
items at the
Inventor
.
Dynamite is required for the quest
Dangerous Curiosity
as well as
The Hidden Path
.
Locations
Dynamite can be found in the following locations:
Staunton Mine
(x1)
Hanneffy Mine
(x1)
Four Hills
(x1)
Cronley's Hideout
(x1-2)
Tyrant's Hold
(x2)
The Conflagration
(x1)
The Immolation
(x2)
Stonerend Quarry
(x2)
Fort Haron
(x2)
Fort Ikon Armory
(x1)
Shaded Basin
(x1)
Additional Dynamite can be found randomly in Scrap Piles in Mines and the Outlaw camps atop the
Four Hills
. The Unique Boss
"Moneybags" Martin
may also drop Dynamite when slain.
Crafting
Dynamite may be crafted by the Black Legion
Blacksmiths
at
Homestead
and
Fort Ikon
.
Ingredients:
Aether Shard
(1)
Searing Ember
(1)
Scavenged Plating
(1)
Iron bits (5000)
Crafts:
Dynamite
(3)

Eldritch Corruption
Quest Info
Given by:
Kira
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
Cult of Dreeg
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
In Service of Dreeg
Unlocks:
Dreeg's Usurper
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Item
Eldritch Corruption is an
Act 7
main
quest
, offered by
Kira
after accepting the
In Service of Dreeg
quest.
Objectives
Destroy Guardians of Ishtal (0/15)
Slay the Packhounds of Galfang (0/15)
Eliminate Okaloth's Unchained (0/15)
Return to Kira at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
The Guardians of Ishtal are found in various places in and around the
Cairan Docks
.
The Packhounds are found around the
Korvan Sands
.
Okaloth's Unchained are Wraith creatures found scattered in packs throughout the
Temple of Osyr
.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
4000
16000
40000
Cult of Dreeg
Reputation
+250
Item
Random Partial Component
Kira will then offer the
Dreeg's Usurper
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
A seer in the Dreeg camp has reported a disturbing vision.
She spoke of horrific creatures, minions of the Forgotten God, brought forth from the eldritch realm to corrupt and defile ancient sites of power.
This corruption empowers the servants of Korvaak. If the Witch Gods are to be successful in the coming battle this cannot continue.
Travel north to the ruined Temple of Osyr, The Korvan Sands, and the Cairan Docks and cleanse these sites of the fiends that inhabit them.
Objectives:
Destroy Guardians of Ishtal
Slay the Packhounds of Galfang
Eliminate Okaloth's Unchained
You have successfully purged Korvaak's minions. This will give the Witch Gods Cults an additional edge in the conflict ahead.
Report back to Kira at the Conclave of the Three.
Objectives:
Return to Kira at the Conclave of the Three

Act 3
side quest offered by
Brother Elluvius
in
Kymon's Sanctuary

Making a Stand
.
Objectives
Kill Master Ravok
Return to Brother Elluvius
Guide
Master Ravok, the Death's Whisper
can be found in
Fort Haron
, to the north-west of the
Blood Grove
Riftgate. Battle your way through the Order of Death's Vigil members to where Ravok is located at the end of the fort interior. Return to Brother Elluvius when he has been slain.
location Master Ravok

Elite
Ultimate
XP
11000

70000

Random Component

The Sacred Ashes

Quest Log
Quest log
The Order has taken over Fort Haron, in the northern Blood Grove. Brother Elluvius, on behalf of Father Kymon, has instructed you to assault the fortress and eliminate an important member of the Order by the name Master Ravok.
Objectives:
Kill Master Ravok
You have dealt with the necromancer, as Brother Elluvius instructed you to. Report back to him at Sorrow's Bastion.
Objectives:
Return to Brother Elluvius

======================================================================
PAGE: Fabric
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Fabric
======================================================================

"A little worn and stained, but otherwise in good condition."
Fabric is a quest item that can be found in chests around the
Abandoned Waterfront
. It is used in the quest
The Seamstress
.

PAGE: Family Matters
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Family_Matters
======================================================================

Family Matters
Quest Info
Given by:
Daila Thornsbury
Location:
Mourndale
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
A Sister's Love
Unlocks:
A Mother's Gift
Rewards:
XP, Item
This is an
Act 6
side
quest
, offered by
Daila Thornsbury
in
Mourndale
after completing
A Sister's Love
.
Dailla continues to pursue her brother, but cannot follow Dravis into the void. She asks you to search the Cinder Wastes on her behalf.
Objectives
Pursue Dravis into the Cinder Wastes
Collect Dravis' Offering from his Thrall
Bring Dravis' Offering to Daila in Mourndale
Guide
The Chthonic Rift leading to the
Cinder Wastes
has several possible spawn points in the Chthonic camps around Mourndale. There the boss creature
Bandragos, Thrall of Dravis
will drop the
Dravis' Offering
quest item when slain.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
22000
52000
96000
Item
Random Epic Weapon
Blazeheart
Quest Log
Quest log
Dravis is being brash and arrogant. He willingly stepped into the void itself to pursue his father. Daila has asked you to look into this lead. Dravis had entered the Cinder Wastes, through a rift somewhere in Mourndale.
Objectives:
Pursue Dravis into the Cinder Wastes
There was no sign of Dravis, but you did find another clue on his fallen minions. Return it to Daila in Mourndale, outside of Malmouth.
Objectives:
Collect Dravis' Offering from his Thrall
Bring Dravis' Offering to Daila in Mourndale

======================================================================
PAGE: Fate of the Bloodsworn
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Fate_of_the_Bloodsworn
======================================================================

Fate of the Bloodsworn
Quest Info
Given by:
N/A
Location:
Temple of Ateph
Faction:
N/A
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Bloodsworn Damned
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP, Item, Note
Fate of the Bloodsworn is a small
Act 7
side
quest
, and is available only if the player has completed the act 6 quest
The Bloodsworn Damned
and allowed the Bloodsworn to go free, making it clear they did not make use of the second chance they had been given. The quest is activated on entering the second level of the
Temple of Ateph
.
Objectives
Find the Bloodsworn Manuscript (0/1)
Guide
Enter the second level of the Temple of Ateph. Kill the Chthonian Rylok Boss named
Ketan'Thunn
. A nearby
Bloodsworn Corpse
can then be looted to collect the
Bloodsworn Manuscript
quest item and complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
800
4000
12000
Note
Bloodsworn Manuscript Excerpt
Item
Random Partial Component
Quest Log
Quest log
When you approached the altar in the Temple of Ateph, you discovered a number of Bloodsworn cultist corpses strewn about. You were assaulted by a Chthonian monstrosity, perhaps the result of a failed summoning.
Upon closer inspection, these Bloodsworn seem familiar. Search the Temple of Ateph, in the Ruins of Abyd north of the Vanguard of the Three, for any clues regarding how these cultists got here and what they were trying to do.
Objectives:
Find the Bloodsworn Manuscript

======================================================================
PAGE: Find Elsa
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Find_Elsa
======================================================================

Find Elsa
Quest Info
Given by:
Mornay
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Warden
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP
This is an
Act 2
quest
offered by
Mornay
after completing
The Warden
.
He and and his scouting partner
Elsa
were ambushed by outlaws when scouting north of Devil's Crossing and he fears they still have her.
Objectives
Discover Elsa's fate
Let Mornay know about Elsa
Guide
When you talk to Darius Cronley he tells you she escaped; the outlaws no longer have her.
This quest can also be resolved If you find Elsa in the
Barren Highlands
- she is camped by the road just over the natural bridge. She will explain that she has no desire to return to Mornay or Devil's Crossing and is striking out on her own for Homestead.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2500
14000
32000
Quest Log
Quest log
Mornay's scouting partner, Elsa, is probably still alive and in the hands of those brutes. If you find a way to rescue her from their clutches, Mornay will be eternally grateful.
Objectives:
Discover Elsa's fate
You have discovered Elsa's fate and should inform Mornay in Devil's Crossing of your discovery.
Objectives:
Let Mornay know about Elsa

======================================================================
PAGE: First Seal of Morgoneth
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/First_Seal_of_Morgoneth
======================================================================

"In the darkness bound, Morgoneth's vile tongue saw seven fall from grace. Joined in the night, his fate became theirs. No longer will they bask in the light of the Eldritch Sun. They craved the cold embrace of night and so forever will they roam its dark tapestry.
The way is shut, the heresy sealed. But should the Korvan faith be shaken once more by Morgoneth's folly, then seek the second seal where stone meets the bleached sands, beyond the watchful eye of twin gryphons.
I pray that knowledge of this black stain upon the Korvan lands will be lost with our final breaths."
The First Seal of Moroneth is a quest item used in the
Paying Debts
quest in
Forgotten Gods
. It drops from
Gurblix the Digested
, the boss creature in the third level of the
Maw of Enaht
.

======================================================================

Flesh and Iron
Quest Info
Given by:
Harmond
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Something for Nothing
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Scrap
Flesh and Iron is an
Act 1
side quest, offered by
Harmond
in
Devil's Crossing
.
Objectives
Slay Balros, the Malformed
Slay Hagra, the Tormented
Return to Harmond
Guide
Balros and Hagra are a pair of Fleshwarped mutants located in the
Moldering Fields
area of the Burrwitch Outskirts. They spawn together by a house on the left hand side of the road.
Return to Harmond after killing them both.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
450
13500
29000
Iron
1200
5000
12000
Item
Scrap (3)
Quest Log
Quest log
Harmond's lust for the suffering of the Dead seems insatiable. He told you of Balros and Hagrad in the Moldering Fields, two horribly mutated souls that pursued the survivors fleeing Burrwitch. Return to him after they are dead.
Objectives:
Slay Balros, the Malformed
Slay Hagra, the Tormented
You have slain Balros and Hagra.
Return to Harmond in Devil's Crossing.
Objectives:
Return to Harmond in Devil's Crossing

======================================================================
PAGE: For the Children
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/For_the_Children
======================================================================

For the Children
Quest Info
Given by:
Alicia
Location:
New Harbor
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Paying Tributes
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP
This is an
Act 2
side quest, offered by
Alicia
at
New Harbor
if you killed Silas in the
Paying Tributes
quest.
Background
Someone in Cronley's Gang witnessed the killing of
Silas
, and arrived shortly after you left to take revenge on the fishing village, killing everyone and taking the children to Cronley's Hideout. Alicia begs you to rescue them.
Objectives
Rescue Oscar Jr. and Judith from
Cronley's Hideout
.
Check up on Oscar Jr. and Judith in Devil's Crossing.
Guide
The children will be found locked in cages in the area immediately beyond Darius Cronley's boss room. On talking to them, you will automatically open a riftgate so they can travel safely to
Devil's Crossing
.
The children will be found on the upper level of the prison with Constance, Alex and Jane. Talk to Oscar Jr. to claim the reward and complete the quest.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
1500
8000
22000
Quest Log
Quest log
Because you killed Silas, the outlaw overseer at New Harbor, the rest of Cronley's gang took revenge on the fishing village. You must rescue the children from Darius' clutches, deep within Cronley's Hideout.
Objectives:
Rescue Oscar Jr. and Judith from Cronley's Hideout
You have rescued Oscar Jr. and Judith from Cronley's Hideout and safely transported them to Devil's Crossing. You should check up on them.
Objectives:
Check up on Oscar Jr. and Judith in Devil's Crossing

======================================================================
PAGE: For the People
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/For_the_People
======================================================================

For the People
Quest Info
Given by:
Inquisitor Creed
Location:
Sewer Hideout
Faction:
Malmouth Resistance
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Someone on the Inside
Unlocks:
Tip of the Spear
Stoking the Flames
Mad Ramblings
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Item
This is an
Act 6
Main
quest
, offered by
Inquisitor Creed
after completing
Someone on the Inside
.
Creed has heard of an old Resistance outpost in the Steelcap District.  He believes re-taking it will boost morale and provide a useful base of operations in the battle for Malmouth.
Objectives
Retake the base in the Steelcap District
Speak to Inquisitor Creed in the Resistance Hideout
Guide
Take the Northwest exit from the
Sewer Hideout
to reach the
Steelcap District
. The Riftgate there will be swarming with Aetherials; defeat the waves of enemies to capture the Rift Gate and sieze the outpost.
Inquisitor Creed will appear north of the Rift, speak to him to receive the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
42000
82000
138000
Malmouth Resistance
Reputation
+1000
Item
Scrap
(8)
Creed will then offer the
Tip of the Spear
quest,
Korinia
will offer
Stoking the Flames
, and
Ivonda
will offer
Mad Ramblings
.
Quest Log
Quest log
Korinia, the resistance leader, has informed Creed of an old base of operations up in the Steelcap District. Inquisitor Creed thinks this may be a way to gain a foothold in the city and launch a counter-attack on the Aetherials. Reach the Steelcap District through the city sewers and help the resistance fighters retake their base.
Objectives:
Retake the base in the Steelcap District
The battle for the resistance base was successful. Though the base appears to have been heavily damaged, it is secure enough for now. There's a lot of work to be done before it's fully operational. Speak to Inquisitor Creed and find out what he's planning next.
Objectives:
Speak to Inquisitor Creed in the Resistance Hideout

"A fragmented passage on old Arkovia’s history. Impossible to decipher without the remaining pieces."
Forgotten Passage is a quest item required for the
The Depths of Old Arkovia
quest. It can be found on various Ancient Lecterns in the
Arkovian Undercity
.

Future Sisters
Quest Info
Given by:
Guardian Syndia
Location:
Coven's Refuge
Faction:
Coven of Ugdenbog
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
-
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 5
side
quest
, offered by
Guardian Syndia
in
Coven's Refuge
.
Guardian Syndia informs you that several witches traveling to join the coven have not yet arrived, and suspects something may have happened to them. She asks you to look for them while in Ugdenbog.
Objectives
Rescue the traveling witches
Speak to Guardian Syndia at the Coven's Refuge
Guide
The witches can be found in
Ugdenbog
, held prisoner by Wendigo cultists some way north of the
Ugdenbog Rift
. Speak to them and you will open a riftgate to transport them to safety in Coven's Refuge. Return to Guardian Syndia for the reward.
Quest Location
Rewards
Component Reward Table
Black Tallow
Ectoplasm
Haunted Steel
Rotten Heart
Serrated Spike
Severed Claw
Vengeful Wraith
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
12000
25000
54000
Coven of Ugdenbog
Reputation
+250
Item
Scrap
(x5)
Item
Random Partial Component
Quest Log
Quest log
Guardian Syndia of the Coven of Ugdenbog has asked you to seek out a retinue of future sisters that never arrived at the refuge.
She speculates that the cannibals out in Ugdenbog to the north have found them first. Syndia offered you some materials should you rescue those that are still alive.
Objectives:
Rescue the traveling witches
You found some of the lost sisters out in Ugdenbog and returned them to the refuge.
You should speak to Guardian Syndia at the Coven's Refuge for a reward.
Objectives:
Speak to Guardian Syndia at the Coven's Refuge

======================================================================
PAGE: Good Aspirants are Difficult to Find
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Good_Aspirants_are_Difficult_to_Find
======================================================================

Good Aspirants are Difficult to Find
Quest Info
Given by:
Keisen
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
Cult of Solael
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Loyalty to the Three
Unlocks:
Worthy of Solael
Rewards:
XP, Scrap
Good Aspirants are Difficult to Find
is an
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Keisen
in the
Conclave of the Three
after completing the
Loyalty to the Three
quest.
Keisen has sent a group of aspirants to scour the Temple of Osyr for valuable artifacts. They are late in returning and Kaisen asks you to find them, or at least the objects they have scavenged.
Objectives
Find the Solael Aspirants
Speak with Keisen at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
Kait and Elita, the missing Aspirants, can be found outside the
Temple City of Osyr
, north-west of the Riftgate.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2000
22000
58000
Cult of Solael
Reputation
+250
Item
Scrap
(x5)
Keisen will then offer the
Worthy of Solael
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
What was once a battle against a raving zealot has turned into an assault on a forgotten god. The cults were ill-prepared for a conflict of this magnitude.
A group of Solael aspirants was sent out to the Temple of Osyr, to the north of the Conclave of the Three, to scout and gather any relics they could scavenge to aid in the upcoming attack.
They should have returned yesterday, but no one has heard from them.
Keisen has asked you find them and return with anything they found, and possibly with them too.
Objectives:
Find the Solael Aspirants
You found the missing group of aspirants and returned them to the Conclave of the Three.
Report back to Keisen.
Objectives:
Speak with Keisen at the Conclave of the Three

"the impossible to decipher scribblings of the mad Arcanist Oswald Hargate."
Hargate's Formula is a quest item required for the
The Origin of the Slith
side quest. It can be found in an Ornate Strongbox in level 2 of
Hargate's Laboratory
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Hargate's Mysteries
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Hargate's_Mysteries
======================================================================

Hargate's Mysteries
Quest Info
Given by:
Kasparov
Location:
The Infestation
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Origin of the Slith
Unlocks:
n/a
Rewards:
XP, Items
This is a small
Act 6
side
quest
, available on encountering a Strange Crystal Formation in
The Infestation
, if the player has completed
The Origin of the Slith
and kept
Hargate's Formula
.
The strange crystal hums with unusual energies, and resembles a phenomenon described in Hargate's Formula. Perhaps comparing the notes with the formation will help make sense of some of the late Hargate's work.
Objectives
Study the Crystal Formation using Hargate's Formula
Guide
The Strange Crystal Formation can be found in the final section of
The Infestation
. Choosing to study the crystal will destroy it and complete the quest. The reward on Ultimate will allow the player to summon a floating Aether Crystal pet.
Crystal location
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
10000
23000
50000
Item
Aetherial Missive
Aetherial Mutagen
Hargate's Crystal
Quest Log
Quest log
You encountered a strange aether crystal formation within Malmouth that resonated with energy. After studying it using Hargate's Formula, you changed its mutagenic properties.
Objectives:
Study the Crystal Formation using Hargate's Formula

"To my dear brother: May this amulet keep you strong in battle. -Sybil"
Hart's Amulet is a quest item required for the
A Sister's Gift
quest. It is looted from
Milton Hart
in the
Sodden Hollow
.

"The still glowing aether eyes stare back blankly at you."
The Head of Archivist Thelon is a quest item  required for
The Outcast's Revenge
quest. it drops from Archivist Thelon in
Port Valbury: High Town
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Heart of Darkness
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Heart_of_Darkness
======================================================================

"It continues to beat within your bag with an eerily steady rhythm."
The Heart of Darkness is a quest item used in
Lokarr's Secret Quest
. It is crafted by
Arcturus - Cursed Smith
in
Gloomwald
(Ultimate only).
Ingredients:
1x Ancient Heart
1x Black Tallow
1x Consecrated Wrapping

======================================================================
PAGE: Helping Out
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Helping_Out
======================================================================

Helping Out
Quest Info
Given by:
Captain John Bourbon
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
Devil's Crossing
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Waking to Misery
Unlocks:
Securing Burrwitch
Rewards:
XP, Rep
Helping Out
is the second main quest in
Act 1
. It is given by
Captain John Bourbon
after completing the
Waking to Misery
quest.
Background
Since
the Taken
has killed
the Reanimator
who was behind the
walking dead
attacking
Devil's Crossing
, the attacks have become less frequent and more severe. This allows
Captain Bourbon
to start planning the next major move, but in the meantime, while his scouts haven't fully reported yet, he expects the protagonist to help out other survivors.
Kasparov
, the local scientist, wished to speak to the player character about their connection to the
Aetherials
, while
Barnabas
, the handyman, needs help with fixing the water pump.
Objectives
Help Barnabas with the Water Pump
Help Kasparov with his research
Meet Bourbon inside the Prison
Guide
Kasparov can be found in the house next to the
riftgate
in Devil's Crossing. Barnabas can be found just outside the prison walls by the windmill, to the south.
Talk to Barnabas to receive the
And Not a Drop to Drink
side quest.
Talk to Kasparov to receive the
Kasparov's Experiment
side quest.
After completing the two side quests return to Captain Bourbon for the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
300
11000
40000
Reputation
+150 (Devil's Crossing)
Bourbon will then offer the next quest,
Securing Burrwitch
.
Quest Log
Quest log
Bourbon has asked you to help out Kasparov and Barnabas while he waits for his scouts to return. Kasparov does his research near the Riftgate in Devil's Crossing. Barnabas can be found just outside the prison walls by the windmill, on the south side.
Objectives:
Help Barnabas with the Water Pump
Help Kasparov with his research
Now that you have helped Kasparov and Barnabas, you should report back to Bourbon in Devil's Crossing. He should be awaiting your return inside the prison, in his office.
Objectives:
Meet Bourbon inside the Prison

======================================================================
PAGE: Hidden Wealth
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Hidden_Wealth
======================================================================

Hidden Wealth
Quest Info
Given by:
None
Location:
Rotting Croplands
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
None
Unlocks:
One-Shot Chest
Rewards:
XP, Note
This is a small
Act 3
side
quest
, activated when you find
The Last Will of Marthos Everbrook
on a corpse inside a house in either the
Infested Farms
or the
Rotting Croplands
.
The Will details the location of some buried treasure and will lead to a
One-Shot Chest
.
Objectives
Seek out the Hidden Treasure
Guide
The corpse bearing the
Last Will of Marthos Everbrook
spawns in one of four locations (see map below). The Hidden Wealth is located on the upper western edge of the Rotting Croplands. A quest marker will be visible on the map as you draw near. You will need to place 1
Dynamite
at the Detonation Site to uncover the chest; the quest concludes when it is opened.
Note that the Detonation Site only appears after the quest is activated.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
5500
18000
34000
Quest Log
Quest log
You have found an old will describing the location of a treasure buried somewhere in the hills west of Homestead. Some notes written along the bottom indicate that you will need explosives. This seems worth investigating further.
Objectives:
Seek out the Hidden Treasure
Gallery
Locations for finding the
Last Will of Marthos Everbrook
Hidden Wealth Location

In Service of Bysmiel
Quest Info
Given by:
Byscilla, Matron of Rifts

Cult of Bysmiel

This is an
Act 7
main
quest
, offered by
Byscilla, Matron of Rifts
after choosing to work with the
Cult of Bysmiel
during the
Loyalty to the Three
quest.
Byscilla says that the Forgotten God is stirring beneath his Temple, and plans have been made to destroy him.
Objectives

Alain

and
The Power of Galfang
. When these are complete, Byscilla can be found at the
Vanguard of the Three
and the quest turned in.

======================================================================

Infested Fields
Quest Info
Given by:
Douglass Sullivan Oldbarrow
Location:
Homestead
Faction:
Homestead
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
We Need Food
Unlocks:
Culling the Swarm
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep
This is An
Act 3
main
quest
, given by
Douglass Sullivan Oldbarrow
in Homestead after completing the
We Need Food
quest.
Background
Douglass Oldbarrow has asked you to help the farmers with the Dermapterans that infest the Elmsworth and Thorsnbury farms to the west of Homestead. The Black Legion seems deaf to the farmers' pleas for assistance, but Douglass firmly believes that there simply won't be enough food to go around if additional farmland is not secured.
Objectives
Clear out the Dermapteran Egg Clusters near Homestead (0/10)
Return to Douglass in Homestead
Guide
Head out through Homestead's north gate and turn west. (Note that you must have completed the
A Timely Arrival
and
Infested Fields
quests to be allowed through the gate.)
The Egg Clusters are easily found in the farmland just outside Homestead and will be marked with a star on the corner map. Clear out
Thornsbury Farm
, and the neighboring
Elmsworth Farm
to the south.
After destroying 10 Egg Clusters you can then return to Douglass to complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
9000
36000
70000
Iron
1200
5000
11000
Homestead
Reputation
+500
Douglass will then offer the
Culling the Swarm
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Douglass Oldbarrow has implored you to help the farmers with the Dermapterans infesting the Elmsworth and Thorsnbury farms to the west of Homestead. The Black Legion seems deaf to the farmers' pleas for assistance, but Douglass firmly believes that there simply won't be enough food to go around if additional farmland is not secured. Head out into the infested fields and destroy the Dermapteran egg clusters. That should drive them out.
Objective:
Clear out the Dermapteran Egg Clusters near Homestead (0/10)
You have destroyed the egg clusters infesting the Elmsworth and Thornsbury farms, along with many Dermapterans guarding them. Return to Homestead and inform Douglass that the farms are once again clear of infestation.
Objective:
Return to Douglass in Homestead

PAGE: Into the Jaws of Madness

======================================================================

Into the Jaws of Madness
Quest Info
Given by:
Garradia
Location:
Coven's Refuge
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
A Witch's Bargain
Unlocks:
Along the Void's Edge
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 5
main
quest
, offered by
Garradia
after completing the
A Witch's Bargain
quest.
Having recovered the Ugdenbog Fetish, Garradia will now help in bringing back Ulgrim from the Void and reaching Malmouth.
Objectives
Bring Ulgrim's Keepsake to the Altar of Rattosh
Perform the ritual to locate Ulgrim
Find the entrance to the Void's Edge within the Desolate Wastes
Find Ulgrim at the Void's Edge
Guide
The Altar of Rattosh is located north of the Barrowholm Rift. There, place
Ulgrim's Keepsake
on the altar, and you will be able to enter the Chthonic Rift into the
Desolate Wastes
.
At the northern end of the map is the entrance to the
Void's Edge
, where Ulgrim can be found. He will appear to have lost his mind, and talking to Ulgrim will present many dialogue options. Using his name will cause him to come to his senses and the quest will end.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
33000
68000
120000
Black Legion
Reputation
+500
Quest Log
Quest log
Garradia of the Coven of Ugdenbog has kept her end of the bargain. She marked Ulgrim's Keepsake with a ritual binding and informed you of an ancient altar once used by the coven during its darker years. It has fallen into disuse and the site has since been reclaimed by the swamp, but the veil is weakened there and should serve as a conduit for what you seek.
Bring Ulgrim's Keepsake to the Altar of Rattosh, located in Ugdenbog to the north of Barrowholm, and perform Garradia's ritual.
Objectives:
Bring Ulgrim's Keepsake to the Altar of Rattosh
Perform the ritual to locate Ulgrim
Using Garradia's ritual, you were able to open a rift to the Chthonic void and, with luck, Ulgrim. The warrior was pulled in to the darkness from which the Loghorrean itself was spawned and so you must now travel deep into the void, deeper than anyone had ever dared before.
Enter the portal at the Altar of Rattosh and traverse the Desolate Wastes to find the portal to the Void's Edge.
Objectives:
Find the entrance to the Void's Edge within the Desolate Wastes
The Void's Edge looms before you and with it some of the void's most dangerous beings. Make your way carefully through this treacherous place and find out what happened to Ulgrim.
Objectives:
Find Ulgrim at the Void's Edge

======================================================================
PAGE: Iris of Eternal Night
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Iris_of_Eternal_Night
======================================================================

"The Iris trembles with terrifying potential. Its jewels seem duller in sunlight."
The Iris of Eternal Night is a quest item required for the
Paying Debts
quest in
Forgotten Gods
. It drops from the
Morgoneth's Collection
treasure chest at the end of the
Tomb of the Heretic
challenge dungeon.
The Iris will drop whether the quest is active or not.

PAGE: Karroz's Tome

"A tome filled with dark rituals that depict the return of a great darkness from within the Necropolis."
This is a quest item dropped by
Karroz, Sigil of Ch'thon
during the
Reaping What You Sow
quest.

======================================================================
PAGE: Kasparov's Experiment
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Kasparov's_Experiment
======================================================================

Kasparov's Experiment
Quest Info
Given by:
Kasparov
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
none
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Helping Out
Unlocks:
The Inventor's Apprentice
Rewards:
XP, Skill Point
Kasparov's Experiment is an
Act 1
quest which forms part of the
Helping Out
quest.
The inventor Kasparov has developed a prototype device he believes is capable of  allowing anyone who possesses it to open portals attuned to rift gates, but he needs
Aether Crystals
to power it.
Objectives
Collect Aether Crystals for Kasparov (0/4)
Bring the Aether Crystals to Kasparov in Devil's Crossing.
Guide
The crystals can be easily found around
Burial Hill
during the
Waking to Misery
quest.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
250
10000
36000
1 Skill Point
Kasparov will then offer another side quest,
The Inventor's Apprentice
.
Quest Log
Quest log
The inventor Kasparov has developed a prototype device he believes is capable of allowing anyone possessing it to open portals to attuned rift gates, but he needs Aether Crystals to power it.
Aether Crystals are often found near large collections of corpses, such as graveyards. Gather a few of them and return to Kasparov.
Objectives:
Collect Aether Crystals for Kasparov (0/4)
Bring the Aether Crystals to Kasparov in Devil's Crossing

, offered by

.
Kasparov believes he has deciphered the notes recovered from Hargate's laboratory, and has attuned an Aether Crystal to the specifications they contain. He may have found a way to reverse the effects of the corrupting energies the crystals emanate.
Objectives
Witness Kasparov's Experiment
Guide
Speaking to Kasparov will both begin and end the quest.
The Kasparov's Crystal reward item on Ultimate Difficulty will allow the player to summon a cosmetic pet.

You watched as Kasparov put what he had learned within Hargate's Formula to use. The experiment's results were...mixed as usual, but hope remains that Kasparov will find a solution for Aetherial mutation some day.

Kymon's Deserters
Quest Info
Given by:
Alain
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
Cult of Bysmiel
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Byscilla's Plan
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Item
Kymon's Deserters is an
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Alain
after completing
Byscilla's Plan
and reaching Honored Faction Status with the
Cult of Bysmiel
.
The Cult has spotted a group of Kymon's Chosen deserters fleeing the Korvan Basin. They have also stolen an ancient Korvan artifact,which must be recovered.
Objectives
Recover the relic from the Kymon's Chosen Deserters
Deliver the relic to Alain at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
The Kymon's Chosen Deserters are located in the
Sunbane Oasis
.
Brother Haggan
can be spoken to and the player can either convince him to hand over the artifact peacefully, or kill him for it. Either way, the
Mummified Flesh of Korvaak
quest item is recovered, to be returned to Alain.
Deserter Location
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
13000
30000
65000
Cult of Bysmiel
Reputation
+500
Item
Blueprint:
Emblem of Korvan Swiftness
Blueprint:
Glyph of Korvan Swiftness
Blueprint:
Rune of Korvan Swiftness
Quest Log
Quest log
Bysmiel's spies have spotted a group of Kymon's Chosen fleeing the battlefield. It is believed that they are trying to escape with an ancient Korvan relic.
The relic must be recovered.
The lives of the Chosen were forfeit the moment they sold their souls to Kymon's foolish crusade. Find them within the Sunbane Oasis, to the east of the Cairan Docks.
Objectives:
Recover the relic from the Kymon's Chosen Deserters
Deliver the relic to Alain at the Conclave of the Three

======================================================================
PAGE: Kymon's Secret
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Kymon's_Secret
======================================================================

Kymon's Secret
Quest Info
Given by:
Father Kymon
Location:
Kymon's Sanctuary
Faction:
Kymon's Chosen
Type:
Side quest
Prerequisites:
Braving the Void
Honored Faction Status
Unlocks:
A Pledge to Cairn
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Item
Kymon's Secret is a side quest offered by
Father Kymon
in
Kymon's Sanctuary
, after completing
Braving the Void
and gaining
Honored
Faction status.
Background
Father Kymon seeks a powerful relic, hidden behind a false wall in the
Tomb of Korvaak
, and asks you to obtain it for him.
Objectives
Search for the Eye of Korvaak (0/1)
Return to Father Kymon
Guide
Loose Torch
The Tomb of Korvaak is located to the south-east of the
Asterkarn Valley
rift. At the end of the dungeon, in the final room where
Harvoul, the Earthshaker
is located, there is a Loose Torch on a wall which will open a secret door.
Sharanatu, Harbinger of the Void
is located at the end of the area beyond this secret door, and will drop the
Eye of Korvaak
when killed.
Completing the quest unlocks the Iron Gate to Kymon's Study, where
The Messenger
is located and which contains two notes.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
16000
44500
82000
Reputation
+2000
Item
2 Random Rare Partial Components
Quest Log
Quest log
Father Kymon has a special task he has entrusted only to you. Within the Asterkarn Mountain, north of Darkvale, there is a tomb which houses a powerful relic known as the Eye of Korvaak. Father Kymon wishes you to recover the relic as it will please Empyrion. The Eye is said to be a lens into a man's soul, allowing Kymon to peer into the hearts of his followers and tell the truly devout apart from the false. The Eye is hidden from mortal hands behind a false wall. Look for a torch that has lost its flame. Should you recover the Eye, Kymon will entrust you with his innermost secrets and allow you to enter his study.
Objectives:
Search for the Eye of Korvaak (0/1)
Return to Father Kymon

CATEGORIES: Quests

======================================================================

Legion Retribution
Quest Info
Given by:
Spellbreaker Moira
Location:
Fort Ikon
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Honored Faction Status
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Items
This is an
Act 4
side
quest
, offered by
Spellbreaker Moira
after reaching
Honored
faction status with the Black Legion.
Moira tells of intense Aetherial terraforming activity in the region now known as the Immolation, near Deadman's Gulch, and asks you to deal with it.
Objectives
Slay the Herald of Destruction
Report to Spellbreaker Moira
Guide
From
Deadman's Gulch
, use the Mine Entrance at the end of the valley of aetherflame. This will take you to
The Immolation
, where the
Herald of Destruction
can be found. Note that the area is full of Aether Crystals and damaging ground effects.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
16000
65000
108000
Black Legion
Reputation
+1000
Item
2 Rare Partial Components
Quest Log
Quest log
Spellbreaker Moira of the Black Legion has tasked you with a dangerous mission that should cripple the Aetherials' ability to transform Cairn into whatever hell they came from. To her, it's not just about that though. This is a mission of payback, of revenge for lives taken. Travel to Deadman's Gulch and reopen the sealed off mine-shaft leading to the area called the Immolation. There, among the Aetherfire, you will find the Herald of Destruction, a giant Aetherial obelisk that has been terraforming the landscape. Destroy it, take revenge upon the Aetherials in the name of the Black Legion.
Objectives:
Slay the Herald of Destruction
You have slain the Herald of Destruction, thus crippling the Aetherials' effort to terraform Cairn and taking revenge upon the Aetherials for the lives lost in Moira's battalion. You should report back to her in Fort Ikon.
Objectives:
Report to Spellbreaker Moira

======================================================================
PAGE: Liberate the Liberators
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Liberate_the_Liberators
======================================================================

Liberate the Liberators
Quest Info
Given by:
Captain Wilfor
Location:
Steelcap District
Faction:
Malmouth Resistance
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Stoking the Flames
Unlocks:
The Blackiron Docks
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 6
side
quest
, offered by
Captain Wilfor
in the
Steelcap District
Resistance Hideout as part of the
Stoking the Flames
quest.
Several Resistance memebers have gone out to search the Steelcap District for supplies, but some have not returned. Captain Wilfor asks you the search for Hyram and Nadia, as well as any other survivors.
Objectives
Find and Rescue Hyram
Find and Rescue Nadia
Speak to Captain Wilfor at the Resistance Hideout
Guide
Hyram and Nadia can be found in Malmouth Harbor, Hyram with three other survivors on the second level of a house, and Nadia with one other in a separate building to the South East. Randomly Hyram & Nadia can swap locations.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
20000
36000
72000
Malmouth Resistance
Reputation
+250
Item
Aetherial Mutagen
Quest Log
Quest log
Several members of the Resistance never returned from their recent excurson into Aetherial territory. Captain Wilfor wasn't sure they'd be up to the task, and it appears he was correct. Unfortunately it now means that a scavenging operation in the Steelcrap District has turned into a rescue. Find Hyram and Nadia along with any other survivors, if they are still alive.
Objectives:
Find and Rescue Hyram
Find and Rescue Nadia
You have successfully rescued Hyram and Nadia and should report back to Captain Wilfor at the Resistance Hideout.
Objectives:
Speak to Captain Wilfor at the Resistance Hideout

======================================================================
PAGE: Lokarr's Secret Quest
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Lokarr's_Secret_Quest
======================================================================

Lokarr's Secret Quest
Quest Info
Given by:
n/a
Location:
n/a
Faction:
n/a
Type:
n/a
Prerequisites:
n/a
Unlocks:
Edge of Reality
Rewards:
n/a
Lokarr's Secret Quest
is available on Ultimate difficulty only. There are several steps required, with no attached quest and only cryptic clues given for each step.
The "quest" unlocks the secret
Edge of Reality
level, and allows the player to fight
Lokarr
in the
Crucible of the Dead
.
Guide
1) The quest begins with finding
Arcturus - Cursed Smith
in
Gloomwald
. On completing
The Gloomwald Stash
side quest, he can be found west of the secret area containing
Nane's Stash
, in a second secret area accessed by passing under some giant tangled roots. There, next to Arcturus, can be found a Rotting Corpse which holds the
Turn Back!
Note
. This note provides a clue for finding the Sanctum:
Do not be so Blue in the face. When Flame meets Flame, so shall the way forward be opened...
Arcturus himself can be used to craft the
Heart of Darkness
, the flavor text to which provides another clue -
"Teeming with vile energies that hunger for an ashen altar"
2) This leads the player to the
Desolate Wastes
, accessed via the
Altar of Rattosh
. On the northern edge of the area is a stone altar with an Urn next to it. The Urn contains the
Mythical Stormheart
. The Urn can only spawn if the
Heart of Darkness
is in the player's inventory.
3) In the Malmouth Outskirts, the player will find, next to the
Ruined Shrine
, an altar and circle with a blue flame. This is one of the flames referred to in the
Turn Back!
note. The other is
Flameond Bleu
, an Aetherial zombie creature who has 3 possible spawn points around
Malmouth Outskirts
.
On finding Flameond, he must be led to the altar next to the Shrine - it is helpful to clear the area first, as other creatures will attack him.
Sacrificing Flamond Bleu at the magic circle will open an
Aetherial Rift
to a secret area adjacent Malmouth Outskirts.
4) There, the player will encounter a Bound Spirit, who will ask for the three objects:
Heart of Darkness
,
Mythical Stormheart
and
Sahdina's Memento
.
Sahdina's Memento can be found in
Devil's Crossing
, next to the corpse of the Aetherial Colossus lying over
Kerrick's
destroyed merchant stand. Moving close enough will add the item automatically to the player inventory.
Handing the items in to the Bound Spirit will destroy two of them, but the Mythical Stormheart will be retained. Another Aetherial Rift will be opened, which leads to the Sanctum of the Chosen.
5) The Sanctum contains the
You Are Not Welcome!
note, which provides the final clue -
Root of All Evil, flourishing in the wake of blood
.
Behind the
Ruined Shrine
in the Sanctum is a
Stone Door
, which leads to the
Edge of Reality
. About a quarter of the way along the area is a secret path leading to the
Root of All Evil
, a creature that, when destroyed, will open an
Aetherial Rift
to the
Crucible of the Dead
, where Lokarr can be found.
Gallery
Arcturus' Location
Mythical Stormheart Location
Flameond Bleu Locations
Root of All Evil Location

======================================================================
PAGE: Lost Armaments
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Lost_Armaments
======================================================================

Lost Armaments
Quest Info
Given by:
Weapons Master Borrov
Location:
Homestead
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Friendly Status
Unlocks:
Nothing
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep
This is an
Act 3
side
quest
, granted by
Weapons Master Borrov
in
Homestead
. It is available once you have Friendly status with the Black Legion.
Background
Weapons Master Borrov is distraught by the fact that the Black Legion had to abandon its artillery on the road when the
Aetherials
attacked Homestead in force. The area is now covered in Aetherfire and it is far too dangerous to recover them.
Objectives
Recover the Lost Cannons in the Conflagration
Return to Weapons Master Borrov in Homestead
Guide
Head north-east (south-east of Fallow Fields) from the Homestead Rift Gate and make your way through
The Conflagration
. The Abandoned Cannons are located at the very end of the area, by the broken bridge, and will have a quest marker on the map. You will also have to get past the boss creature
Herald of the Flame
. Click on the Abandoned Cannon to reclaim it then return to Borrov to complete the quest.
Screen Shot of map for location of Lost Armaments
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
13000
40000
75000
Iron
2000
10000
20000
Black Legion
Reputation
+250
When the quest is complete two cannons will appear on the Homestead ramparts.
Quest Log
Quest log
Weapons Master Borrov of the Black Legion is distraught by the loss of several cannons that the Legion was forced to abandon in an area northeast of Homestead known as the Conflagration. When you asked about it, he warned you that their recovery is the equivalent of suicide as the area burns with aetherfire.
Objective:
Recover the Lost Cannons in the Conflagration
You have entered the Conflagration against better judgment and destroyed the Aetherial creature they call the Herald of Flame.
With it out of the way, the Black Legion can now safely reclaim the cannons they were forced to leave behind. Return to Weapons Master Borrov in Homestead with the news.
Objective:
Return to Weapons Master Borrov in Homestead

======================================================================
PAGE: Lost Father
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Lost_Father
======================================================================

Lost Father
Quest Info
Given by:
Amala Torven
Location:
Fort Ikon
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Side quest
Prerequisites:
Desperate Measures
Unlocks:
n/a
Rewards:
XP, Item
This is a small
Act 5
side
quest
, offered by
Amala Torven
after accepting the
Desperate Measures
quest.
Whilst traveling from Malmouth to Devil's Crossing, Amala Torven and her father were attacked by cannibals in Gloomwald. Amala was forced to leave her injured father behind in order to seek aid. She asks if you can search for him.
Objectives
Find Garett Torven in Gloomwald
Speak with Amala Torven in Devil's Crossing
Guide
Garett Torven
can be found in
Gloomwald
, directly south of the Gloomwald Crossing Rift. Talk to him and he will be teleported to safety in
Devil's Crossing
. Return there and speak to Amala to claim the reward.
Garett's Location
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
9000
20000
48000
Item
Tonic of Reshaping
Quest Log
Quest log
Amala's father, Garett, was too injured to go on and Amala was forced to abandon him in Gloomwald in order to seek assistance. She eventually found her way to Devil's Crossing, but her father is still out there.
Amala has hopes that he is still alive, but many dangers lurk within the thorned wood. She has beseeched you to seek out Garett in Gloomwald on your way up to Ugdenbog, north of the Burrwitch Estates.
Objectives:
Find Garett Torven in Gloomwald
You found Amala's father and sent him to the safety of Devil's Crossing.
Speak to Amala in Devil's Crossing to see how he is faring.
Objectives:
Speak with Amala Torven in Devil's Crossing

======================================================================
PAGE: Lost Survivor
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Lost_Survivor
======================================================================

Lost Survivor
Quest Info
Given by:
Faldis
Location:
Lower Crossing
Faction:
Devil's Crossing
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
None
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep, Scrap
Lost Survivor
is an
Act 1
side quest available from
Faldis
in
Lower Crossing
.
Faldis, scavenging for supplies in the Lower Crossing, has become trapped inside a house surrounded by
rift scourges
and the walking dead.
Objectives
Speak to Faldis inside
Devil's Crossing
Guide
Faldis can be found inside a house just before the Lower Crossing Rift. Speaking to him will provide the option of opening a rift for him back to Devil's Crossing.
Unless playing on Elite or Ultimate, it is necessary to complete
Waking to Misery
before you can speak to Faldis inside the prison to complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
150
9500
22000
Iron
500
3000
8000
Reputation
+50 (Devil's Crossing)
Item
Scrap (1)
Quest Log
Quest log
Faldis was out on a scavenging mission for Devil's Crossing when he became trapped by a bunch of Rift Scourges. You convinced him to take your riftgate back to Devil's Crossing. Speak to Faldis inside the prison.
(You may need to earn Bourbon's trust first.)
Objectives:
Speak to Faldis inside Devil's Crossing

======================================================================
PAGE: Loyalty to the Three
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Loyalty_to_the_Three
======================================================================

Loyalty to the Three
Quest Info
Given by:
The Emissary
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
The Eldritch Trials
Unlocks:
In Service of Bysmiel
In Service of Dreeg
In Service of Solael
Rewards:
XP, Rep
This is an
Act 7
main
quest
, offered by
The Emissary
in the
Conclave of the Three
after completing the
The Emissary
quest.
The Emissary says the time has come to choose which Witch God to serve,
Dreeg
,
Bysmiel
or
Solael
.
Objectives
Speak to Byscilla, Draellus and Sagon
Pledge yourself to one of the Witch God cults
Guide
Speak to each of the cult leaders -
Byscilla, Matron of Rifts
,
Draellus, Oracle of Dreeg
, or
Sagon, Vicar of Solael
, and choose which to align with. Each will offer a different quest line, but all three faction vendors will be available to the player.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
500
5000
12000
Reputation
+100
On completion, Byscilla will offer the
In Service of Bysmiel
quest, Draellus
In Service of Dreeg
or Sagon
In Service of Solael
.
the following side quests will also be made available:
Now You Owe Me
(from
Riggs
)
Tomb Brothers
(from
Anorak
)
Good Aspirants are Difficult to Find
(from
Keisen
)
Quest Log
Quest log
The Emissary explained that the camp is a gathering of those faithful to the Witch Gods.
They're preparing for a battle of some sort and each of the three have requested your assistance.
However, you must choose one to pledge your loyalty to. Speak with the leader of each camp and choose your path forward.
Objectives:
Speak to Byscilla, Draellus and Sagon
Pledge yourself to one of the Witch God cults

in the

======================================================================
PAGE: Lumber for the Legion
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Lumber_for_the_Legion
======================================================================

Lumber for the Legion
Quest Info
Given by:
Sergeant Serriv
Location:
Homestead
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
?
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Scrap
Lumber for the Legion is an
Act 3
side quest offered by Sergeant Serriv in
Homestead
after completing
The Aetherial Farm
and gaining Friendly status with
The Black Legion
.
Completing this quest results in the repair of a building in the southwest corner of Homestead.
Background
Homestead is running low on Building supplies and Serriv asks you to take care of the Chthonic spawn that has overrun the nearby lumber mill.
Objectives
Clear out Gryver's Mill in the Blood Grove (0/18)
Return to Sergeant Serriv in Homestead
Guide
Seargant Serrive is located under  a small tent on on the ramparts of Homestead. After accepting the quest, make your way to
Gryver's Mill
, southwest of the
Blood Grove
Rift. The Chthonic consist of Harbingers and Devourers and can be found easily, clustered around a  building. After destroying them return to Segeant Serriv for the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
12000
38000
75000
Black Legion
Reputation
+100
Item
Scrap (3)
Quest Log
Quest log
Homestead is running low on building supplies, particularly lumber, but there are still many repairs that require attention. Sergeant Serriv of the Black Legion has pointed out that there is an abandoned lumber mill in the Blood Grove called Gryver's Mill. However, it is overrun with Chthonic spawn. She has asked Captain Somer for assistance in this matter, but the Captain believes the casualties would be too great for too little gain; but you are not under the Captain's command. If you clear out the lumber mill in the Blood Grove, then the Black Legion can send in guards to keep it secure. To enter the Blood Grove, head north out of Homestead.
Objectives:
Clear out Gryver's Mill in the Blood Grove (0/18)
You have cleared out the Chthonians rampaging through Gryver's Mill. Inform Sergeant Serriv in Homestead of your success.
Objectives:
Return to Sergeant Serriv in Homestead
Map Exact Location
Location of Lumber for the Legion quest

======================================================================
PAGE: Mad Ramblings
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Mad_Ramblings
======================================================================

Mad Ramblings
Quest Info
Given by:
Ivonda
Location:
Steelcap District
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
-
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 6
side
quest
, offered by
Ivonda
in the
Steelcap District
Resistance Hideout.
Ivonda appears to have lost her mind, but tells you she has also lost a note. She suggests you might find it for her.
Objectives
Acquire Ivonda's Memory
Bring Ivonda's Memory to her at the Resistance Hideout
Guide
The
Ivonda's Memory
quest item can be found in a chest in the northernmost tip of
Malmouth Harbor
, inside a house. The chest that contains the item will not spawn unless the quest from Ivonda has been accepted. To note you will also pick up Ivonda's Memory Clippings, a Lore item.
The memory can be returned to Ivonda immediately, or the player can first follow the clues by using the clippings to a secret treasure.
Returning the quest item right away will earn Ivonda's thanks and the reward of a single loot chest
Ivonda's Gift
. This chest will contain an Epic or Legendary item, and will spawn to the northeast of her, near some tents. (The player will have to leave the area and return for the chest to appear).
If the player decides to investigate Ivonda's secret, the clues in the clippings note will lead to the
Tomb of Herald Mathis
. There, a
Loose Torch
can be activated (it is the only unlit torch in the dungeon, at the beginning of the level). This will open a secret door leading to a Crypt Entrance. and
Ivonda’s Hideaway
, a storage room with several treasure chests that contain rare items. The
A Mad Stash
achievement
can be earned upon entering this storage room.
The note can then be returned to Ivonda after claiming the treasure to complete the quest but
Ivonda's Gift
will not spawn. The different dialogue options are for flavor only and will not affect the ending of the quest.
If you do not desire or already have the achievement, you can trigger the torch and enter the hidden area without entering the crypt. If you then riftgate out you can turn the quest in and receive
Ivonda's Gift
, and return to your riftgate to loot the crypt.
Note Location
Torch lcoation
Torch lcoation on map
Rewards
If you return the quest item right away:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
17000
32000
70000
Malmouth Resistance
Reputation
+250
If you Investigate Ivonda's secret:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
17000
32000
70000
Quest Log
Quest log
Ivonda is a survivor at the Resistance Hideout in Malmouth, but she doesn't seem to quite be all there. She was rambling on about some treasure she stashed away before the attacks, but she's forgotten where. You can help her by finding whatever reminder she had left for herself, but where is that even?
Objectives:
Acquire Ivonda's Memory
Bring Ivonda's Memory to her at the Resistance Hideout

The Cult of Ch'thon has been expanding its reach and their activities in Darkvale have been tolerated for too long. One of the cult's more prominent members, Bolvar the Bloodbinder has been spotted to the north, in Blood Grove. Father Kymon wishes him eliminated as the vermin he is. End his life for the good of us all.

PAGE: Malmouth, the Fallen City

Malmouth, the Fallen City
Quest Info
Given by:
Ulgrim
Location:
Lone Watch
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Along the Void's Edge
Unlocks:
Someone on the Inside
Bring Out Your Dead
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 6
main
quest
, offered by
Ulgrim
in
Lone Watch
after completing
Along the Void's Edge
.
Having made it through the Void to the outskirts of Malmouth, Ulgrim says the nearby Riftgate must be secured before searching for survivors in Malmouth.
Objectives
Secure a riftgate outside of Malmouth
Speak to Ulgrim outside Malmouth
Enter the Malmouth Sewers and Search for Survivors
Speak with Ulgrim in the Malmouth Sewers
Guide
Reach the
Malmouth Outskirts
riftgate and defeat the waves of Aetherials to activate it. The entrance to the
Malmouth Sewers
is a short distance from the riftgate; Survivors in the form of the
Malmouth Resistance
can be found at the end of the sewers. Speak to
Captain Wilfor
and tell him the Black Legion is on it's way; Ulgrim will then appear through the riftgate.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
3800
75000

Ulgrim will then offer the

Quest log
Ulgrim is still in no state to travel but you need to reach the city of Malmouth. Make your way through the outskirts of Malmouth and look for the entrance of Malmouth to the north. A riftgate there should suffice as a rally point, clear any nearby threats and lock it down.
Objectives:
Secure a riftgate outside of Malmouth
The riftgate outside Malmouth is cleared but the bridge into the city can only be raised from the far side of the river. You need to find another way into the city. Speak with Ulgrim and find out if he knows another way in.
Objectives:
Speak to Ulgrim outside Malmouth
Ulgrim suggested taking the sewers into the city. Just down river from the bridge is a sewer outlet that leads into the underbelly of Malmouth. Before the Grim Dawn, this route was used to smuggle contraband in and out of the Candle District. Use the sewer entrance to enter the city and search for any survivors that might know what's happening behind the city walls.
Objectives:
Enter the Malmouth Sewers and Search for Survivors
After scouring the city's sewers you've come across a group of refugees. They're using an old pumping station as a place to hide from the terrors up on the surface. Report to Ulgrim outside the refugee camp to figure out your next move.

Paying Debts
Quest Info
Given by:
Riggs
Location:
Conclave of the Three

The Forgotten God

Paying Debts is an
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Riggs
after completing
Deeper in Debt
and
The Forgotten God
. The quest leads the player to the
Tomb of the Heretic
"Roguelike" Dungeon, although it can be entered without accepting the quest.
Riggs has heard of an artifact called the Iris of Eternal Night, which lies deep in the Tomb of the Heretic. He asks you to retrieve it for him to repay the debt owed to him.
Note that, if the player refuses to work for Riggs, he will issue a death threat, and his "Associates" can then be periodically encountered throughout Act 7 until the quest is accepted.
Objectives
Obtain the First Seal of Morgoneth
Obtain the Second Seal of Morgoneth
Obtain the Third Seal of Morgoneth
Open the way to the Lost Oasis
Defeat Morgoneth at the Tomb of the Heretic (Requires Skeleton Key)
Claim the Iris of Eternal Night
Deliver the Iris to Riggs at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
The
First Seal of Morgoneth
is found on the third level of the
Maw of Enaht
and drops from the boss creature,
Gurblix the Digested
.
The
Second Seal
is found in the
Forlorn Bastion
, which is accessed via a secret path south of the
Korvan Sands
Rift Gate at the two Griffon Statues. It drops from the Boss,
Jarinthor the Sandstorm
.
The
Third Seal
is found in the
Howling Depths
, accessed via a secret path in the
Howling Chasm
. The seal drops from
Hallanx the Forgotten
.
With all three Seals, The
Tomb Entrance
in the
Valley of the Chosen
can be unlocked. This leads to the
Path of the Damned
, the
Lost Oasis
and then the
Tomb of the Heretic
.
Grand Magus Morgoneth
is found at the end of the third level, and the
Iris of Eternal Night
can be recovered from a chest in the treasure room after Morgoneth is defeated.
The Seals and Iris can also be collected independently of the quest and turned in later.
Location of First Seal
Location of Second Seal
Location of Third Seal
Tomb Entrance location
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
30000
80000
150000
Item
Random Epic Accessory
Random Legendary Accessory
Quest Log
Quest log
You owe a debt to Riggs and he's finally ready to get his end of the bargain.
As you'd expect, Riggs does not have a simple request. He's informed you of a Lost Oasis beyond the Valley of the Chosen, where a powerful artifact known as the Iris of Eternal Night lies hidden.
However, the ancient Korvan people had sealed it away centuries ago and the key was scattered to the sands. Riggs has knowledge of the first piece, but the texts are profoundly cryptic: so that the darkness of Morgoneth may never know the light of the Eldritch Sun, the way forward has been fed to the devouring sands.
Riggs has left the rest to you. Acquire the Focusing Iris and your debt will be considered repaid.
Objectives:
Obtain the First Seal of Morgoneth
Obtain the Second Seal of Morgoneth
Obtain the Third Seal of Morgoneth
Open the way to the Lost Oasis
The way to the Lost Oasis has been unsealed. You now have the means to seek out Morgoneth and claim his Iris, thus clearing you of your debt to Riggs.
Proceed through the Path of the Damned and find the entrance to the Tomb of the Heretic. Beware of what you may find inside, for the tomb was sealed with good reason.
Endure its dangers and make your way to the Conduit of Eternal Night, where the dark sorcerer Morgoneth awaits.
This task will require a Skeleton Key.
Objectives:
Defeat Morgoneth at the Tomb of the Heretic
You have triumphed over the darkness swelling within the Tomb of the Heretic. The way to the Iris Riggs demands has opened.
Claim the Iris at the Tomb of the Heretic and return it to Riggs at the Vanguard of the Three.
Objectives:
Claim the Iris of Eternal Night
Deliver the Iris to Riggs at the Conclave of the Three

Rift gate.
Quest Log
A group of survivors in New Harbor are being forced to work for Cronley's gang, and the quota for their deliveries keeps increasing. Alicia says her people have fallen behind in collecting scrap, and fear the repercussions. She asks you to collect the missing scrap in the village's stead.
Objectives
Collect Scrap (5/5)
Deliver the Scrap to Silas at New Harbor
Return to Alicia at New Harbor
Background
When talking to Silas you can choose to deal with him in one of three ways:
Give him the Scrap. Talk to Alicia again for the reward.
Bribe Silas to leave New Harbor. Pay him 2500 Iron and he will be only too happy to move on.
Kill Silas. You will then need to fight him. Speak to Alicia afterwards. (Note that this option will provoke retaliation, killing everyone in New Harbor except the children in the follow-on quest).
Alternatively, kill Darius Cronley before speaking to Silas and Silas will flee. Speaking to Alicia will then immediately complete the quest.
Rewards

(3)

8000
22000

For the Children
.
Quest Log
Quest log
Alicia from New Harbor in Old Arkovia. Her village is being extorted by the nearby bandits and the quota for their deliveries keeps increasing. With her people spread thin trying to collect enough fish for the tribute, they have fallen behind on their scrap collecting. If they do not deliver enough scrap to Silas, their overseer, he will undoubtedly execute someone. Alicia was very clear that no harm should come to Silas as she fears retribution. She has asked you to collect the missing scrap in the village's stead. The bandits have a stronghold on the Four Hills nearby that should have scrap.
Objectives:
Collect Scrap (5/5)
Deliver the Scrap to Silas at New Harbor.
You have delivered the scrap to Silas, ensuring that New Harbor does not suffer the wrath of the bandits. You should let Alicia know that Silas is appeased.
Objectives:
Return to Alicia at New Harbor
You have bribed Silas to leave New Harbor alone. You should let Alicia know that the outlaws will leave them alone from now on.
Objectives:
Return to Alicia at New Harbor
You have opted to slay Silas rather than perpetrating the extortion happening at New Harbor. Kill Silas and end his tyranny over the fishermen.
Objectives:
Kill Silas
You have slain Silas, liberating New Harbor of the bandit influence. You should let Alicia know of your actions.
Objectives:
Return to Alicia at New Harbor
You have slain Cronley and scattered his gang. Silas fled before you had a chance to deal with him. Speak to Alicia about the good news.
Objectives:
Return to Alicia at New Harbor

-

This is an
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Vorak
in the
Vanguard of the Three
.
Korvaak's zealots are trying to release an eldritch monstrosity imprisoned within the Tomb of Ariath. Vorak proposes to release it first, and destroy it before it can gather strength.
Objectives
Destroy the Eastern Conduit
Destroy the Northern Conduit
Destroy the Western Conduit
Slay the Duskreaper
Speak with Vorak at the Vanguard of the Three
Guide
The
Tomb of Ariath
has a single entrance in the
Valley of the Chosen
. Destroying the three Binding Conduits will cause

to spawn in the central area. Defeat it and return to Vorak.

Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
4000
16000
40000
Iron
8000
12000
24000
Cult of Bysmiel
Reputation

Quest Log
Quest log
Bysmiel's web brings word of a peculiar gathering of Korvaak's zealots in the Valley of the Chosen in the Infernal Wastes to the northwest.
There are whispers of an eldritch monstrosity that was once imprisoned within the Tomb of Ariath. Vorak speculates that they intend to release this creature and use it as a weapon.
Within the tomb are three conduits said to bind the creature there. If they are broken, the beast will be unleashed.
Vorak has a rather perverse strategy to deal with this. Rather than thwarting the zealots, he suggests that you release the creature and slay it before it has a chance to recover from centuries of imprisonment. Then Korvaak's minions will have one less resource to draw upon.
Find the Tomb of Ariath in the Valley of the Chosen, destroy the conduits, release the beast and slay it before the enemy has a chance to claim it.
Objectives:
Destroy the Eastern Conduit
Destroy the Northern Conduit
Destroy the Western Conduit
The three conduits are destroyed, enter the heart of the Tomb of Ariath, in the Infernal Wastes, and slay the creature contained within.
Objectives:
Slay the Duskreaper
The Duskreaper is no more.
Return to Vorak at the Vanguard of the Three to report on your success.
Objectives:
Speak with Vorak at the Vanguard of the Three

side quest offered by
Brother Elluvius
in
Kymon's Sanctuary
after completing
The Prophet's Call
.
Before Kymon's Chosen can trust you completely, you must demonstrate that you have no alignment with the Cult of Ch'thon. Brother Elluvius asks you to collect
Chthonic Seals of Binding
that they may be destroyed.
Objectives
Gather Chthonic Seals of Binding (0/3)

Guide
The seals drop regularly from Chthonic Cultists in
The Blood Grove
and throughout the game.
When you have collected three, return them to Brother Elluvius.

Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
1000
35000
67000
Reputation
+250
Brother Elluvius will then offer the
Making a Stand
Quest Log
Quest log
The vile Cult of Ch'thon has long been an agent of corruption and chaos within Cairn, but their activities since the Grim Dawn are reaching catastrophic levels. Even now they summon creatures from the Void using their heathen blood rituals. These rituals must be stopped at any cost. The cultists are known to use special Seals of Binding when practicing their art. If you truly are interested in Father Kymon's mission, then you must recover these Seals and bring them to Brother Elluvius at Sorrow's Bastion so that they can be incinerated in Empyrion's fire.
Objectives:
Gather Chthonic Seals of Binding (0/3)
