======================================================================
PAGE: Quests
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Quests
======================================================================

Quests in Grim Dawn provide objectives for the player and allow the story of the game to advance.
Main quests
are integral to the game's plot, and completion is necessary for the game to progress.
Side-quests
are usually optional missions that can provide valuable rewards and experience, as well as encouraging exploration of the game world.
Completing quests can grant
rewards
such as
Experience
points,
Faction Reputation
,
items
, Skill and Attribute points and extra Inventory Bags.
Below are listed all available quests.

Secret Quests
The base
Grim Dawn
game, as well as the
Ashes of Malmouth
and
Forgotten Gods
Expansions, each have a secret quest. They are intended to be discovered through following cryptic clues left for the player. Although each quest lacks explicit objectives and text, they lead to "Easter Egg" secret areas with secret bosses and items.

Lokarr's Secret Quest

======================================================================
PAGE: Reaping What You Sow
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Reaping_What_You_Sow
======================================================================

Reaping What You Sow
Quest Info
Given by:
Captain Somer
Location:
Homestead
Faction:
The Black Legion
Homestead
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Blood Harvest
Unlocks:
The Inquisitor
Rewards:
XP, Item Reputation
Reaping What You Sow is an
Act 3
main quest, offered by
Captain Somer
in
Homestead
after completing the
Blood Harvest
quest.
This quest leads to the final boss fight for Act 3.
Objectives
Slay Karroz, Sigil of Ch'thon (0/1)
Collect Karroz's Tome (0/1)
Return to Captain Somer in Homestead
Guide
Karroz is located at the end of the second level of
Darkvale Gate
, which lies beyond the
Village of Darkvale
. Defeat him, collect the
Karroz's Tome
quest item and then return to Captain Somer.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
16000
40000
79000
Reputation
+500 (Black Legion)
+500 (Homestead)
Item
Random Epic item (accessory)
Captain Somer will then offer the
The Inquisitor
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Captain Somer is determined to reconnect her forces with the bulk of the Legion to the north. Her scouts have uncovered the identity of the cult's leader in the region, one by the name Karroz, the Sigil of Ch'thon. He has entrenched himself at the Darkvale Gate, far north of Sorrow's Bastion. The captain wishes him assassinated so that the cultist chain of command is crippled and the Legion can advance on their position.
Objectives:
Slay Karroz, Sigil of Ch'thon
You have slain Karroz and uncovered the truth regarding the cultist presence here. You should report back to Captain Somer in Homestead immediately.
Objectives:
Collect Karroz's Tome
Return to Captain Somer in Homestead

Return to Inquisitor Creed
Quest Info
Given by:
n/a
Location:
n/a
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Main
Prerequisites:
The Bane of Cairn
Unlocks:
Desperate Measures
Rewards:
XP
This is a small
Act 5
main
quest
, available to characters that have finished the base game prior to installing the
Ashes of Malmouth
Expansion. It is granted automatically on commencing the Expansion to direct the player back to the main quest line.
Objectives
Speak to Inquisitor Creed at Fort Ikon
Guide
Speaking with
Inquisitor Creed
will provide several dialogue options which will initiate the Expansion cut-scene. Creed will then offer the
Desperate Measures
quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
5000
9000
15000
Quest Log
Quest log
Inquisitor Creed may have some news regarding Ulgrim's situation.
Go speak with him at Fort Ikon immediately.
Objectives:
Speak to Inquisitor Creed at Fort Ikon

======================================================================
PAGE: Rhowari Legacy
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Rhowari_Legacy
======================================================================

Rhowari Legacy
Quest Info
Given by:
Amkala
Location:
Old Arkovia
Faction:
Rovers
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Honored status
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Item, Devotion Point
Rhowari Legacy is an
Act 2
side
quest
, offered by
Amkala
after gaining Honored Faction status with the
Rovers
.
Background
Amkala tells you of the shrine to Mogdrogen, far away in the Asterkarn Mountains, which is sacred to the Rovers. The shrine has been destroyed by the Cult of Ch'thon and its pieces scattered. Amkala asks you to recover the pieces and restore the shrine.
Objectives
Find Runed Stone of Mogdrogen (0/1)
Find Spirit of Mogdrogen (0/1)
Collect Ancient Heart (0/1)
Restore the Shrine of Mogdrogen
Defeat the spawns of Ch'thon
Speak to the Avatar of Mogdrogen
Guide
Shrine location
The
Runed Stone of Mogdrogen
can be found in the
Ashen Waste
, while the
Spirit of Mogdrogen
can be found in
The Forsaken Wastes
. Both quest items have randomised spawn points and will be resting on the ground. A Star icon on the minimap will indicate your proximity.
The
Ancient Heart
can be farmed for from Beasts or retrieved from the player stash.
Take the three items to the ruined shrine of Mogdrogen, located on the eastern edge of the
Asterkarn Valley
. Placing the items in the shrine will  release three waves of chthonic creatures. When these are defeated the
Avatar of Mogdrogen
will appear. Speak to him and he will grant the reward for completing the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
16000
65000
108000
Rovers
Reputation
+1500
Devotion
1 Devotion Point
Item
2 Rare Components
Quest Log
Quest log
Far to the north, in the Asterkarn Mountains, the Cult of Ch'thon has desecrated the Shrine of Mogdrogen, a place sacred to the Rovers. Amkala has asked you to recover the parts of the shrine that had been stolen by the cultists and to restore the shrine by returning the pieces, along with an Ancient Heart, to the Shrine. The pieces are lost to the void, through rifts open in the Blood Grove, to the north of Homestead, and the Plains of Strife, north of Fort Ikon.
Objectives:
Find Runed Stone of Mogdrogen
Find Spirit of Mogdrogen
Collect Ancient Heart
Restore the Shrine of Mogdrogen
You have restored the Shrine of Mogdrogen, but the Chthonians infesting the area are manifesting themselves. Destroy them all.
Objectives:
Defeat the spawns of Ch'thon
You have cleansed the Shrine of Mogdrogen. An Avatar of Mogdrogen has appeared from the Shrine to thank you for your service. Speak to him.
Objectives:
Speak to the Avatar of Mogdrogen

Rictor's Thanks
Quest Info
Given by:
Rictor Clarke
Location:
Steelcap District
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Side Quest

Unlocks:

XP
This is a small
Act 6
side
quest
, offered by
Rictor Clarke
in the
Steelcap District
after completing the
Survivors
Quest.
Rictor is grateful you rescued Vivian, even though his own death is near. He tells you of his stash in his old shop by the docks, saying they are yours if you find them.
Objectives
Open Rictor's Stash
Guide
Rictor's Stash is found north of Rictor's position, in the Malmouth Harbor area. A
Detonation Site
revealed after Rictor tells you of his stash will uncover a secret  room in a building with a
One-Shot Chest
.
Stash Location
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
17000
32000
70000
Quest Log
Quest log
A wounded survivor named Rictor told you about his stash, hidden in a shop near the Blackiron Docks.
As he is not long for this world, he offered what he had gathered as thanks to you for taking care of Vivien.
Objectives:
Open Rictor's Stash

Rise of the Insurgence
Quest Info
Given by:
Korinia
Location:
Steelcap District
Faction:
Malmouth Resistance
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Blackiron Docks
Honored Faction Status
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 6
side
quest
, offered by
Korinia
in the
Steelcap District
Resistance Hideout after completing
The Blackiron Docks
and reaching
Honored
Faction Status with the
Malmouth Resistance
.
Objectives
Kill Dreven Cole
Kill Cyrian Marcan
Kill Alberran Rein
Speak to Korinia at the Resistance Hideout
Guide
Dreven Cole
,
Alberran Rein
and
Cyrian Marcan
can be found in the
Chamber of the High Council
, which has a single entrance in the south of
Crown Hill
.
After killing the three councilmen return to Korinia.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
40000
65000
112000
Malmouth Resistance
Reputation
+1000
Item
Epic Accessory
Legendary Accessory
Quest Log
Quest log
Even if everything living inside the Fleshworks is exterminated, there are other Aetherials actively fighting against the survivors in Malmouth. A trio of councilmen in charge of many of the operations here in Malmouth. As such, they were valuable targets for the Aetherials invading Cairn. All three had fallen to possession and turned into heavily twisted versions of their former selves. They now reside within the Chamber of the High Council, located in a tower on the south end of Crown Hill. If Malmouth is ever to be truly secure, they must be eliminated.
Objectives:
Kill Dreven Cole
Kill Cyrian Marcan
Kill Alberran Rein
You have dealt with the corrupted councilmen, as Korinia had requested. Report back to her at the Resistance Hideout.
Objectives:
Speak to Korinia at the Resistance Hideout

"Concentrated secretion from giant wasps of Old Arkovia. Widely believed to carry restorative powers."
Royal Jelly is a quest item required for the
A Royal Remedy
quest.
It can be looted from
Venomwing Queens
and
Wasp
Heroes & Bosses in and around the
Stirring Hive
,
Swarming Hive
,
Staunton Mine
, or from Wasp Nest containers.

potions
Royal Jelly Balm

Royal Jelly Essence
Royal Jelly Extract

"Part of the Shrine of Mogdrogen."

quest.

======================================================================
PAGE: Runestone of Bysmiel
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Runestone_of_Bysmiel
======================================================================

"Runestone carried by the followers of Bysmiel. There is an inscription along the edge: ...And so, by the light of the EASTERN star, the Three joined together at their Sanctum. Bound by divine blood, their quarrels put to rest. The Covenant of the Three was forged."
The Runestone of Bysmiel is a quest item used in
The Hidden Path
. It drops from the
Guardian of Bysmiel
in the Hidden Path area of the
Asterkarn Valley
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Runestone of Dreeg
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Runestone_of_Dreeg
======================================================================

"Runestone carried by the thralls of Dreeg. There is an inscription along the edge: Though the Three are now as one, it was not always so. Wary of the other's power, they quarelled across Cairn in destructive displays of Eldritch might. Mountains crumbled and RIVERS shifted, but no god emerged the victor..."
The Runestone of Dreeg is a quest item used in
The Hidden Path
. It drops from the
Guardian of Dreeg
in the Hidden Path area of
Lower Crossing
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Runestone of Solael
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Runestone_of_Solael
======================================================================

""Runestone carried by the adherents of Solael. There is an inscription along the edge: ...In the end it was Solael who looked past the carnage and saw the inevitability of their actions. In truth, none could triumph where all three were equal. He sent his loyal Attendant to speak before the rest of a resolution. They would seal a pact, there among the SWAMPY remains of their last skirmish."
The Runestone of Solael is a quest item used in
The Hidden Path
. It drops from the
Guardian of Solael
in the Hidden Path area of the
Broken Hills
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Sacred Ashes of Empyrion
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Sacred_Ashes_of_Empyrion
======================================================================

"The ashes of Archon Barthollem, devout follower of the Lightbringer."
The Sacred Ashes of Empyrion a quest item used in
The Sacred Ashes (Kymon's Chosen)
. It drops from
Malkadarr, Champion of Death's Vigil
in level 2 of the
Tomb of Archon Barthollem
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Savior
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Savior
======================================================================

Savior
Quest Info
Given by:
Nicoh Erin
Location:
Candle District
Faction:
n/a
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
none
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Item
This is a small
Act 5
side
quest
, activated when talking to
Nicoh Erin
after encountering him in the
Candle District
.
Nicoh has been protecting some children (Nissa and Timor) from the Aetherials for some time. He appears to be somewhat unhinged and resistant to help.
Objectives
Speak to Nicoh Erin at the Resistance Hideout
OR:
Kill Nicoh Erin
Speak to Nissa at the Candle District
Guide
Nicoh's Location
Nicoh and the children are found in a building in the north-west corner of the Candle District.
The result of the quest (kill or save) is random for each game session, and choice of dialogue option has no impact on how the quest ends. To change the outcome, you will need to interrupt talking with Nicoh without choosing one of the options to end the dialogue, simply walk away. Then you need to quit the game session and try again.
Rewards
Component Reward Table
Ballistic Plating
Mark of Illusions
Oleron's Blood
Purified Salt
Reinforced Shell
Resilient Plating
Wardstone
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
17000
32000
70000
Item
Random Partial Component
Quest Log
Quest log
Nicoh Erin appears to have been rescuing children from the Malmouth Candle District. You managed to convince him that the resistance can protect the children and he agreed to move them to the Sewer Hideout. You should speak to him to see how they're doing.
Objectives:
Speak to Nicoh Erin at the Resistance Hideout
Nicoh Erin claimed he was rescuing children from the Malmouth Candle District but he grew belligerent when you offered to help. He refused to move the children to safety and became violent. Do what must be done to make sure the children stay safe.
Objectives:
Kill Nicoh Erin
Nicoh Erin refused to listen to reason and take the children to safety, so you did what had to be done. Speak to the young girl Nissa in the Candle District and send the children to the Resistance Hideout.
Speak to Nissa at the Candle District

======================================================================
PAGE: Scrap
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Scrap
======================================================================

"Scrap material such as bolts, leather cords and low-grade metals that can be used to fasten together items or structures."
Scrap is a quest item that drops throughout the game from monsters and containers. It can be used as a
Crafting
item, in quests, and also to repair bridges.
Scrap is used in the following quests:
And Not a Drop to Drink
Murderers and Worse
Paying Tributes
We Need Food

======================================================================
PAGE: Seals of Binding
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Seals_of_Binding
======================================================================

Seals of Binding
Quest Info
Given by:
Master Varuuk
Location:
Bastion of the Order
Faction:
Order of Death's Vigil
Type:
side quest
Prerequisites:
Worthy of the Order
Unlocks:
A Catalyst
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Reputation
Seals of Binding is an
Act 3
side quest, offered by
Master Varuuk
in the
Bastion of the Order
after completing the
Worthy of the Order
quest.
Chthonic Seals of Binding
, used by
cultists
to stabilise
chthonic rifts
, are required by the order to aid their own ritual to bring
Malkadarr
back from the dead.
Objectives
Gather Chthonic Seals of Binding (0/3)
Bring the Seals of Binding to Master Varuuk at
Sorrow's Bastion
Guide
The seals drop regularly from Chthonic Cultists in
The Blood Grove
and throughout the game.
When you have collected three, return them to Master Varuuk to complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
11000
36000
70000
Iron
1500
7500
15000
Death's Vigil
Reputation
+250
Master Varuuk will then offer the
A Catalyst
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
The ritual involved in bringing back Malkadarr is a complicated and unstable one. The cultists in the Blood Grove use Seals of Binding to stabilize their rituals. Gather some of these Seals for Master Varuuk at Sorrow's Bastion so that the Order can use them to bring back Malkadarr's soul from beyond the veil of death.
Objectives:
Gather Chthonic Seals of Binding (0/3)
Bring the Seals of Binding to Master Varuuk at Sorrow's Bastion
Dialogue
(Immediately after completing the prerequisite quest)
Master Varuuk
You have entered the pit of despair and emerged unscathed. Impressive.
Perhaps you truly are worthy of the Order. Should you be interested, the next task is both an opportunity to strike out at the Legion's enemies and to air our cause.
[Question] What is it?
Master Varuuk
The Cult of Ch'thon is experienced in summoning rituals, something we can use to our advantage.
We will take what we need from the Cult, while crippling them in the process. Interested?
[Question] Go on.
Master Varuuk
The Cult uses Chthonic Seals of Binding to maintain the rifts into the
Void
. Many of their more powerful members carry these on their person at all times.
Should the Cult be denied these Seals, then their rituals will destabilize, denying them valuable reinforcements.
Their loss is our gain. Bring me the Seals so that we can use them to stabilize our own ritual.
[Accepts quest] I will gather the Seals.
[Refuses quest] Find someone else.
[Question] Are these the Seals you seek?
(Only available if you have already gathered the required Seals of Binding; this will accept and immediately complete the quest)
Master Varuuk
Yes, these appear to be in good shape. They will be most useful in returning Malkadarr to this world.
[Ends conversation] Perhaps another time.
[Ends conversation] Perhaps another time.

======================================================================
PAGE: Second Seal of Morgoneth
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Second_Seal_of_Morgoneth
======================================================================

"In the darkness bound, Morgoneth sought to disguise his intentions in the light of Ateph. But by the grace of the Eldritch Sun, the veil was lifted from his machinations. He served a great hunger, and hunger is all he shall ever know.
The way is shut, the heresy sealed. But should the Korvan faith be shaken once more by Morgoneth's folly, then seek the final seal deep within the howling abyss.
May no other ever set eyes upon the night's terrors."
The Second Seal of Moroneth is a quest item required to open the entrance to the
Path of the Damned
, and is needed in the
Paying Debts
quest in
Forgotten Gods
. It drops from
Jarinthar the Sandstorm
, the boss creature of the
Forlorn Bastion
.

PAGE: Secrets of the Lost
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Secrets_of_the_Lost
======================================================================

Secrets of the Lost
Quest Info
Given by:
Anasteria
Location:
Fort Ikon Prison
Faction:
The Outcast
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Wrath of the Beast
Unlocks:
Black Heart of the Void
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
Secrets of the Lost is an
Act 4
Faction side quest offered by
Anasteria
in the
Fort Ikon Prison
, after completing the
Wrath of the Beast
quest.
Anasteria seeks to access the powerful divination magic of Old Arkovia, and believes recovering an ancient tome from the depths of the Steps of Torment will be of use.
The crafting of a
Skeleton Key
is required to complete this quest.
Objectives
Acquire the Archive of Fates Untold
Bring the Archive to Anasteria
Guide
The
Shade of Elnadrin
can be found on level 4 of the
Steps of Torment
. He will drop the
Archive of Fates Untold
when slain.
Note that it is necessary to craft a
Skeleton Key
to complete this quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
16000
44000
81000
Reputation
+1500 (The Outcast)
-200 (Black Legion)
Item
2 Rare Partial Components
Anasteria will then offer the
Black Heart of the Void
side-quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Anasteria is interested in lost artifacts, particularly from the Arkovian era. She has implored you to enter the Steps of Torment in the Broken Hills, the section beyond the sealed ancient gates, and banish the skeletal fiend known as the Shade of Elnadrin. Take its tome, known as the Archive of Fates Untold, and bring it to Anasteria at the Fort Ikon Prison.
Objectives:
Acquire the Archive of Fates Untold
Bring the Archive to Anasteria

======================================================================
PAGE: Securing Burrwitch
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Securing_Burrwitch
======================================================================

Securing Burrwitch
Quest Info
Given by:
Captain John Bourbon
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
None
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Helping Out
Unlocks:
The Warden
Rewards:
XP
This is an
Act 1
quest offered by
Captain John Bourbon
after completing the
Helping Out
quest.
Background
The dead are concentrated heavily in
Burrwitch Village
and Bourbon wants to investigate further to find out why. He asks you to capture the riftgate in order to secure a foothold in the area.
Objectives
Secure the Portal in Burrwitch Village
Slay all Aetherials swarming around the Burrwitch Riftgate
Report back to John Bourbon
Guide
Make your way through the Burrwitch Outskirts until you come to the Burrwitch Village entrance; the Riftgate can be easily found just inside. Before you can activate it however, you must face 3 waves of monsters which will spawn around the riftgate, each group larger than the last. When you have defeated the final wave, the riftgate will be secure.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
350
22000
54000
Bourbon will then offer the next main quest,
The Warden
.
Quest Log
Quest log
Reconaissance data from John Bourbon's scouts indicates that Burrwitch must be critical to Aetherial operations in the area.
Perhaps the mastermind behind all this tragedy is hiding somewhere in the village. Before you can search for it, however, you must secure a means of entry.
Find a riftgate within Burrwitch and secure it for the Survivors. Burrwitch is located to the north of Devil's Crossing, past Wightmire.
Objectives:
Secure the Portal in Burrwitch Village
The Burrwitch Riftgate is surrounded by Aetherials. You will need to clear them out before you can secure it.
Objectives:
Slay all Aetherials swarming around the Burrwitch Riftgate
With the Burrwitch riftgate secure, return to Captain John Bourbon in Devil's Crossing for further instructions.
Objectives:
Report back to John Bourbon

Seeking the Order
Quest Info
Given by:
Haruuv
Location:
Homestead
Faction:
Order of Death's Vigil
Type:
side quest
Prerequisites:
Allies Among the Ashes
Unlocks:
Worthy of the Order
Rewards:
XP
Seeking the Order is an
Act 3
side quest offered by
Haruuv
in
Homestead
, after choosing to side with the
Order of Death's Vigil
in the
Allies Among the Ashes
quest.
Objectives
Speak to Master Varuuk
Guide
Master Varuuk
is located in the
Bastion of the Order
, which can be found just to the left of the
Sorrow's Bastion
Riftgate.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
8000
32000
48000
Varuuk will then offer the
Worthy of the Order
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Haruuv, a representative of the Order of Death's Vigil, has asked you to travel to a crypt near Sorrow's Bastion, where the Order has its sanctum. To reach the crypt, follow the road north out of Homestead, through the Fallow Fields. When you've reached the ruins of Sorrow's Bastion, look west for the crypt entrance. Once inside, speak to Master Varuuk.
Objectives:
Speak to Master Varuuk

Service Beyond Death
Quest Info
Given by:
The Keeper of Tomes
Location:
Bastion of the Order
Faction:
Order of Death's Vigil
Type:
side quest
Prerequisites:
The Sacred Ashes
Unlocks:
The Search for Uroboruuk
Rewards:
Service Beyond Death is a side quest offered by
The Keeper of Tomes
in the
Bastion of the Order
, after completing
The Sacred Ashes
and gaining Respected faction reputation with the order.
Now that the Order has everything necessary to undertake the resurrection of Malkadarr, the ritual can begin.
Objectives
Assist in the resurrection of Malkadarr
Speak to the Keeper of Tomes
Guide
Initiating the quest unlocks the
Chamber of Souls
, the sealed section of the Bastion of the Order, just east from where you activate the quest. On entering the area and speaking to the npc within, several waves of undead will appear which the player will need to defeat. This includes the shade of
Noveria Stormfire
, previously slain in the
A Catalyst
quest.
After the last wave the ritual will come to an end and Malkadarr will appear outside the Chamber. Speak to the Keeper of Tomes for the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
15000
43000
79000
Death's Vigil
Reputation
+1000
Item
Random Epic Weapon
The Keeper will then offer the next quest,
The Search for Uroboruuk
, once the player has reached
Honored
faction status with the Order.
Quest Log
Quest log
You have gathered all the necessary materials for Malkadarr's resurrection. Often times, malignant spirits will gather around such a ritual, making it dangerous for the participants, so the Keeper of Tomes wishes for you to watch over the ritual at Sorrow's Bastion while the necromancers perform the Rite of Resurrection.
Objectives:
Assist in the resurrection of Malkadarr
The ritual was a success and Malkadarr walks Cairn once again. Speak to the Keeper of Tomes at Sorrow's Bastion of your success.
Objectives:
Speak to the Keeper of Tomes
Dialogue
(
Before accepting the quest
)
The Keeper of Tomes
We now have everything we need to perform the Rite of Resurrection. Your loyalty and assistance have earned you the right to see Malkadarr return to this world.
Do you wish to join us?
What does this ritual entail?
The ritual will be dangerous, of that I can assure you. Malignant spirits will be drawn to it like moths to the flame. I need you to dispatch anything that tries to interfere.
Join us at the Chamber of Souls, its doors have been unlocked to you. Keep the chamber clear of spirits so that Malkadarr can find his way back to us.
I will assist you in the ritual.
I will have no part in this.
What happens if I fail?
Then we risk allowing another to enter Malkadarr's vessel.
Should that happen, we will be forced to destroy it, and Malkadarr will be forever lost to us.
Do not fail us.
I will assist you in the ritual.
I will have no part in this.
I'm afraid not.
(
Talking to the Keeper of Tomes before finishing the ritual
)
The Keeper of Tomes
Please head over to the Chamber of Souls.
Your assistance is required.
Where should I go?
The Chamber of Souls is right here in our sanctum. Join the ritual and secure Malkadarr's soul from beyond!
I will go there now.
I will.
(
Talking to Soulkeeper Kaandris before starting the ritual
)
Soulkeeper Kaandris
Everything is in place.
The ritual will require my complete attention, so it falls on you to keep the dead contained while I search for Malkadarr. I will be shielded from their presence, but should any of the spirits remain when the ritual is finished, the results could be disastrous.
Are you ready to begin?
What do I have to do?
The ritual will draw spirits to itself like a beacon in the darkness. Make sure that whatever comes through the veil is not around for long.
You must keep the room clear so that it is Malkadarr we bring back, and not some wayward soul.
I am ready. (Begin Ritual)
I'm not ready to begin yet.
I am ready. (Begin Ritual)
I'm not ready to begin yet.

You have done the Order a great service.
What of Malkadarr?
He shall resume his duties under the Keeper of Tomes, his knowledge preserved for future generations.
Farewell.
You're welcome.

Talking to Malkadarr, Champion of Death's Vigil after finishing the ritual

Malkadarr
So, it is you I must thank for my resurrection?
So what happens now?
That is for the Keeper to decide. I am hers to command.
Are you her slave?
A strong way to put it, but in a sense.
Whatever the Keeper wishes shall be done.
Why would you agree to this?
To gain access to the innermost secrets of Necromancy, I had to agree to this binding, so that all I learn is not lost should I perish.
It was a price worth paying; an honor, not a curse.
Will you obey me?
*Malkadarr cackles*
You may have participated in my return, but you are not the one who performed the binding.
I see.
A steep price for knowledge.
Sounds like a terrible fate.
I shall speak to her then.
Welcome back, Malkadarr.

His continued existence is tied to my will. For as long as I demand it, he shall serve his duties.
That seems wrong.
Is it so wrong to sacrifice yourself wholly in the name of a greater cause? Malkadarr knew what was at stake when he joined the first circle and learned its secrets.

======================================================================
PAGE: Skeleton Key
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Skeleton_Key
======================================================================

"If the stories are to be believed, this key will open nearly any ancient door".
Skeleton Keys
are items used to unlock the roguelike sections of various
challenge dungeons
.
Obtaining
From quests:
One Skeleton Key, along with
the blueprint
, is given by
Kalderos
upon completing the quest
Descent into Torment
.
One Skeleton Key is given by
Mogdrogen
upon starting the quest
Cleanse the Corruption
.
One Skeleton Key is given by
Riggs
upon starting the quest
Paying Debts
.
From crafting:
A
blacksmith
can craft a Skeleton Key if the
blueprint
and the resources are available.
An
inventor
can produce a Skeleton Key when
Dismantling
Epic or Legendary items.
Usage
Skeleton Keys are used to open the sealed entrances to
challenge dungeons
. The key is consumed upon use.
Challenge dungeons that require a Skeleton Key to open are:
levels 4 and 5 of the
Steps of Torment
.
levels 2-4 of the
Bastion of Chaos
.
Port Valbury
.
The
Feral Thicket
in the
Ancient Grove
.
AoM
The
Tomb of the Heretic
in the
Lost Oasis
.
FG
Masteries

PAGE: Slith Necklace

"Carried by Slith Shamans, for only they know what."
Slith Necklaces are Quest Items used in the quest
That Good Old Slith Charm
.
The necklaces can drop from
Slith Shamans
.

PAGE: Tale of Two Blacksmiths

Tale of Two Blacksmiths
Quest Info
Given by:
Duncan
Location:
Burrwitch Outskirts
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Unlocks:
Blacksmith
Rewards:
XP
This is an
Act 1
quest offered by
Duncan
when you find him in the
Burrwitch Outskirts
. Depending on how you finish this quest, you will unlock the
Blacksmith
services of either
Duncan
or
Angrim
. Read about the
Choice of Blacksmiths
to help decide for each character.
Note: Once you reach Elite difficulty, you may side with a different blacksmith. This allows your character to have access to both blacksmiths by selecting the appropriate difficulty.
Background
Duncan asks you if you can locate someone. His master Angrim left the camp earlier in search of a group of survivors "more worthy" of his smithing talents. Without his master's forging hammer, Duncan cannot provide proper equipment to the refugees. He promises to join you at Devil's Crossing if you can recover the hammer.
Objectives
Speak to Angrim in the Burrwitch Outskirts
Guide
Angrim can be found in a secluded area some way to the east of the Burrwitch Outskirts riftgate. Talking to him will present you with several dialogue options.
Side with Duncan.
You can either talk Angrim into handing over the Malleum Menhir or fight and kill him for it. In either case, deliver the forge hammer to Duncan at the refugee camp once you have it. Duncan will agree to join you in
Devil's Crossing
when his work at the refugee camp is finished. Return to the prison and speak to Duncan for the reward.
Side with Angrim
. You can  invite him back to Devil's Crossing. A rift will be opened for him to travel to Devil's Crossing where he will set up shop inside the prison.
Rewards
Side with Duncan:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
800
22000
55000
Side with Angrim:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
350
22000
55000
Quest Log
Quest log
Duncan, a young blacksmith at a refugee camp in the Burrwitch Outskirts, has implored you to seek out his master, Angrim. Angrim left the camp recently, heading northeast, to seek out what he called "more capable" individuals. Duncan wishes to help the refugees survive by providing them with proper equipment, but for this he needs the Malleum Menhir, an ancient forging hammer in the possession of his master.
If you recover the hammer from Angrim, then Duncan can make the lives of the refugees easier, after which he will gladly join you at Devil's Crossing.
Objectives:
Speak to Angrim in the Burrwitch Outskirts
You have acquired Malleum Menhir from Angrim. Duncan is eagerly awaiting its delivery at the refugee camp near the riftgate in the Burrwitch Outskirts.
Objectives:
Collect Malleum Menhir from Angrim
Deliver Malleum Menhir to Duncan at the refugee camp
You have decided that killing Angrim is the only way you'll get Malleum Menhir from him. Kill Angrim to claim the forging hammer, then deliver it to Duncan at the refugee camp near the riftgate in Burrwitch Outskirts.
Objectives:
Kill Angrim and recover Malleum Menhir
Deliver Malleum Menhir to Duncan at the refugee camp
You have convinced Duncan to join your cause at Devil's Crossing. Speak to him inside the prison, once he arrives from the refugee camp.
Objectives:
Speak to Duncan in Devil's Crossing
You have convinced Angrim to join your cause at Devil's Crossing. Speak to him inside the prison.
Objectives:
Speak to Angrim in Devil's Crossing

The Aetherial Farm is an
Act 3
main
quest
, and is offered by
Captain Somer
after completing
The Black Legion's Finest
.
Background
The Aetherials are occupying an area of farmland known as
The Gruesome Harvest
, and collecting corpses on which to conduct their resurrection techniques. For some time now the barn in the area has been giving off a blinding light both day and night, until now. Somer believes that whatever the Aetherials are planning is almost complete and must be stopped before it is too late.
Objectives
Destroy the Aetherial Amalgamation (1/1)
Return to Captain Somer in Homestead
Guide
The Gruesome Harvest is located to the west of Homestead, at the end of the Rotting Croplands. You will come to a gated enclosure full of Aetherials; it is best to lure them out through the gate to thin them out. Inside the enclosure lies a barn holding an Aetherial boss creature,
The Amalgamation
. Destroy it and report back to Captain Somer for the reward.

Captain Somer of the Black Legion has sent you on a special operation to disrupt Aetherial activity near Homestead. You are to cross the Infested Farms and Rotten Croplands to the west of Homestead in order to enter the Gruesome Harvest. There you will find the Aetherials entrenched and in the process of creating some sort of sick monstrosity within one of the barns. Destroy the abomination before it can wreck havoc across the farmlands.

======================================================================
PAGE: The Aetherial Witch
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/The_Aetherial_Witch
======================================================================

The Aetherial Witch
Quest Info
Given by:
Captain Reave
Location:
Fort Ikon
Faction:
The Black Legion
The Outcast
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
N/A
Unlocks:
Cult Activity
Power of our Enemies
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 4
side quest offered by
Captain Reave
after completing the
Betrayal at Fort Ikon
quest.
The Legion is harboring a Possessed witch named Anasteria, and Inquisitor Creed has ordered her not to be harmed. Captain Reave however blames her witchcraft for the betrayal by Commander Lucius, and asks you to deal with her.
Objectives
Speak to Anasteria at the Fort Ikon Prison
Optional:
Slay Anasteria
Report to Captain Reave at Fort Ikon
Guide
Anasteria
is located in the
Fort Ikon Prison
. Talk to her and decide whether to kill her or let her live.
Benefits to letting her live
Unlock the
Outcast
faction, equipment, bounty table, and quest line, which increases Outcast reputation and decreases
Black Legion
reputation.
Access to some of the best Aether Resistance augments in the game, able to be applied on weapons and armor.
Benefits to killing her
Unlock the
Fort Ikon Prison
dungeon with Anasteria as a boss at the end and a great source of
The Black Legion
reputation farming, Elite mobs, and gear.
Access to
Outcast's Secret
, a Legendary helm that only drops from Anasteria.
Notes
As with most quests, your choices in one difficulty can be different in the next. However, with Anasteria it is a little different. Changing your mind with her in a new difficulty will cause your Outcast reputation to reset to 0 (Tolerated) across all difficulties. This also means that, while she may still be friendly in The Fort Ikon Prison in a difficulty she was befriended, her augments and equipment will no longer be available in any difficulty.
Outcast reputation is gained very quickly, as the quests from Anasteria have very high reputation rewards, but they also decrease Black Legion reputation at the same time. This reputation loss is easily offset by running a Black legion Bounty and using a
Writ of the Black Legion
.
The Fort Ikon Prison (as an enemy dungeon after killing Anasteria) is a short, one-level dungeon packed with Elites and an end boss (Anasteria), making it an excellent spot for farming gear.
One option is to kill Anasteria in Normal and Elite difficulties and befriend her in Ultimate. This will provide very useful 70+ gear and augments to your already-high-level character, along with most likely being Revered with The Black Legion by the time you reach Ultimate. Access to the Outcast's Aether Resistance augments can be useful; the
Order of Death's Vigil
and
The Black Legion
quartermasters have similar augments, but with less Aether Resistance.
A second option is to befriend her in Normal and Elite difficulties and kill her in Ultimate. This will cause her dungeon to be unlocked at the highest difficulty that will provide you with the best possible loot. Also, Anasteria gains strength as your reputation decreases by killing her, making her fight tougher, but allowing easy-to-find Nemesis mobs to spawn inside once you reach Nemesis reputation.
A third option is to befriend her in all difficulties and then, using a separate character, kill her in all difficulties. This will provide you with all of her dungeon's loot which can be shared in the Item Transfer Stash.
Rewards
Spare Anasteria:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
8000
20000
50000
Reputation
-250 (Black Legion)
+250 (The Outcast)
Anasteria will then offer the
Power of our Enemies
quest.
Kill Anasteria:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
16000
40000
100000
Reputation
+1000 (Black Legion)
Captain Reave will then offer the
Cult Activity
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Captain Reave of the Black Legion has determined that all of the Legion's recent troubles stem from the arrival of an aetherial witch in their midst. He is under strict orders not to harm Anasteria, but you are under no such obligation. Head into the Fort Ikon prison and deal with this traitorous wretch.
Objectives:
Speak to Anasteria at the Fort Ikon Prison
You have spoken with Anasteria and agreed with Reave's assessment. Anasteria needs to die.
Objectives:
Slay Anasteria
You have slain the Aetherial witch Anasteria. Report back to Captain Reave at Fort Ikon of your success.
Objectives:
Report to Captain Reave at Fort Ikon

The Coven's Walls
Quest Info
Given by:
Garradia
Location:
Coven's Refuge
Faction:
Coven of Ugdenbog
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
A Witch's Bargain
Unlocks:
Pruning The Weeds
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 5
side
quest
, offered by
Garradia
in
Coven's Refuge
after completing
A Witch's Bargain
.
Garradia says that ever since the Ugdenbog Fetish was stolen, the coven wards and protective spells have begun to fail. To restore the wards they require new materials.
Objectives
Gather Venomgaze Bile
Gather Leafmane Alpha Horn
Gather Ugdenbloom
Bring the materials to Garradia at the Coven's Refuge
Guide
The
Venomgaze Bile
quest item drops from Basilisks, The
Leafmane Alpha Horn
from Leafmane Alphas, and
Ugdenbloom
from Swamp Golems. All can be obtained easily in
Ugdenbog
. Return them to Garradia for the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
13000
27000
58000
Iron Bits
8000
16000
30000
Coven of Ugdenbog
Reputation
+250
Garradia will then offer the
Pruning The Weeds
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Garradia has asked you to gather some materials to prepare for the Coven's new protective ritual. She requires Venomgaze Bile from Venomgaze Basilisks, a Horn from a Leafmane Alpha, and an Ugdenbloom found growing around the bog or from the Ugdenbog Golems.
When you have all three, bring them to Garradia at the Coven's Refuge in Ugdenbog in exchange for iron bits.
Objectives:
Gather Venomgaze Bile
Gather Leafmane Alpha Horn
Gather Ugdenbloom
Bring the materials to Garradia at the Coven's Refuge

The Depths of Old Arkovia
Quest Info
Given by:
no-one
Location:
Old Arkovia
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
none
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Blueprint
This is an
Act 2
side
quest
obtained by finding a
Forgotten Passage
quest item. The item can be found on an Ancient Lectern either in
Old Arkovia
near the
Arkovian Undercity
entrance, or in the Undercity itself.
Objectives
Collect Forgotten Passages within the ruins of Old Arkovia (0/3)
Guide
The remaining fragments can be easily found on the many Lecterns scattered throughout the Undercity.
When you have collected 3 Forgotten Passages they combine into a
note
entitled
Last Days of Arkovia
.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
3000
15000
38000
Item
1 random Blueprint or Recipe
Item
Last Days of Arkovia
(note)
Quest Log
Quest log
You have discovered a fragment of a long-lost page of Arkovian History. If you find more pieces, perhaps you could decipher what they say. Your best chances are within the Arkovian Undercity, deep beneath the ruins of Old Arkovia.
Objectives:
Collect Forgotten Passages within the ruins of Old Arkovia (0/3)

The Eldritch Trials
Quest Info
Given by:
The Emissary
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
N/A
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
The Emissary
Unlocks:
Loyalty to the Three
Rewards:
xp, rep
The Eldritch Trials is an
Act 7
main quest, offered by
The Emissary
in the
Conclave of the Three
after completing the
The Emissary
quest.
The Emissary seeks assurance that you are indeed the one he seeks, and offers the opportunity to prove yourself by taking part in the Eldritch Trials before joining the Which God Cult.
Objectives
Speak with Kanatha to begin the Eldritch Trials
Speak to the Emissary at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
Talk to
Kanatha, Mistress of the Sentinels
in the center of the Conclave of the Three. On agreeing to face the trials, the player will face several waves of monsters from the Eldritch realm.
After defeating them, return to the Emissary to complete the quest.
Rewards
Faction Reputation is awarded to all three Witch God Cults,
Bysmiel
,
Dreeg
and
Solael
.
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2000
22000
58000
Witch Gods
Reputation
+100
The  Emissary will then offer the
Loyalty to the Three
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
The Emissary's portal has taken you to the Conclave of the Three, a gathering of the Witch God cults within the Korvan Basin.
The air hangs heavy with anticipation of cosmic events waiting to unfold. But before you can be a part of them, you must first prove yourself.
The Emissary refused to tell you any more about this place or why you are even here until you've passed the Eldritch Trials.
Go to the center of camp and speak with Kanatha to begin the test.
Objectives:
Speak with Kanatha to begin the Eldritch Trials
You survived the Eldritch Trials. The Emissary will have to tell you his secrets now.
Speak to him again at the Conclave of the Three.
Objectives:
Speak to the Emissary at the Conclave of the Three

PAGE: The Emissary (quest)

The Emissary
Quest Info
Given by:
The Emissary
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
N/A
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Act 1
questline
Unlocks:
The Eldritch Trials
Rewards:
XP
This is a small
Act 7
side
quest
which introduces the player to the
Forgotten Gods
content.
The Emissary, a representative of the Witch Gods, seeks aid in the struggle against a rising power in the distant Korvan lands.
Objectives
Follow
The Emissary
through his portal
Guide
On completion of  the
Act 1
quest line,
The Emissary
will appear in
Devil's Crossing
.
For characters previously leveled before installing Forgotten Gods, he will also appear in
Homestead
,
Fort Ikon
,
Coven's Refuge
and/or
Sewer Hideout
.
The Emissary
will invite the player to join him in the Korvan lands, and on agreement will disappear through a portal. Following him,the portal will take the player to the
Conclave of the Three
, where they can talk to
The Emissary
again to complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
400
4000
10000
Quest Log
Quest log
You have spoken with a mysterious entity who called himself the Emissary.
He was scant on details, whispering only of great powers that gather in a far off land. He claims he was sent to Erulan to recruit you specifically, but would offer no further details.
Follow the Emissary through his portal and speak with him again on the other side.
Objectives:
Follow the Emissary through his portal

The Eye of Ekur
Quest Info
Given by:
Raiken
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
Cult of Solael
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
In Service of Solael
Unlocks:
No Room for Weakness
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Item
The Eye of Ekur is an
Act 7
main
quest
, offered by
Raiken
after accepting the
In Service of Solael
quest.
An ancient temple dedicated to some long forgotten entity called Osyr lies not far to the north. It houses a relic of great power known as the Eye of Ekur. The Raiken asks that the relic be recovered and brought to him.
Objectives
Acquire the Eye of Ekur
Deliver the eye to Raiken at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
The
Eye of Ekur
is located on the second level of the
Temple of Osyr
, inside an
Ancient Sarcophagus
. The Sarcophagus is in the boss room with
Ramzul, High Priest of Osyr
. After collecting the Eye, return to Raiken.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
4000
16000
40000
Cult of Solael
Reputation
+250
Item
Random Partial Component
Raiken will then offer the
No Room for Weakness
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
You spoke with Raiken in the Solael camp. He seeks an ancient relic that may be used as a weapon in the fight against the servants of Korvaak.
Raiken believes this relic, the Eye of Ekur, is housed in a tomb beneath the Temple of Osyr but several attempts to breach the temple and retrieve it have failed. Now you must try.
Head north through the Korvan Plateau to the Temple of Osyr and recover the relic.
Objectives:
Acquire the Eye of Ekur
Deliver the eye to Raiken at the Conclave of the Three

CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/The_Feast

The Feast
Quest Info
Given by:
Scorv Egdenor
Location:
Barrowholm
Faction:
Barrowholm
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Meddling Witch
Unlocks:
Cast Off the Flesh
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Item
This is an
Act 5
side
quest
, offered by
Scorv Egdenor
in
Barrowholm
, after completing the
Meddling Witch
side quest and reaching
Respected
Faction status.
Scorv Egdenor says The eve of Ravager's return is nigh, and in order to appease him Scorv asks you to collect the hearts of three Wendigo Ancients known as Handarroth, Ollivioth and Yuvolloth.
Objectives
Collect Handarroth's Heart (0/1)
Collect Ollivioth's Heart (0/1)
Collect Yuvolloth's Heart (0/1)
Bring the Hearts to Scorv Egdenor in Barrowholm
Guide
Handarroth
has 5 possible spawn points in
Gloomwald
, either a small way north of the Gloomwald rift, or midway between that and Gloomwald Crossing.
Ollivioth
has 3 possible locations in
Ugdenbog
, not far south of the riftgate. Can also be found south of Barrowholm rift.
Yuvolloth
has 3 possible locations in Ugdenbog. Two of them are east from
Coven's Refuge
, on the edge of the area (location 1). To find the other spawn spot (not on the gallery below), you may go to location 1 and walk in a straight northwest line until you find him. The other is south of the Ugdenbog riftgate (location 2).
Handarroth's Locations
Ollivioth's Location 1
Ollivioth's Location 2 & 3
Yuvolloth's Location 1
Yuvolloth's location 2
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
24000
42000
82000
Item
Random Blueprint
Item
Tonic of Reshaping
Barrowholm
Reputation
+1000
Scorv Egdenor
will then offer the
Cast off the Flesh
side quest, after reaching
Honored
Faction status.
Quest Log
Quest log
Ravager will soon be here and it will hunger for the hearts of the living. But not just any hearts will do for the spirit's first meal.
You have been instructed by Scorv to set out into Ugdenbog and Gloomwald and slay three Wendigo Ancients known as Handarroth, Ollivioth and Yuvoloth. These creatures have long ago outlived their purpose and must now perform one final duty for Ravager: act as a catalyst for his glorious entry into Cairn. The Great Wendigo Spirit has called to them and drawn them out of hiding so that you can perform the necessary rites.
Once you have collected the hearts of the three ancients, bring them to Scorv Egdenor at Barrowholm.
Objectives:
Collect Handarroth's Heart (0/1)
Collect Ollivioth's Heart (0/1)
Collect Yuvoloth's Heart (0/1)
Bring the Hearts to Scorv Egdenor in Barrowholm

The Final Seal
Quest Info
Given by:
Matron Malostria
Location:
Coven's Refuge
Faction:
Coven of Ugdenbog
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Honored Faction Status
Power in the Circles
Unlocks:
-
Rewards:
XP, Reputation, Item
This is an
Act 5
side
quest
, offered by
Matron Malostria
in
Coven's Refuge
after completing
Power in the Circles
and gaining
Honored
Faction Status.
Everything is in place to perform the ritual which will reactivate the  Coven's wards and seal off the refuge from malevolent forces. Matron Malostria asks you to protect her while she casts the spell.
Objectives
Activate the Fetish to Begin the Ritual
Assist in the Coven's Warding Ritual
Speak to Matron Malostria at the Coven's Refuge
Guide
Activate the Ward in the center of the circle to begin the ritual. Several waves of Ugdenbog monsters will appear to disrupt the ritual, culmination in the appearance of the
Stone Basilisk
boss. When the waves are defeated and the ritual is complete, talk to Madam Malostria.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
34000
56000
101000
Item
Random Epic Accessory
Random Legendary Accessory
Coven of Ugdenbog
Reputation
+2000
Quest Log
Quest log
You have made the preparations, you have gathered the materials. The time has come to perform Matron Malostria's ritual and reactivate the coven's wards protecting the refuge.
As the matron will be vulnerable during the ritual, she has entrusted you in keeping her safe. Make sure that nothing interrupts her work, no matter how strange.
Objectives:
Activate the Fetish to Begin the Ritual
Assist in the Coven's Warding Ritual
The ritual was a success and the Coven's wards are now active across Ugdenbog. Speak to Matron Malostria at the Coven's Refuge of the success.
Objectives:
Speak to Matron Malostria at the Coven's Refuge

The Forgotten God
Quest Info
Given by:
Uroboruuk

Path of Ascension

Main Quest

Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Items
The Forgotten God is the concluding main quest in
Act 7
, granted by
Uroboruuk
after completing
Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
.
Objectives
Gain access to the Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
Obtain the Sigil of the Three
Use the Sigil of the Three to open the Eldritch Gate
Enter the Eldritch Realm
Banish Korvaak, the Eldritch Sun
Return to the Conclave of the Three
Guide
...
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
25000
55000
102000
Reputation
+1000 (Cult of Bysmiel)
+1000 (Cult of Dreegl)
+1000 (Cult of Solael)
Item
Random Epic Weapon
Random Legendary Weapon
Item
Celestial Lotus
Quest Log
Quest log
With his dying words, Uroboruuk has lifted the veil protecting the Tomb of the Eldritch Sun. You must enter it and deal with the forgotten god.
Objectives:
Gain access to the Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
You have entered the tomb, but your task is far from finished. You must traverse its dangers and find the inner sanctum capable of breaching the veil itself.
Use the Sigil bestowed upon you by the Witch Gods to open the way to Korvaak's hiding place. Enter the rift and bring an end to the primordial god.
Objectives:
Obtain the Sigil of the Three
Use the Sigil of the Three to open the Eldritch Gate
You found the inner chamber of the Tomb of the Eldritch Sun and opened the way to the Eldritch Realm.
Only one thing remains to be done: banish Korvaak.
Objectives:
Enter the Eldritch Realm
Banish Korvaak, the Eldritch Sun
You have done the impossible. Korvaak, the Eldritch Sun, has been banished from existence, his physical vessel destroyed.
Return to the Conclave of the Three with news of your success.
Objectives:
Return to the Conclave of the Three

The Future is Madness
Quest Info
Given by:
Kira
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
Cult of Dreeg
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
A Future Foretold
,
Honored Faction Status
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Blueprint
The Future is Madness is an
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Kira
in the
Conclave of the Three
, after completing
A Future Foretold
and reaching Honored Faction Status with the
Cult of Dreeg
.
Objectives
Acquire the Hexstone of Dreeg
Use the Hexstone to purge Inarah's defenses in the Tomb of Nephos
Speak with Inarah at the Tomb of Nephos
Eliminate Inarah, the Afflicted
Return to Kira at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
The
Hexstone of Dreeg
quest item is given by Kira on acceptance of the quest. The entrance to the
Tomb of Nephos
is a short way south of the
Korvan City Rift
. in the middle of the tomb lies a glowing green gate locked by a
Sorcerous Barrier
, which is opened by the Hexstone. in  a room beyond,
Inarah, the Afflicted
can be found, who will attack the player after speaking with her. Kill her then return to Kira.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
13000
30000
65000
Cult of Dreeg
Reputation
+500
Item
Blueprint:
Emblem of Dreeg's Vector
Blueprint:
Glyph of Dreeg's Vector
Blueprint:
Rune of Dreeg's Vector
Quest Log
Quest log
One of the honored seers of Dreeg had succumbed to the Mind Reaper you defeated and now serves as its vessel.
Inarah was last seen headed to the Tomb of Nephos, within the Valley of the Chosen, in the Infernal Wastes. What the Mind Reaper seeks there is unknown, but it cannot be allowed to pass.
Track down Inarah and do whatever is necessary. You have been issued a Hexstone of Dreeg to dispel any defenses she may have erected to thwart pursuers.
Objectives:
Acquire the Hexstone of Dreeg
Use the Hexstone to purge Inarah's defenses in the Tomb of Nephos
You have dispelled Inarah's magic within the Tomb of Nephos in the Valley of the Chosen.
Seek her out and speak to her in the depths of the tomb.
Objectives:
Speak with Inarah at the Tomb of Nephos
Inarah is beyond help. The Mind Reaper has complete control over her.
You must slay her in her hideout within the Tomb of Nephos, in the Valley of the Chosen.
Objectives:
Eliminate Inarah, the Afflicted
Inarah has been eliminated. Unfortunately this is another great loss for the Dreeg Cult, but the Mind Reaper could not have been allowed to endure.
You did what had to be done.
Report back to Kira at the Conclave of the Three.
Objectives:
Return to Kira at the Conclave of the Three

This is a small
Act 5
side
quest
, granted when the player finds the
Nane's Stash
note. The note contains directions to find a
One-Shot Chest
.
Objectives
Find Nane's Secret Stash
Guide
Nane's note is found inside a small chest inside a house in
Gloomwald
; picking it up will initiate the quest. The Secret Stash is located to the north of where the note is found. A quest marker will be visible on the map as you draw near. You will need to place 1
Dynamite
at the
Detonation Site
to access a small secret area containing Nane's Stash. The quest concludes when it is opened.
Note that the Detonation Site only appears after the quest is activated.
Note and Stash locations

Elite
Ultimate

The Gloomweaver
Quest Info
Given by:
Deathmark Vallar
Location:
Pine Barrens
Faction:
The Black Legion
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Pride of the Jagged Waste
Unlocks:
The Groble Tyrant
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep
This is an
Act 3
quest offered by
Deathmark Vallar
after completing
Pride of the Jagged Waste
.
You are asked to slay
Ungoliax, the Gloomweaver
, a giant spider whose spawn are terrorizing the locals.
Objectives
Slay Ungoliax in the caves of the Shaded Basin (0/1)
Return to Deathmark Vallar at his camp in the Pine Barrens.
Guide
Ungoliax can be found in the
Forgotten Depths
, a cave with two marked entrances easily found while exploring the
Shaded Basin
. It can also be accessed via the one-way entrance in
Bloodbriar's Lair
. Kill the creature and return to Vallar for your reward.
Quest Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
11500
38000
70000
Iron
1650
6500
14000
Black Legion
Reputation
+100
Vallar will then offer you a third and last quest,
The Groble Tyrant
.
Quest Log
Quest log
You have proven yourself against Mogara, so Deathmark Vallar has entrusted you with the elimination of another highly dangerous pest. A great spider known as Ungoliax the Gloomweaver has her lair somewhere within the Shaded Basin, to the south of his camp in the Pine Barrens. her spawn crawl out of the darkest places of the world in order to terrorize the locals and gather food for their ravenous queen. This must end. Seek out the lair of Ungoliax and end her life.
Objectives:
Slay Ungoliax in the caves of the Shaded Basin (0/1)
You have slain Ungoliax the Gloomweaver and should report back to Deathmark Vallar at his camp in the Pine Barrens.
Objectives:
Return to Deathmark Vallar at his camp in the Pine Barrens

quest
offered by
Deathmark Vallar
after completing
The Gloomweaver
.
Objectives
Slay
Bloodfeast the Ruthless
at Tyrant's Hold (0/1)
Return to Deathmark Vallar at his camp in the Pine Barrens.
Guide
Bloodfeast can be found in the upper corner of the interior section of
Tyrant's Hold
, which lies to the east of the
Jagged Waste
. He presents a similar fight to
Gutworm, the Maneater
but is surrounded by groble packs with other dranghouls. Return to Vallar after killing Bloodfeast for your reward.
Bloodfeast also guards a
One-Shot Chest
.

XP
13000
40000
75000
Black Legion
Reputation

Quest Log
Quest log
Bloodfeast the Ruthless is a vicious dranghoul that has driven the local grobles into a frenzy. With the dranghoul rallying them under a single banner, the grobles are becoming a serious threat to the region that cannot be ignored. If you slay Bloodfeast, then the grobles should scatter and return to their tribal groups. Bloodfeast makes his home in a nearby ruined fort known as Tyrant's Hold, to the east of Deathmark Vallar's camp in the Pine Barrens.
Objectives:
Slay Bloodfeast the Ruthless at Tyrant's Hold
You have ended the reign of Bloodfeast the Ruthless and should report back to Deathmark Vallar at his camp in the Pine Barrens.
Objectives:

The Heart of Onarix
Quest Info
Given by:
Sagon, Vicar of Solael
Location:
Vanguard of the Three
Faction:
Cult of Solael
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
In Service of Solael
Unlocks:
Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Item
The Heart of Onarix is an
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Sagon
in the
Vanguard of the Three
after completing
In Service of Solael
.
Objectives
Obtain the Eye of Ekur
Activate the Altar at Burning Spire
Acquire the Heart of Onarix
Bring the heart to Sagon at the Vanguard of the Three
Guide
Sagon will give the player the
Eye of Ekur
quest item, previously handed to Raiken during the
Eye of Ekur
quest. It can be taken to the
Burning Spire
, a raised area a with an altar a short way north-east from the Vanguard of the Three.
Placing it on the Altar of Abyd will open a portal to the
Bloodied Wastes
, a Chthonic Void area. There,
Onarix, the Razorhide
can be found and slain. he will drop the
Heart of Onarix
quest item, which can then be returned to Sagon.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
6000
21000
52000
Cult of Solael
Reputation
+250
Item
Eldritch Essence
Sagon will then offer the
Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Solael requires that you endure one final task before the battle at hand.
Sagon has inscribed a rune upon the Eye of Ekur and returned it to you.
With it, you can activate the altar upon the Burning Spire in the Ruins of Abyd to the north. Sagon tells you that this will tear open a rift to the Bloodied Wastes, where an abomination named Onarix dwells.
Step inside the rift and slay this creature and return with its heart as offering to Solael.
Objectives:
Obtain the Eye of Ekur
Activate the Altar at Burning Spire
You used the Eye of Ekur atop the Burning Spire in the Ruins of Abyd. A rift has opened that will take you to the Bloodied Wastes.
Step inside and slay the abomination known as Onarix. Gather its heart and return it to Sagon at the Vanguard of the Three as offering to Solael.
Objectives:
Acquire the Heart of Onarix
Bring the heart to Sagon at the Vanguard of the Three

======================================================================
PAGE: The Hidden Path
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/The_Hidden_Path
======================================================================

The Hidden Path
Quest Info
Given by:
None
Location:
Lower Crossing
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
Act 2
Unlocks:
n/a
Rewards:
XP, Attribute Point, Skill Point
The Hidden Path is an extended side quest taking place across all four acts of Grim Dawn. Although beginning in Act 1, the player must first reach Act 2 to obtain some
Dynamite
before the quest can be unlocked.
The quest expands on the in-game lore pertaining to the three
Witch Gods
of Cairn.
Objectives
Acquire the Runestone of Dreeg
Continue down the Hidden Path
Acquire the Runestone of Solael
Acquire the Runestone of Bysmiel
Find the entrance to the Temple of the Three
Explore the Temple of the Three
Enter the Sanctum of the Witch Gods
Guide
Runestone of Dreeg
Hidden Path area
The Hidden Path is accessed by unblocking a secret area in
Lower Crossing
. Two
Dynamite
are required for the
Detonation Site
. A small hidden side-area can then be explored, at the end of which lies the
Guardian of Dreeg
boss creature. On death it will drop the
Runestone of Dreeg
and  a note,
The Hidden Path - Dreeg
. Picking up the Runestone will activate the quest. The note provides details for the next stage of the quest.
Runestone of Solael
Hidden Path Entrance
The quest continues in Act 2. In the south-west of the
Broken Hills
a second secret area can be discovered behind a stone gate. There the player will encounter the
Guardian of Solael
. On death it will drop the
Runestone of Solael
and a note,
The Hidden Path - Solael
.
Runestone of Bysmiel
Note Location
The Third stone can be found in the
Asterkarn Valley
region, in Act 4. From the Rift gate head northwest to an area with standing stones and (Normal difficulty only in base game and Ashes of Malmouth, all difficulties with Forgotten Gods) a Devotion Shrine. Close by behind a destructible crumbling wall is another note,
The Hidden Path - Desecrated
, which gives a clue for the location of the final Runestone.
Hidden Path Entrance
Backtracking through the Asterkarn Valley to the edge of the Asterkarn Road area, a third secret area can be located. Exploring this area will lead the player to a breakable wall which uncovers the entrance to a cave containing the
Guardian of Bysmiel
, who will drop the
Runestone of Bysmiel
and
The Hidden Path - Bysmiel
note. Picking up the Runestone will grant the Player a quest progress reward of  an Attribute Point.
Foundation of Corpses Entrance
This section of the Hidden Path also contains a Loose Stone which, when activated, opens a door to the
Foundation of Corpses
, an optional secret challenge area containing
Rashalga, the Mad Queen
.
Temple of the Three
Marked Stone location.
Screenshot of the Marked Stone.
Together, all three Runestones provide a clue as to the location of the
Temple of the Three
- the
East Marsh
. On entering the area and following the road to the first bridge, head south east, following the river edge, to find a large Marked Stone (which is partially concealed by trees and is at the bend where the river heads north east). The stone will open if the player has all three Runestones, revealing another small hidden area which leads to the entrance of the Temple of the Three.  There is also a shrine here on all difficulties if you have the Forgotten Gods expansion.
At the end of the Temple dungeon lies the bossroom of
The Sentinel
. Killing him will unlock the
Sanctum of the Witch Gods
, where the player can speak to
The Attendant
and complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
5000
27000
60000
1 Attribute Point
1 Skill Point
Quest Log
Quest log
You now have the Runestone of Dreeg and learned clues as to the location of Solael's shrine. Seek it out.
Objectives:
Acquire the Runestone of Solael
Continue down the Hidden Path
You now have two of the runestones and learned clues as to the location of Bysmiel's shrine. Seek it out.
Objectives:
Acquire the Runestone of Solael
Continue down the Hidden Path
The Witch Gods have left clues to the location of their hidden temple upon the three runestones. Study them and seek out the entrance.
Objectives:
Find the entrance to the Temple of the Three
You have entered the Temple of the Three. Explore its depths to learn its secrets.
Objectives:
Explore the Temple of the Three
You have survived the trials set before you by the three Witch Gods. Enter their sanctum to see what was so carefully protected.
Objectives:
Enter the Sanctum of the Witch Gods

The Inventor's Apprentice
Quest Info
Given by:
Kasparov
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:

The Inventor's Apprentice is an
Act 1
side quest offered by
Kasparov
. It is the second quest given by Kasparov.
Background
Kasparov has sent out his apprentice to collect parts for his research and has been gone far too long. He asks you to find her.
Objectives
Find Kasparov's Apprentice in the cellars beneath the
Burrwitch Estates
Portal Kasparov's Apprentice to safety
Speak to Darlet in Devil's Crossing
Guide
Darlet
can be found in the
Dank Cellar
beneath a building in the Burrwitch Estates. Head northeast from the Burrwitch Village Riftgate across the bridge, then turn to the northwest. the cellar entrance will be just outside the first house on the left. Make your way through the packs of monsters to Darlet's hiding place in the south-east corner of the Cellar. You will open a portal automatically for her when you talk to her, and she will return to Devil's Crossing. Speak to her there to complete the quest.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
600
22000
61000
Reputation
+100 (Devil's Crossing)
Darlet will now offer her services as an
Inventor
.
Gallery
Cellar Location
Quest Log
Quest log
Kasparov had sent out his apprentice, Darlet, to collect parts for his research and she has yet to return. If she is still alive, she is bound to be in one of the cellars in the Burrwitch Estates.
Kasparov feels a little responsible for her current situation and has implored you to find her.
Objectives:
Find Kasparov's Apprentice in the cellars beneath the Burrwitch Estates
You found Kasparov's Apprentice, Darlet, in a cellar underneath the Burrwitch Estates.
You should open a portal for her so she can travel back to Devil's Crossing.&
Objectives:
Portal Kasparov's Apprentice to safety
Kasparov's Apprentice should be safe back in Devil's Crossing.
Speak to her to see how she is recovering from her ordeal.
Objectives:
Speak to Darlet in Devil's Crossing

======================================================================
PAGE: The Last Will of Marthos Everbrook
CATEGORIES: Quest Items
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/The_Last_Will_of_Marthos_Everbrook
======================================================================

The Last Will of Marthos Everbrook is a
note
with several possible locations. It can be found on a corpse inside a house in either the
Infested Farms
or the
Rotting Croplands
. Finding it initiates the
Hidden Wealth
quest.
Locations
Here be written the last will and decree of the late Marthos Anthony Everbrook II.
To my daughter, dearest Lizzy, I leave the farmstead and its surrounding orchards. Let the land, which has blessed our family with harvest for generations, continue to provide for you and your children. And now to my bullheaded sons, Edric and Anthony, you have filled my remaining years with your endless bickering over whom would inherit my fortune. To you, I leave nothing but these words.
I had the farmhands bury the gold somewhere on the Everbrook lands. You now have but two options: move on with your miserable lives and start anew through backbreaking labor, just as your great grandfather did before you, or squander your youth searching for that which you do not deserve. I trust you will make the right decision.
*Along the bottom, you can barely make out some scribbled notes in a different handwriting: In the hills, up the road from Thornsbury's. Bring explosives.*

The Aetherial Fleshworks infest vast portions of the city of Malmouth, a terrifying sight considering all this was grown from living human flesh. The entrance is nearly impenetrable, but Ulgrim believes if you sabotage the vents spewing out vast amounts of heat and steam across Crown Hill, the Fleshworks will be forced to open or else risk critical failure. Once you have destroyed the vents, head for the entrance to the Aetherial stronghold on the northern end of Crown Hill.

The Caravan Driver,
Luther Graves
, will be located in one of several monster camps around the Foggy Bank.
Slith camps with cages
If you do not speak to him the quest will not continue and you will receive no reward.
When you do speak to him, he tells you his caravan was attacked by Slith and his guards all killed. They only kept him alive in order to eat later. You can then either extort money from him, or help him with good will. You then open a Riftgate for him and he teleports to Devil's Crossing.
Luther will have set up shop beside the Prison gates. Speak to him once more to complete the quest.

Guide
The isle is reached by boat. A Row Boat can be found just outside Devil's Crossing in act 1 (Lower Crossing); after crossing the bridge turn left and follow the water-line until you reach it. Clicking on the boat will teleport you to Hargate's Isle.
At the north of the island is an abandoned house with a Trap Door that leads to
Hargate's Laboratory
. The formula can be found in an Ornate Strongbox at the end of Floor 2.
On returning to Kasparov you can then choose to hand over the formula or keep it for yourself.
Keeping the Formula unlocks another sidequest in

,
Hargate's Mysteries
. Returning the Formula will unlock the

row boat location

Quest Log
Quest log
Kasparov has sent you on another of his mad scientific inquiries. This time he wishes to recover the research notes of one Oswald Hargate, an Arcanist who, nearly a century ago, created the first slith. Kasparov believes that Oswald must have used the Aether's mutative properties to perform his forbidden work. He hopes to leverage this information to counteract some of the horrible effects the Aetherial presence has had on Cairn's flora and fauna.
There is a row boat in Lower Crossing, near the bridge leading to the prison, which you can use to travel to the abandoned island where Hargate's lab is rumored to be hidden. The area will be teeming with slith, so be prepared to deal with the serpents.
Objectives:

What is it?
Underneath Fort Ikon to the north, there is a crypt dedicated to an ancient faith. Therein lies the Tomb of Archon Barthollem, a once powerful priest. The Archon was cremated upon death, his ashes stored within a sacred urn. In order to bring back Malkadarr, we must gather these ashes. They will serve as the core of his revenant body.

Quest Log
Quest log
Father Kymon has experienced a premonition. The Ashes of Empyrion, a relic sacred to the Chosen, is hidden underneath Fort Ikon to the north, in a crypt known as the Tomb of Archon Barthollem. But the Order of Death's Vigil had already laid claim to the Archon's burial chamber. The Order's necromancers have found the ashes and are using them to fuel some twisted ritual. You must stop them and reclaim the ashes for the Chosen. Let nothing stand in your way.

The Tome of Eanatum
Quest Info
Given by:
Kargon
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
N/A
Type:
Side Quest

Loyalty to the Three
Unlocks:
Transmuting

XP
The Tome of Eanatum is an
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Kargon
in the
Conclave of the Three
. This quest unlocks the
Inventor
's ability to Transmute
Item Sets
into different items of the same set.
Kargon has sent his apprentice, Canen, to retrieve a powerful magical tome, and has not come back. He suspects Canen has made off with it, and asks you to retrieve it.
Objectives
Retrieve the Tome of Eanatum
Bring the tome to Kargon at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
Canen's Corpse can be found in the
Sunbane Oasis
. The
Tome
can be looted from the body and returned to Kargon.
Tome location
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2000
22000
58000
Quest Log
Quest log
Kargon, a self-described inventor at the Conclave of the Three, has asked you to find a missing object for him.
Apparently he had sent out his understudy to retrieve a valuable tome from the Valley of the Chosen.
That was more than two days ago and the last he's heard of his student is that he was wandering somewhere in the Sunbane Oasis to the east of the Cairan Docks.
Kargon suspects the worst...that the apprentice ran off with the tome. Apprentices are like flies, but that tome is one of a kind.
Kargon has asked you to search the Sunbane Oasis for the Tome of Eanatum. Finding the apprentice is secondary.
Objectives:
Retrieve the Tome of Eanatum
Bring the tome to Kargon at the Conclave of the Three

======================================================================
PAGE: The Warden (quest)
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/The_Warden_(quest)
======================================================================

The Warden
Quest Info
Given by:
John Bourbon
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
Devil's Crossing
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Securing Burrwitch
Unlocks:
Murderers and Worse
Rewards:
XP, Rep
The Warden is the concluding
Act 1
quest offered by
Captain John Bourbon
after completing the
Securing Burrwitch
quest.
Background
John Bourbon believes that the
Aetherial
responsible for the atrocities at Burrwitch has possessed the former warden of
Devil's Crossing
,
Warden Krieg
.
According to logs found in the prison, Warden Krieg was experimenting on prisoners in a secret laboratory underneath his mansion in Burrwitch proper.
Objectives
Access The Warden's Cellar
Find The Warden's Laboratory
Slay Warden Krieg
Report back to Captain John Bourbon
Guide
Enter and make your way through
The Warden's Cellar
underneath his estate in Burrwitch, making your way to the exit into the
Underground Transit
. Explore this area and eventually you will reach The Warden's Laboratory
Riftgate
.
Continuing past the Riftgate, there is a large area to negotiate before reaching the Warden. There are several sections: the
Hidden Laboratory
,
Living Quarters
,
Inner Laboratory
,
Abandoned Storerooms
and, at the end, the
Underground Jail
. Here you will find the Warden's boss room, behind a large Cell Door. Enter the Warden's room and kill him.
Reward
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2000
22000
58000
Reputation
+1000 (Devil's Crossing)
Bourbon will then offer the
Murderers and Worse
quest and suggest you talk to
Mornay
.
Quest Log
Quest log
John Bourbon believes that the Aetherial responsible for the atrocities at Burrwitch has possessed the body of the former warden of Devil's Crossing, Warden Krieg.
According to the logs in the prison, Warden Krieg, or whatever he has become, was experimenting on prisoners in a secret laboratory underneath his mansion in Burrwitch proper.
The laboratory can be accessed via the Warden's cellar underneath his estate in Burrwitch.
Objectives:
Access the Warden's Cellar
Find the Warden's Laboratory
You have entered the bowels of the Warden's twisted facilities. These atrocities end here.
Objectives:
Slay Warden Krieg
Warden Krieg has been slain by your hand! John Bourbon and the other survivors will want to hear of this triumph.
Objectives:
Report back to Captain John Bourbon

Reputation
+100
Quade will then offer the
Disarming the Enemy
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
Quade and his group are unlike most Rovers. Rather than stand by and watch as the outlaws destroyed their lives, they instead took up arms and marched against the enemy. It was Quade's group that rescued Mornay during his last venture into .
It would be wise to speak with Quade if you are to attack the outlaws at their strongest. His camp should be near the Four Hills in Old Arkovia.
Objectives:
Speak to Quade at the Rover camp in Old Arkovia.
