The Word of Rahn
Quest Info
Given by:
Raiken
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
Cult of Solael
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
The Heart of Onarix
,
Honored Faction Status
Unlocks:
N/A
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Item
This is an
Act 7
side
quest
, offered by
Raiken
after completing
The Heart of Onarix
and reaching
Honored
Faction Status with the
Cult of Solael
.
Raiken has learned of some forgotten fragments of secret knowledge, still hidden in the Korvan City, and offers to share it. He tells of three silver statues that can be activated and the fragments recovered and deciphered.
Objectives
Collect the First Word of Rahn
Collect the Second Word of Rahn
Collect the Third Word of Rahn
Return the fragments to Raiken at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
The three Mysterious Statues can be found in the
Remnants of Korvan City
(see map below). Each statue requires a randomized riddle or question to be answered correctly in order to be activated.
Statue 1
Whom do you serve?
(Rahn)
Flat as an autumn leaf, round as a wedding ring. Has two eyes yet cannot see a thing.
(a Button)
It has no hinges, no key, not even a lid; yet inside a golden treasure is hid.
(An Egg)
It cries without voice...flutters without wings...bites yet has no teeth...mutters and yet is mouthless...
(The Wind)
Statue 2
When men sleep, it rises. A friend to thieves, it knows not the touch of the sun, yet fears not the dark.
(The Moon)
A lover scorned, and endless rage. A burning eye to mark the pain.
(Ulzuin)
It sits on no throne, bears no crown, but all must begin their journey here.
(Crossroads)
The sand flows as time ebbs. They have but one master, and even he must bend an ear.
(Azrakaa)
Statue 3
I've watched you coming, but cannot see. I bled for you yet have no blood. Eternal agony through immortality
. (Dreeg)
A lover's touch, a web of lies. Who will whisper of your demise?
(Bysmiel)
A heart so vile, the shadows squirm. A flame so dark, evil's cloaked within.
(Solael)
A drop of blood, a celestial sin, a death for every wound, yet with no end.
(Ch'thon)
On activation, each statue will drop a
Word of Rahn
quest item. Return to Raiken with all three to complete the quest and claim the reward.
Rewards
In addition to the
Rune Augments
Blueprints, completing the quest will unlock the
Map Room of Rahn
secret area, which has a hidden entrance located in the middle of the triangle formed by the three statues.
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
10000
25000
60000
Cult of Solael
Reputation
+500
Item
Blueprint:
Emblem of Rahn's Might
Blueprint:
Glyph of Rahn's Might
Blueprint:
Rune of Rahn's Might
Quest Log
Quest log
Raiken has uncovered a secret hidden in Korvan City that he believes may remain untouched.
Somewhere in the ruins of the city are three silver statues. Hidden in each statue is a fragment of an ancient tablet called The Words of Rahn.
Locate the statues, find a way to activate them and recover the fragments.
In return, Raiken has promised to decipher their secrets and share their knowledge with you.
Objectives:
Collect the First Word of Rahn
Collect the Second Word of Rahn
Collect the Third Word of Rahn
Return the fragments to Raiken at the Conclave of the Three

If you decide to help Ugdall, he will ask you to bring him a

, which has a chance to drop from

creatures. After finding one, hand it in to Ugdall.
If you decide to kill him, he will turn hostile; defeating him will complete the quest.

Quest Log
Quest log
You discovered a wraith deep within a tomb that has been overtaken by Ugdenbog's wild growth. The wraith, while able to communicate with you, seemed to be very unstable. Despite that, you offered to help it pass on peacefully beyond the veil. Ugdall believes that with enough spiritual energy, it can pierce the veil on its own. A tormented Wendigo Spirit has no place in the mortal realm, claim one from the most powerful and ancient Wendigos roaming the bog and bring it to the wraith within the Tomb of Ugdall in Ugdenbog.
Objectives:
Collect a Wendigo Spirit
Bring the Collect a Wendigo Spirit to Ugdall
You discovered a wraith deep within a tomb that has been overtaken by Ugdenbog's wild growth. The wraith, while able to communicate with you, seemed to be very unstable. You did not take any chances. It must be banished from this world by any means necessary.

Banish Ugdall

"In the darkness bound, Morgoneth forged his betrayal. In the Tomb of the Heretic, his soul knows no rest.
The way is shut, the heresy sealed. But should the Korvan faith be shaken once more by Morgoneth's folly, then steel your soul against the tendrils of night and deliver the keys to the Path of the Damned, beyond the resting place of our chosen champions.
With great sacrifice, we sealed away the night. Do not take lightly what awaits in its embrace."
The Third Seal of Moroneth is a quest item required to open the entrance to the
Path of the Damned
, and is needed in the
Paying Debts
quest in
Forgotten Gods
. It drops from
Hallanx the Forgotten
, the boss creature of the
Howling Chasm
.

Tip of the Spear
Quest Info
Given by:
Inquisitor Creed
Location:
Steelcap District
Faction:
Malmouth Resistance
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
For the People
Unlocks:
The Living Factory
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
This is an
Act 6
main
quest
, offered by
Inquisitor Creed
in the
Steelcap District
Resistance Hideout after completing
For the People
.
It is time to begin the assault on Crown Hill. Creed asks you to gather some explosives and breach the Crown Hill gates.
Objectives
Acquire Creed's Additive
Recover the Resistance Bomb
Destroy the Gate to Crown Hill
Claim the Crown Hill Riftgate
Speak with Ulgrim in Crown Hill
Guide
Creed will supply the
Creed's Additive
quest item on acceptance of the quest, and the
Resistance Bomb
is found on the bridge leading to the  Crown Hill gates, past the Steelcap District and Malmouth Harbor.  Place both items in the
Demolition Site
in front of the gates to enter Crown Hill, the Rift Gate can be acrivated. Creed will appear nearby, speak to him for the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
46000
88000
148000
Malmouth Resistance
Reputation
+500
Inquisitor Creed will then offer the final main quest,
The Living Factory
.
Quest Log
Quest log
According to resistance intel, the main Aetherial force has walled themselves off in the Crown Hill district. The only way to access it is over the causeway through its massive front gates. Before the fall of their base, the resistance made a failed attempt to demolish the gates with an improvised explosive. Inquisitor Creed wants you to lead a renewed assault on Crown Hill. Recover the Resistance Bomb and use it to destroy the gate. Creed has also given you an additive that he claims will make the explosive more potent.
Objectives:
Acquire Creed's Additive
Recover the Resistance Bomb
Destroy the Gate to Crown Hill
With the gates to Crown Hill destroyed, the resistance fighters and the Black Legion can now begin their final assault. Claim the riftgate on the far side of the gates so more troops can be moved to Crown Hill.
Objectives:
Claim the Crown Hill Riftgate
Speak with Ulgrim in Crown Hill

, offered by

Loyalty to the Three
quest.
Anorak became separated from his two brothers while looting around the Cairan Docks. They went into an old temple and have not been seen since. He asks you to look for them.
Objectives
Find Anorak's brothers
Learn Anderan's fate
Speak with Anderan's spirit
Find a way to release Anderan's spirit
Return to Anorak at the Conclave of the Three
Guide
Anorak's brother Aaral can be found, injured, in the
Cairan Docks
, outside the entrance to the
Sandblown Ruins
. and says his brother Anderan is still inside. After sending Aaral through a rift, enter the Sandblown Ruins. At the far end of the first level is a Rotting Corpse and some
Dynamite
. The Corpse belongs to Anderan, and clicking on the corpse will summon his ghost. Anderan explains he was killed by a spell from a crazed priest, and is now trapped in the ruins until the priest is dealt with.
Tirgan, the Mad Priest
is found at the end of the second level. After slaying him return to Anorak, who is now reunited with his brothers.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
2000
12000
30000
Cult of Bysmiel
Reputation
+250
Item
Random Rare Partial Component
Quest Log
Quest log
You spoke with Anorak from the Bysmiel camp. It appears he and his brothers are tomb raiders of a sort, working together to recover, or to be honest steal, ancient artifacts from the countless temples and tombs scattered across the Korvan Basin.
On their last outing, Anorak got separated from his brothers, Aaral and Anderan, and he was unable to find them before it got dark. He has not heard from either since and he's afraid to leave the camp in case they return or try to contact him.
Anorak asked you to seek them out at their last known location, near the Cairan Docks, north of the Korvan Plateau.
Objectives:
Find Anorak's brothers
You found Anorak's brother Aaral, but he was alone. It appears the two borhters had uncovered something in the Sandblown Ruins below the Cairan Docks, but something went terribly wrong.
Aaral panicked and ran back to the surface, leaving Anderan behind.
Aaral now fears the worst, but he's too much of a coward to return to the ruins.
Enter the Sandblown Ruins and search for Anderan.
Objectives:
Learn Anderan's fate
You found a body within the Sandblown Ruins beneath the Cairan Docks which you suspect is Anderan.
However, when you inspected the body, a spectral form materialized. It appears Anderan's spirit is still bound to the mortal plane.
Objectives:
Speak with Anderan's spirit
You spoke with Anderan's ghost. Apparently he had been killed by a rockslide while trying to follow Aaral out of the temple.
However, more sinister things are afoot than an unfortunate accident. Anderan is bound to the physical realm due to a ritual deep within the temple ruins. He believes some kind of necromancer is at work here.
If Anderan is to be freed, whatever is binding him here needs to be stopped. Explore deeper inside the Sandblown Ruins beneath the Cairan Docks, find the source of the spell binding Anderan and set him free.
Objectives:
Find a way to release Anderan's spirit
A mad priest was performing necromantic rituals within the ruins, but you eliminated him.
Return to Anorak and Aaral back at the Conclave of the Three and inform them of Anderan's fate.
Objectives:
Return to Anorak at the Conclave of the Three

Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
Quest Info
Given by:
Faction-specific
Location:
Vanguard of the Three
Faction:
Type:
Main Quest
Prerequisites:
Faction-specific
Unlocks:
The Forgotten God
Rewards:
XP, Rep, Skill Point
Tomb of the Eldritch Sun is an
Act 7
main quest
quest
. It is offered, in the
Vanguard of the Three
, by the leader of whichever Witch God Faction the player has aligned with:
Byscilla, Matron of Rifts
after completing
Byscilla's Plan
Draellus, Oracle of Dreeg
after completing
A Future Foretold
Sagon, Vicar of Solael
after completing
The Heart of Onarix
Objectives
Collect the Sigil of the Three
Find the Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
Defeat Dravis
Speak with Uroboruuk
Guide
The entrance to the
Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
is found at the north-eastern end of the
Remnants of Korvan City
. Outside the entrance are
Dravis
and
Uroboruuk
. Speak to Dravis to begin the fight. After defeating him, speak to Uroboruuk to complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
15000
38000
75000
Reputation
+750 (Cult of Bysmiel)
+750 (Cult of Dreegl)
+750 (Cult of Solael)
Misc
-
-
1 Skill Point
Uroboruuk will then offer the
The Forgotten God
quest. he will also leave behind the
Uroboruuk's Possessions
loot chest. which contains the
Mother's Pendant
quest item. Picking it up will activate the
A Mother's Gift
quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
The Witch God cults stand united. The preparations are complete. The time has come to march upon Korvaak's forces and eliminate the threat that has even the Witch Gods disturbed.
You are to travel north, beyond the Infernal Wastes and into the remains of Korvan City. There you must ascend the steps of the Tomb of the Eldritch Sun and make your way inside.
You have been given a Sigil crafted by the Witch Gods themselves to breach the veil itself and find the hiding place of the forgotten god.
Objectives:
Collect the Sigil of the Three
Find the Tomb of the Eldritch Sun
You have reached the tomb, but an unusual sight awaited you.
An ancient necromancer lies defeated before a twisted and broken man named Dravis. This figure seems intent on claiming the power of the tomb for himself.
You came here to vanquish a foe, not allow another to simply take it place.
Crush Dravis and proceed with your mission.
Objectives:
Defeat Dravis
You have vanquished Dravis, but the way forward is sealed.
Speak to the dying necromancer and decide what to do next.
Objectives:
Speak with Uroboruuk

Trapped and Alone
Quest Info
Given by:
Kalista
Location:
Buried Crypt
Faction:
Rovers
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
None
Unlocks:
Nothing
Rewards:
XP, Item, Rep
This is a small
Act 3
side
quest
. It begins when you talk to a young girl named Kalista who has apparently become trapped in the
Buried Crypt
and asks for your help in escaping.
This quest has two possible endings.
Objectives
Slay Ballog'Nath in the Buried Crypt
OR
Check on Kalista in the Rover Camp
Slay Ballog'Nath in the Rover Camp
Guide
Elara's Journal
, found in the nearby rover camp, provides some clues about what lies inside the Crypt. Talking to the rovers will reveal that they are uneasy about staying in the area and intend to leave it soon.
After discovering Kalista in the Crypt, the conversation with her can take two courses.
You can agree to help her out of the crypt and open a rift gate to teleport her to the Rover camp nearby. On returning to the camp to check on her, you will find that the Rovers have been slaughtered by a Ch'thonian demon,
Ballog'Nath, the Hellfire
, who was disguised as Kalista. Kill the creature to end the quest.
You can decide something is not right with Kalista and question her on it. She will give up her ruse and transform into Ballog'Nath and attack you. Kill the creature to end the quest.
Rewards
If you help Kalista:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
9000
36000
73000
Item
Blood of Ch'thon
(1)
Item
Riftstone
(Partial Component)
If you kill her in the crypt:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
9000
36000
73000
Item
Blood of Ch'thon
(1)
Rovers
Reputation
+250
Quest Log
Quest log
You called Kalista's bluff and she revealed herself to be a Chthonian spawn by the name Ballog'Nath. Slay her in the Buried Tomb.
Objectives:
Slay Ballog'Nath in the Buried Tomb
You have found a terrified young girl by the name Kalista in an old tomb. She became trapped in the tomb after the entrance collapsed. You opened a riftgate, allowing the girl to travel back to her family in a Rover camp in the southern Rotting Croplands. You should check on how she's doing.
Objectives:
Check on Kalista in the Rover Camp
The Rover camp in the Rotting Croplands has been destroyed by a Chthonian and the girl Kalista is nowhere to be found. Slay the creature responsible for this tragedy, Ballog'Nath.
Objectives:
Slay Ballog'Nath in the Rover Camp

Hiram has been injured by a rogue troll that has been rampaging in the vicinity. The troll is a danger to the Rover camp and all travelers in the area.

Quest log
Hiram of the Rovers was severely injured when a rogue troll came down from the mountains and began rampaging about Old Arkovia. With the troll so close by, Hiram is concerned for the safety of his people and implored you to put down the troll before it causes any more harm. You should be able to find Gulgoth, the Rampaging down the road from the Rover camp in Old Arkovia, likely wreaking havoc.

Vengeance
Quest Info
Given by:
Drew Larkin
Location:
Arkovian Foothills
Faction:
None
Type:
Side Quest
Prerequisites:
None
Unlocks:
A Familiar Face
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Item
This
quest
is an
Act 2
side quest. It begins when you find
Drew Larkin
in the
Arkovian Foothills
. If you agree to avenge him, he will grant the quest.
Background
You encounter Drew Larkin dying on the side of the road. He says he was travelling with his partner and a cart full of salvaged scrap. His partner jumped him in the middle of the night and stabbed him, making off with the loot and leaving him to die. Larkin asks that, should you run into a man named Isaiah, to kill him on his behalf.
Objectives
Deal with Isaiah Reddan.
Guide
Isaiah Reddan
can be found just a little further along the road. Talk to him and you will be presented with several options.
Hear him out.
Extort him.
Kill Isaiah as asked.
If you hear Isaiah out he will explain that Drew Larkin tried to rape his daughter and that he was defending her.  You can accept his word or ask for half his profits in exchange for letting him live.
If you don't kill Isaiah he will later appear in
Homestead
as a Special Goods vendor with his daughter Josephine. He will sell various rare components like
Focusing Prism
and
Blessed Steel
. The prices he offers depend on whether you extorted him; if you didn't, he buys and sells at much better prices.
If choose to kill Isaiah you will have the opportunity to fight him. Killing him will end the quest. You will later have to face Isaiah's daughter
Josephine Reddan
, who will be waiting in turn for revenge across the bridge to the
Rocky Coast
. You will have to fight her as well, and she will drop the
Reddan Memento Ring
.
Rewards
Believe Isaiah:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
1200
8000
26000
Extort:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
1200
8000
26000
Iron
1000
4000
9000
Kill Isaiah:
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
1200
8000
26000
Item
Reddan Memento Ring

PAGE: Waking to Misery
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Waking_to_Misery
======================================================================

Waking to Misery
Quest Info
Given by:
Hangman Jarvis
Captain John Bourbon
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
Devil's Crossing
Type:
Main quest
Prerequisites:
none
Unlocks:
Helping Out
Welcome to Devil's Crossing
Rewards:
XP, Iron, Rep
Waking to Misery
is the opening quest of
Act 1
. This is the first quest in the game, given by
Hangman Jarvis
or
Captain John Bourbon
depending on who the player speaks to first in
Devil's Crossing
. It is also possible to speak to neither of them, in that case, the quest skips to stage 4 as soon as
Kyzogg the Reanimator
is slain.
Background
The player character, known as "
the Taken
", is one of many humans possessed by an
Aetherial
. This particular Aetherial vessel has been captured by the people of Devil's Crossing, contained by the wards cast by their mage
Sahdina
, and sentenced to death by hanging, as all Taken are. When the
Aetherial
who had possessed the player character flees their body before the vessel dies in the noose,
Captain John Bourbon
spares the life of the protagonist, who is now back to being a human.
When the Taken regains consciousness, they find themself standing in a rune-covered magical circle surrounded by a ring of salt, near a broken noose. Hangman Jarvis, who is standing nearby, informs the protagonist of their former possession, and that
Captain Bourbon
wishes to speak to them. It is also possible to recieve the second part of the quest directly by speaking to Captain Bourbon without recieving the quest from Hangman Jarvis.
Objectives
Speak to Captain John Bourbon at Devil's Crossing.
Enter the Cave under
Burial Hill
.
Kill
Kyzogg the Reanimator
.
Return to Captain John Bourbon.
Guide
The captain is located in the courtyard of Devil's Crossing prison, a short distance from Hangman Jarvis. Talk to him, and he will explain that something is reanimating the dead with Aetherial energy and that he would like you to put a stop to it.
After talking to Bourbon, head north across the bridge and make your way through the ruins of
Lower Crossing
, following the directions given by Bourbon. Eventually the Lower Crossing
Riftgate
can be found by a fork in the road, and activated. Follow the road left and up Burial Hill to the cave entrance.
Once you have entered
The Burial Cave
, find and kill the boss creature Kyzogg the Reanimator. He is located in the south-east corner of the cave, and can summon a number of minions; these are best thinned out or separated from Kyzogg.
After killing the Reanimator, report back to the Captain to claim the reward.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
350
19000
44000
Iron
300
2000
7500
Reputation
+500 (Devil's Crossing)
After completing this quest, John Bourbon will offer you the
Helping Out
quest.
Also,
Rook the Gatekeeper
will now permit access to the prison interior and the NPCs who reside within.
Outcome
The death of
Kyzogg the Reanimator
means that the
walking dead
's relentless assault on the old prison has become much more manageable.
The Taken
has earned recognition, if not trust, among
the people
of
Devil's Crossing
, and is immediately sent by
Captain Bourbon
to
help out the settlement further
.
Quest Log
Quest log
Hangman Jarvis has informed you that Captain John Bourbon was the one responsible for sparing your life from the noose.
The Captain is down the road, near the stone bridge, and wishes to speak with you.
Objectives:
Speak to Captain John Bourbon at Devil's Crossing
Captain Bourbon explained that the survivors at Devil's Crossing are barely enduring through the relentless attacks of the Dead.
He believes they are coming from the caves beneath Burial Hill and has put it upon you to investigate, in exchange for shelter at Devil's Crossing.
Head north across the bridge and through the ruins of Lower Crossing. Once past the stream, Burial Hill will be on the left where the road forks.
Objectives:
Enter the Cave under Burial Hill
A creature in the cave underneath Burial Hill is causing the Dead to rise!
Kill it and Devil's Crossing will get a needed respite from attacks.
Objectives:
Kill Kyzogg the Reanimator
The Reanimator is slain and the Dead should be slowed, for now.
Return to Captain John Bourbon with the good news.
Objectives:
Return to Captain John Bourbon

======================================================================

We Need Food
Quest Info
Given by:
Mornay
Location:
Devil's Crossing
Faction:
Devil's Crossing
Type:
Main quest
Prerequisites:
An Old Threat
Unlocks:
Infested Fields
Rewards:
XP, Reputation
We Need Food marks the beginning of the
Act 3
main
quest
line, and is offered by
Mornay
after completing the
An Old Threat
quest.
Background
With Cronley's Gang finished, it's time to deal with the prison's dwindling food supplies. You must find out if the farmlands of Homestead can still support Devil's Crossing, or if the Grim Dawn has claimed them as it did Burrwitch.
Objectives
Speak to Barnabus in Devil's Crossing
Cross the bridge near Twin Falls to enter Homestead
(Or) Travel through Smuggler's Pass
Follow the Prospector's Trail to Homestead
Clear out the Aetherials outside Homestead
Speak to Douglass in Homestead
Guide
After receiving the quest from Mornay see Barnabus, who will supply directions to Homestead. He gives two possible routes, but the Twin Falls Bridge is irreparably damaged and the only course is to travel through
Smuggler's Pass
. From the Broken Hills travel through the
Barren Highlands
to the Pass, which will in turn bring you out into
Deadman's Gulch
.
Ulgrim can be found here with a small group of survivors; you can gain the
A Timely Arrival
and
Too Late for Rescue
side quests from them.
You will then need to travel through the
Mountain Deeps
to the
Prospector's Trail
. The road from here will take you northeast to Homestead. Clear the monsters just outside then enter and talk to Douglass to complete the quest.
Rewards
Normal
Elite
Ultimate
XP
4000
29000
60000
Devil's Crossing
Reputation
+250
Douglass will then offer you the
Infested Fields
side quest.
Quest Log
Quest log
With the Cronley and his gang dealt with, Captain Bourbon feels it is imperative to deal with the prison's dwindling food supplies. Mornay instructed you to speak to Barnabas about a potential solution to the problem.
Objectives:
Speak to Barnabas in Devil's Crossing
With the bridge connecting to the Arkovian Foothills repaired, you must now carve your way through the wilderness to rediscover a way to the once thriving farming community that supplied the Burrwitch region with its harvests.
Start by following the road out into the Arkovian Foothills, all the way through Old Arkovia. If the bridge near Twin Falls still stands, you can cross it to enter the farmlands, otherwise you may have to find another path. Barnabas mentioned an old smuggling route that ran through the Broken Hills. If you cannot traverse the bridge, you should look for Smuggler's Pass instead.
Objectives:
Cross the bridge near Twin Falls to enter Homestead
(Or) Travel through Smuggler's Pass
You have traveled through Smuggler's Pass and emerged in Deadman's Gulch. If Barnabas' memory is to be believed, there has to be a way to Homestead through here.
Objectives:
Follow the Prospector's Trail to Homestead
Clear out the Aetherials outside Homestead
Speak to Douglass in Homestead

======================================================================
PAGE: Worthy of Merit
CATEGORIES: Quests
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Worthy_of_Merit
======================================================================

Worthy of Merit
Quest Info
Given by:
Marr
Location:
Conclave of the Three
Faction:
?
Type:
Side quest
Prerequisites:
Must be on Elite or Ultimate difficulty
Unlocks:
Merit Tokens
Rewards:
?
Worthy of Merit
is a side quest in the
Forgotten Gods
expansion which is only available on Elite and Ultimate difficulties.  Once you kill Warden Kreig on either difficulty you can talk to the Emissary and go through his portal to the Forgotten Gods content.  Do his first 2 quests: the trial of strength by the Shattered Realm entrance and choosing to ally with one of the Witch God factions.  Then you can talk to Marr who's standing fairly close to the Conclave blacksmith.  He'll give you the quest and to complete it you simply buy a merit from Asgra who's standing next to him. Once you purchase it the quest will complete. Elite merits cost 70,000 iron bits, Ultimate ones are 125,000 bits.
The merits can't be used by the characters who buy them, but they can be put into the transfer stash for other characters to use so they can skip difficulties: either skip Normal with a Champions (Elite) merit or skip Normal/Elite with a Savior's (Ultimate) merit.  Using these merit tokens will grant other characters the attribute/skill points they would get from the quests that give them on the lower difficulty/ies if they haven't gotten those points yet, but not any devotion points.  They can still do those quests on lower difficulties if desired, no points will be given, but the other parts of the quest rewards will.
https://forums.crateentertainment.com/t/merit-tokens-and-how-they-work/103485

after completing

Defeat Atrin

Guide
The three recruits can be found in the central section of the Conclave of the Three, near the footbridge. After fighting them, the player can decide whether they are worthy or not, but the decision has no impact on the quest or the reward.
